Yesu loyali yekale mchanya mwa chidunda cha Mzeituni yolola kuli Ng'handa ya Nguluwi, Petili na Yakubu na Yohani na Andeleya nawamuuza kwa uviso.
Nawamlonjela, “Utulonjele mbuli azi zolawila nili? Ulajilo wachi wotulajila kota mbuli zabehi kulawila?”
Yesu nakawalonjela, milolele, mleche kuhadigwa na munhu.
Mina wenji wokuya kwa itagwa lya heni, chila yumwe yolonga heye ndo heni. Na hewo wowajiliza wanhu wenji.
Lomhulika mbuli ya ngondo na uhesi wa ngondo, mleche kisinza. Mbuli azo zolawila, ila kuduma kung'hali.
Nhanzi imwe yochitowa na iyage, undewa umwe wochitowa na undewa uyage, ahyo kowa na limachinyina na nzala. Mbuli azi ndo kota vila usungu wa mwaluko wa mamo kuponda mwana.
Ila hemwe milolele. Mina wanhu wowahilika hemwe kuli vitala na kuwatowa kuli ng'handa za kusalila. Mohilikwa kwa vilingozi na wandewa kwa chiwalo cha heni, leka mlavye ulolezi kwa hewo.
Ila lokung'hali kufika mwiso, Mbuli Inojile yodamligwa tandi kwa wanhu weng'ha.
Na hewo howowawika hemwe mmoko na kuwahilika kuli chitala, mleche kuwa na lunhwinhwi kwa gala gomlonga, mhela ula houfika, mlonje choneche chompegwa, mina ulonzi womlonga haulawa kwa hemwe, ila wolawa kwa Muhe Yelile.
Wanhu wowahilika wang'holozawo wakopoligwe, na wahaza wodita hihyo kwa wana wawo. Na wana wowabelenhuka wawapondile leka wakopoligwe.
Wowazudilani kwa chiwalo cha heni, ila munhu yula yokwimilila mbaka kuduma ndo heye yoloholigwa.
“Lomkona ‘Izudizo lilinguwifya’ likwima honhu hohawele hake. Yalingusoma yavizele vyoilinguzeleka, aho wawele Yudeya wabilimile kuchidunda.
Yawele kuli chinduwiko cha ng'handa, yaleche kidulika kwinjila mng'handa ya heye kuhola chinhu.
Yawele kumgunda yaleche kuhiluka kaye kuhola igwanda lyake.
Yowa ngondo kwa wachimai wawele na himila na walingonyeza mazuwa ago!
Mumlande Nguluwi leka mbuli azo zileche kulawila mhela wa mbeho.
Mina mhela awo kowa na kugaya kohakunalawila kulawila Nguluwi loyalumbile isi mbaka lehano, na hailawila kahi.
Wone Mkulu nahawapunguzile mazuwa ago, haduhu munhu yahawele yoloholigwa. Ila kwa chiwalo cha wahaguligwe na Nguluwi, nakapunguza mazuwa ago.
“Lelo munhu hoyowalonjela hemwe, ‘Mlole, Kilistu Mlohozi ka hano,’ ama ‘Mlole ka ahala,’ mleche kukunda.
Mina wokuya Kilistu wa udesi na waloli wa udesi. Wodita ulajilo na vinduzanduza wojeza kuwajiliza wala wahaguligwe na Nguluwi.
Ila hemwe milolele, heni nandiwalonjela mbuli yeng'ha loing'hali kulawila.
“Lelo mazuwa ago, kugaya ako hokumala, isanya lyowichigwa jiza na nyelezi halibunguzuka.
Nhondwe zolagala kulawa kilanga na mong'ho ubatilile vinhu avyo vyeng'ha wotigaswa!
Aho wanhu womona Mwana wa Munhu yokuya kuli ng'hungugu kwa ludali lwinji na ukulu.
Hamba kowalajiza wahilisi wa heye wa kilanga wawakungajize wahaguligwe na Nguluwi kulawa nzingo zeng'ha zine, kulawila kuli isi yeng'ha na kilanga kweng'ha.
“Kwa ikuyu milanguse nhelo ayi, hala nhagala lozikwaluka kubahula, mwanguvizela kota mhela wa nhonya wa habehi.
Hihyo namwe homkona mbuli azo zilawila, mvizele kota ka habehi kuya.
Ndanguwalonjelani ndikomya, mbuli azi zeng'ha zolawila kung'hali lulelo alu kubagama.
Ulanga na isi zopuluta, ila ulonzi wa heni haupuluta hebu.
“Ila, kwa mbuli ya zuwa ama saa ayo kuduhu ne yumwe yavizelele kokuya nili, ne wahilisi wa kilanga ne Mwana, ila Mhaza yaliyeng'ha ndo yavizelele.
Milolele na kikala meho, mina hamvizelele mhela awo wokuya nili.
Yowa kota munhu yalinguka hakaye na kwinula majendo kuwalechela vitumagwa wa heye ludali, chila yumwe na mijito ya heye, nakamlonjela mwamizi wa lwizi yawe meho.
Lelo mikale meho, mina hamvizelele mkulu wa ng'handa kohiluka nili, hanji yowa matinazo ama nechilo ama lufuku ama mitondo.
Milolele leka hoyokuya ne hemwe kuvizela, yaleche kuwafika muwasile.
Gondilinguwalonjela hemwe, ndanguwalonjela weng'ha, mikale meho!”
Nagapona mazuwa meli ifiche mnvina ya Pasaka na Mibumunda johajiwichigwe usaso. Watambika wakulu na walangusa wa Malajizo ga Musa wali wopala nzila ya kumibata Yesu kwa chinyele wamkopole.
Ila nawalonga, “Tuleche kumibata mhela wa mnvina ya Pasaka, wanhu wotulemela.”
Yesu nayali Betaniya hakaye ha Simoni nayawele na uswema. Naloyali mchisaga yolya chilyo, mdala yumwe yawele na libuli lya alabasta lilinguguzigwa kwa sendi nyinji na mafuta galingunhunyhilila ga nado inojile ilinguguzigwa kwa sendi nyinji nakoya, nakachumula alyo libuli, nakumjidila Yesu mafuta ago kumutwi.
Wanhu wamwe nawawele aho nawazudila, nawelonjela, “Lekachoni kanguwifya mafuta aga?
Gahaguzigwe kwa sendi denali miya zidatu zilinguhega kwa mwezi umwe ng'hatu, na kupegwa wazunwa.” Nawamng'hanuchila ayo mamo.
Ila Yesu nakawalonjela, “Mumleche, lekachoni mwangumgaza? Nakanditila mbuli inojile.
Wazunwa wa hamwe na hemwe mazuwa gose, ila heni siwa na hemwe mazuwa gose.
Heye nakadita vyoyawezile, nakalujidila lukuli lwangu mafuta galingunhunyhilila kuuwika goya kutiligwa mchilaga.
Ndanguwalonjelani ndikomya, koneche muisi Mbuli Inojile hoidamligwa, chinhu chino choyaditile ayu mdala chodamligwa chiwalo cha kumkumbuchila heye.”
Hamba Yudasi Isikalioti, yumwe wa awala kumi na weli, nakaluta kwa watambika wakulu, leka yambelenhuche Yesu.
Watambika wakulu lowahuliche mbuli ayo, nawasangalala, nawalagana na heye wompa sendi. Lelo Yuda nakaluka kupala ndaze vyoyombelenhuka.
Zuwa lya mwaluko lya mnvina ya mibumunda johajiwichigwe usaso, mhela ula ing'holo lyana lya Pasaka hukopoligwa, walanguswa wa heye nawamuuza, “Kwangugana kohi tukuwichile goya ndiya ya Pasaka?”
Lelo Yesu nakawalajiza walanguswa wa heye weli yowalonjela, “Mlute kuli muji, na amo moting'hana na munhu yumwe yedwichile chiya cha mazi. Mumuwinze,
mbaka kuli ng'handa yoyokwinjila, mkamlonjele yawele na ng'handa kota, mlangusa kangulonga, chakohi chihengo cha heye choyodila ndiya ya Pasaka hamwe na walanguswa wa heye?
Na heye kowalajila chihengo chikulu chizenjigwe mchanya mwa chiyage chiwichigwe goya na kunoligwa. Mtuwichile goya mumo ndiya ya Pasaka.”
Walanguswa nawoka, nawaluta kuli muji, nawafika chila chinhu cha goya kota Yesu vyoyawalonjele. Nawawika goya ndiya ya Pasaka.
Loifichile matinazo, Yesu nakoya hamwe na walanguswa wa heye kumi na weli.
Lowawele wekale mchisaga wolya, Yesu nakalonga, “Ndanguwalonjelani ndikomya, yumwe wa hemwe yalingulya hamwe na heni kombelenhuka.”
Aho walanguswa wa heye nawaluka kisinza, nawamuuza yumweyumwe, “Ndaze, nda heni?”
Yesu nakawalonjela, “Yumwe wa hemwe kumi na weli, yalingudiliza ibumunda hamwe na heni mchisaye.
Ndangukomya Mwana wa Munhu kobagama kota Maandiko Matakatifu vyogalingulonga mbuli ya heye, ila mane yuye munhu ayo yalingumbelenhuka Mwana wa Munhu. Nayahawele goya munhu ayo wone nahapondigwe.”
Nalowali wolya, Yesu nakahola ibumunda, nakota malumbo, nakaumogola, kawapa walanguswa wa heye yolonga, “Mhole, alu ndo lukuli lwangu.”
Hamba kahola chizombe, nakalonga malumbo kwa Nguluwi, nakawapa, weng'ha nawanwa mli chizombe acho.
Yesu nakawalonjela, “Ayi ndo danda ya heni ilingulajila ilagano lya Nguluwi, danda ilingubohoka kwa chiwalo cha wanhu wenji.
Ndanguwalonjela ndikomya, siwila kunwa divai kahi na hemwe, mbaka zuwa honwa divai inji kuli undewa wa Nguluwi.”
Lowasindile kwimba lwimbo, nawoka, nawaluta kuli chidunda cha Mizeituni.
Yesu nakawalonjela walanguswa wa heye, “Hemwe mweng'ha mobilima mondeka ndiliyeka, mina Maandiko Matakatifu gangulonga, “ ‘Ndomtowa mdimi, na ming'holo jeng'ha josambaluka.’
Ila londizilipuka, ndowalongola Galilaya.”
Petili nakamlonjela, “Wone hewo weng'ha wawe na majesa na hegwe na kukuleka, heni sikuleka hebu!”
Yesu nakamlonjela Petili, “Ndangukulonjela ndikomya, nechilo yiyino, izogolo halineka lwa keli, kombela kadatu.”
Ila Petili nakamwidichila yekangaze nakalonga, “Wone ingane kubagama hamwe na hegwe, sikubela ng'oo.” Walanguswa weng'ha nawalonga hihyo.
Lelo nawafika kuli kagunda kalinguchemigwa Getisemane. Yesu nakawalonjela walanguswa wa heye, “Mikale baha, mhela heni ndimlanda Nguluwi.”
Hamba nakawahola Petili na Yakubu na Yohani, nakaluka kuwa na masinzo na kugaya.
Nakawalonjela, “Ndina masinzo lukami mnhumbula behi na kubagama. Mikale hano na muwe meho.”
Nakaluta hamwando, naketoza hasi, nakalanda kwa Nguluwi, wone ilinguganigwa, yaleche kukolela saa ayo ya kugazigwa.
Nakalonga, “Mhaza wa heni, hegwe kuna ludali lwa vinhu vyeng'ha. Umbusile achi chizombe, ila ileche kuwa kota vyondilingugana heni, leka kota vyougana hegwe.”
Hamba nakahiluka kwa walanguswa wala wadatu, nakawafika wawasile. Lelo nakamuuza Petili, “Simoni, lekachoni nakuwasa? Nakulemwela kikala meho ne saa imwe?”
Hamba nakawalonjela, “Mikale meho na kulanda leka mleche kwinjila kuli kujezigwa. Muhe wa munhu wangugana kudita ganojile, ila lukuli lwa ng'hochele.”
Nakaluta kahi kumlanda Nguluwi yohiluchila ulonzi wuwula.
Hamba nakahiluka kahi kwa walanguswa, nakawafika wawasile. Meho gawo nagali gebatigwe na usinjizi. Nahawalizelele lya kumwidichila.
Loyoyile lwa kadatu nakawalonjela, “Mng'hali muwasile na kwesela? Lelo ihega! Saa ifika. Mwana wa Munhu kanguwichigwa mmoko mwa wanhu wawele na gehile.
Mlilimche, tucheni. Mlole, yula munhu yalingumbelenhuka ka habehi.”
Yesu naloyawele yang'hali yolonga, Yudasi yumwe wa wala kumi na weli, nakafika hamwe na chilundo cha wanhu wawele na mipanga na nyimbati. Wanhu awo nawalajizwe na watambika wakulu, na walangusa wa Malajizo ga Musa na wasekulu.
Yuda yambelenhuche nakawapa ulajilo, “Yula munhu yondimnonela ndo heye, mibateni na kumuhilika hali wamizi.”
Yuda loyafichile du, nakamlutila Yesu nakumlonjela, “Mlangusa!” Hamba kamnonela.
Lelo awo wanhu nawamibata Yesu, nawamuwika mmoko.
Yumwe wa wala wawele wemile aho hamwe na Yesu, nakasomola ipanga, nakamtowa nalyo chitumagwa wa mtambika mkulu, nakamdumula ikutu.
Yesu nakawalonjela, “Ndaze, muya na mipanga na nyimbati kota heni nda mbokaji?
Chila zuwa nandali hamwe na hemwe ndilangusa kuli Ng'handa ya Nguluwi, lekachoni hamundibate? Ila sambi igana Maandiko Matakatifu genele.”
Aho walanguswa weng'ha nawamleka, nawabilima.
Nakwali na msongolo yumwe nayawele yomuwinza Yesu yawele, msongolo ayo nayali yavalile igolole. Nawo nawajeza kumibata.
Ila heye nakasulupuka, nakauleka lila igolole, nakubilima kuno yawele mwazi.
Lelo nawamhilika Yesu kwa mtambika mkulu kuwele na watambika wakulu weng'ha na wasekulu na walangusa wa Malajizo ga Musa nakowali woting'hana.
Petili nakamuwinza Yesu kwa kutali, nakenjila mgati mwa lugagala lwa mtambika mkulu, nakekala hamwe na wamizi yokota chiwambilo.
Watambika wakulu na chitala cheng'ha nawaliwopala ulolezi wa kumtagusa Yesu leka wamkopole, ila hawauwene.
Wanhu wenji nawalavya ulolezi wa udesi kwa Yesu, ila ulolezi wa hewo hawiwhanile.
Hamba wanji nawema, na kulavya ulolezi wa udesi wolonga,
“Natumhulika munhu ayu yolonga, ‘Ndogwisanga Ng'handa ayi ya Nguluwi izenjigwe kwa moko ga wanhu, na kwa mazuwa gadatu ndoizenga yinji yohaizenjigwe kwa moko ga wanhu.’ ”
Ila, ulolezi wa hewo nahawiwhanile.
Mtambika mkulu nakema hagati hawo, nakamuuza Yesu, “Ndaze, hulingwidichila ne chinhu? Wanhu awa wangulavya ulolezi wachi kwa hegwe?”
Ila heye nakanyamalila tulu! Nahalonjile ne chinhu. Mtambika mkulu nakamuuza kahi Yesu, “Ndaze, hegwe ndo Kilistu Mlohozi yatambichizwe na Nguluwi, Mwana Nguluwi mkulu?”
Yesu nakedichila, “Ena, nda heni. Kahi, momona Mwana wa Munhu yekale kudilo kwa Nguluwi Yawele na Mong'ho, yalinguya kuli ng'hungugu kulawa kilanga.”
Aho mtambika mkulu nakadadula ivalo lyake kulajila kota nakazudila ng'hatu, na kulonga, “Twangugana ulolezi wachi kahi?
Mumhulika vyoyalingumkovula Nguluwi! Hemwe mwangona ndaze?” Weng'ha nawamula kota imgana yabagame.
Lelo wamwe wa hewo nawaluka kumtemela mite, nawamgubika kumeho na kumtowa na kumlonjela, “Tulagulile lelo, yalikohi yakutowile!” Na vitumagwa nawamhola na kumtowa mizeze.
Petili naloyawele yang'hali hasi kuli lugagala, yumwe wa vitumagwa wadala wa mtambika mkulu nakoya.
Naloyamuwene Petili yokota chiwambilo, nakamlola na kumlonjela, “Nagwe nawali hamwe na Yesu Mnasaleti.”
Ila Petili nakabela, “Mane, sigazelele goulonga!” Hamba Petili nakoka, nakaluta kunze kuluga. Aho izogolo nalika.
Yula chitumagwa naloyamuwene kahi Petili, nakaluka kahi kuwalonjela wanhu nawawele wemile aho, “Munhu ayu ka yumwe wa hewo.”
Petili nakabela kahi. Hado hela, wanhu nawawele wemile aho nawamlojela Petili, “Twangukomya hegwe kwa yumwe wa hewo, mina hegwe kwa Mgalilaya.”
Ila Petili nakaluka kipanjila na kilaha yolonga, “Heni simzelele munhu ayu yomlingulonga mbuli za heye.”
Baho du, izogolo nalika lwa keli. Lelo Petili nakakumbuchila vila Yesu navyoyamlonjele, “Izogolo halineka lwa keli, kombela kadatu.” Petili nakagwa chifunama nakalila lukami.
Vyoifichile lufuku, watambika wakulu nawawika chitala na wasekulu na walangusa wa Malajizo ga Musa, nawamkowela Yesu wamhilichila Pilato.
Pilato nakamuuza Yesu yolonga, “Hegwe kwa mndewa wa Wayahudi?” Yesu nakedichila, nakalonga, “Ena, hegwe nakulonga.”
Watambika wakulu nawamvilizila Yesu mbuli nyinji.
Pilato nakamuuza kahi Yesu lwa keli, “Hambe ulonje chinhu? Ulole vyowokulonjeleza menji.”
Ila Yesu halonjile ne luzi, mbaka Pilato kabubuwala.
Chila mhela wa mnvina ya Pasaka, Pilato nakamchumulilaga munhu yumwe yawele mchinweng'ho yaganigwe na wanhu.
Lelo nakwali na munhu yawele yochemigwa Balaba, nayali yawichigwe mchinweng'ho hamwe na wanhu wanji kwa chiwalo cha kukopola.
Wanhu wenji nawamlutila Pilato womlanda yawaditile kota navyoyali yoditaga.
Pilato nakawauza yolonga, “Mwangugana ndimchumulile mndewa wa hemwe wa Wayahudi?”
Nakalonga ahyo kwa vila nakavizela kota watambika wakulu, nawamigala Yesu kwa heye kwa kumonela fihi hela.
Ila watambika wakulu nawawasonjeleza wanhu wamlande Pilato yawachumulile Balaba.
Pilato nakedichila kwa kuuza yolonga, “Ndimchumulile ayu mlingumchema mndewa wa Wayahudi?”
Wanhu weng'ha nawatowa iyowe kahi wolonga, “Mumuwambe ayo mumsalaba.”
Ila Pilato nakawauza, “Lekachoni? Nakadita choni chihile?” Ila hewo nawalutilila kutowa iyowe, “Muwambeni mumsalaba!”
Pilato nakagana kulinojeza alila likugusi lya wanhu, nakamchumulila Balaba kulawa mchinweng'ho. Nakalajiza Yesu yazapigwe ng'hobwa, hamba nakamlavya yawambigwe mumsalaba.
Hamba wamizi nawamhilika Yesu kuli chitala, mng'handa ya mkulu wa Loma, nawakungajiza chilundo cheng'ha cha wamizi.
Nawamvaliza ikanzu lya chiundewa liwele na lanji ya zambalau, nawatowa ng'hata ya miwa ifandile kota chipembelo, nawamuwichila kumutwi.
Nawaluka kumlamsa wata, “Ulamche Mndewa wa Wayahudi!”
Nawamtowa na idenje kumutwi, nawamtemela mite, nawamfugamila na kumwinamila.
Lowasindile kumbeza, nawamvula lila ikanzu, nawamvalisa nguwo ya heye wamhilika kuza kumuwamba mumsalaba.
Nalowali mnzila, nawating'hana na munhu yumwe yalinguchemigwa Simoni, mwenyeng'haye wa Kilene. Heye nayali mhaza wa Alekizanda na Lufo, mhela awo nayali yolawa kumgunda kuza kuli muji. Lelo nawamlonjela yapiche msalaba wa Yesu kwa lupichi.
Hamba nawamhilika Yesu mbaka honhu hawele hochemigwa Goligota, hazeleche kota Izeje lya Mutwi.
Nawamha divai wahanzile na mikwandi ja kuhoza usungu, ila Yesu nakalema kunwa.
Nawamuwamba mumsalaba, nawegawila nguwo za heye kwa kuzitowela simbi leka wamhagule yalikohi yohola choni.
Nayali saa tatu mitondo howamuwambile Yesu mumsalaba.
Na nongwa ya Yesu nayandichigwa mchibao chiwichigwe mchanya mwa msalaba, “Mndewa wa Wayahudi.”
Hamwe na Yesu nawawawamba wabokaji weli, yumwe kumoso na yumwe kudilo kwa Yesu.
Aho nagenela Maandiko Matakatifu galingulonga, “Nakawichigwa hamwe na wehile.”
Wanhu nawowali wokola honhu aho, nawali wotigasa mitwi jawo na kulonga, “Nawali ulonga koigwisa ng'handa ya Nguluwi na kuizenga kwa mazuwa gadatu.”
Lelo uduliche mumsalaba wilohole gwegwe.
Na hewo watambika wakulu na walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa nawambeza walonga, “Heye nakawalohola wanji, ila kangulemwela kilohola yuye.
Hambi hegwe ndo Kilistu Mlohozi, Mndewa wa Isilaeli! Yeduliche kulawa mumsalaba leka tone na kukunda.” Na wanhu wala weli wawambigwe mumsalaba hamwe na heye nawamliga.
Kulawa saa sita nemisi, mbaka saa tisa matinazo, isi yeng'ha nayali na jiza.
Loifichile saa tisa matinazo, Yesu nakalila kwa lizi likulu, nakalonga, “Eloi, Eloi, lema sabakitani?” Ilinguzeleka, “Nguluwi wa heni, Nguluwi wa heni, lekachoni nakundeka?”
Wanhu wenji nawamemile ahala, lowahuliche ahyo, nawalonga, “Mhulichize. Kangumchema Eliya.”
Munhu yumwe nakahola libofyabofya, nakadilizila mli divai na chinhu chiliusungu, nakawika kuli idenje nakamha Yesu yanwe aku yolonga, “Tulole kota Eliya kokuya kukulohola.”
Yesu nakatowa iyowe na kubagama.
Lelo ipaziya liwele mli ng'handa ya Nguluwi naligawanize honhu helile ng'hatu nalidejeka hagati kulawa kuchanya mbaka hanyi.
Mkulu wa wamizi nayawele ahala, vyoyawene Yesu vyoyabagame, nakalonga, “Kakomya ayu nayali Mwana wa Nguluwi.”
Nawali baho wadala wamwe wolola kwa kutali, yumwe wa awo yali, Maliya Madelena na Salome na Maliya mamo wa Yakubu mdodo na Yose.
Awa nawamuwinza Yesu naloyawele Galilaya na kumkolela mijito, nakwali na wadala wanji wenji woyile Yelusalemu hamwe na heye!
Mhela wa matinazo nawali ufichile. Alyo nalyali zuwa lya kiwika goya, zuwa lilingulongola Zuwa lya Kwesela.
Aho nakoya Yusufu mwenyeng'haye wa Alimataya. Nayali munhu yumwe wa wanhu wakulu kuli chitala, nayali yobeteza kuya kwa Undewa wa Nguluwi. Lelo nakamlutila Pilato ne kudumba, nakalanda yapegwe lukuli lwa Yesu.
Pilato nakabubuwala heko vyoyahuliche kota Yesu kabagama. Lelo nakamchema mkulu wa wamizi, nakamuuza kota Yesu nakabagama hamuwa.
Pilato nakalonjelwa na mkulu yula wa wamizi kota Yesu nayali yabagame katali, nakamkundila Yusufu yahole lukuli lwa Yesu.
Aho Yusufu nakagula sanda iwele na utabuli uzelu, nakaudulisa hasi lukuli, nakahola sanda inojile ng'hatu na kufunjiliza lukuli na kaluta kuwika kuli chilaga chihongoligwe kuli italawe liwele kota mhalika. Nakalihejeza iganga hali lwizi.
Nawo Maliya Madelena na Maliya mayake Yose na nawahona aho honhu hoyatiligwe.
Zuwa lya Kwesela lolimalile, Maliya Madelena na Salome na Maliya mayake Yakubu, nawagula mafuta ga kunhunyhilila wakaubakalize lukuli lwa Yesu.
Lufuku zuwa lya Jumapili, nawafika kuli chilaga, isanya lyolwaluche kulawila.
Na hewo nawali wochilonjela, “Yalikohi yotuhejezela alila iganga hala hali lwizi lwa chilaga?” Nalyo nalyali ling'hangala lukami.
Nalyo nalyali ling'hangala lukami ila lowalolile, nawalyona iganga mina lihejezigwe hafungo.
Nalowenjile mchilaga, nawamona msongolo yumwe yavalile ikanzu izelu, yekale nzingo ya kudilo, nawabubuwala aku wodumba ng'hatu.
Ila ayo msongolo nakawalonjela, “Mleche kububuwala na kudumba. Mwangumpala Yesu yalawile Nasaleti yawambigwe mumsalaba. Kazilipuka, haduhu hano. Mlole honhu howamuwichile.
Lelo mlute mkawalonjele walanguswa wa heye hamwe na Petili. Nakawalongolani kula Galilaya. Ako momona kota vyoyawalonjele.”
Lelo nawalawa hala mchilaga wobilima, ena nawakakama kwa kudumba na kububuwala ng'hatu, nahawamlonjele munhu yoneche chinhu, kwa vila nawadumba lukami.
Yesu loyazilipuche kung'hali lufuku Jumapili, nakelajila tandi kwa Maliya Madelena, yula yalavigwe vijeni vihile saba.
Maliya Madelena nakaluta, nakuwalonjela wala wawele hamwe na Yesu na mhela awo nawali wolombocheza na kulila.
Ila nalowahuliche kota Yesu ka mkomu na kota Maliya Madelena nakamona, hawamkundile.
Hamba Yesu nakawalawila walanguswa weli yawele vinji. Awo walanguswa nawali woluta kumgunda.
Na hewo kahi nawaluta kuwalonjela wayawo. Na hewo kahi hawakundile.
Hamba Yesu nakawalawila awala walanguswa kumi na yumwe nalowawele wolya hamwe mchisaga. Nakawang'hanuchila lukami kwa chiwalo cha kuleka kukunda na ibamba lyawo, mina nahawawakundile wala wamuwene hala loyazilipuche.
Lelo nakawalonjela, “Mlute kuli isi zeng'ha mkadamle Mbuli Inojile kwa wanhu weng'ha.
Yalingukunda na kubatizigwa koloholigwa. Yohambe yakunde kotagusigwa kwa wihe.
Na ulajilo awu, wochibanda na wula wa wala walingukunda. Kwa itagwa lyangu wolavya vijeni na wolonga kwa ulonzi unyale.
Wone webate izoka ama wone wanwe chinhu choneche chiwele na dunga, haiwadita chinhu chihile hebu. Wowawichila moko watamwa, nawo wowa wakomu.”
Mkulu Yesu loyasindile kulonga nawo, nakaholigwa kuka kilanga, nakekala nzingo ya kudilo kwa Nguluwi.
Walanguswa wa Yesu nawaluta wodamla chila honhu. Mkulu nakadita mijito hamwe nawo na kwimiza nzinzili usenga awo kwa ulajilo uwele hamwe na hewo.
Mkulu Teofili, Wanhu wenji wadita kota vila vyowadahile kwandika vinhu vila vilawile hagati hahetwe.
Nawandika vinhu vyotulonjelwe na awala waviwene avyo kwa meho ga hewo kulawa kwaluche na kudamla Mbuli Inojile.
Ahyo mkulu Teofili, lekachoni na heni ndola goya vinhu avyo vyeng'ha kulawa kwaluche, nambona hata heni ndikwandichile goya vila vilawile.
Ndangudita hino leka hegwe nagwe uvizele kukomya kweng'ha kuli vinhu vyoulanguswe.
Mihela Helodi loyali mndewa wa Yudeya, kwali na mtambika yumwe itagwa lyake Sakaliya, heye nayali mchilundo cha watambika cha Abiya. Mdala wa heye nakachemigwa Elisabeti, heye nayali wa lukolo lwa mtambika Aluni.
Weng'ha weli watanganiche hali meho ga Nguluwi, wochikala kwa kuwinza vyoyolonga na kulajiza Mkulu Nguluwi.
Nawalihela mwana, lekachoni Elisabeti nayali mhende, na weng'ha weli wali walalile lukami.
Zuwa limwe Sakaliya nayali yodita mijito ja kutambika kuli Ng'handa ya Nguluwi, lekachoni nayali nzamu ya heye ya kulavya nhambiko.
Kota vyoili chihendo cha watambika, simbi imgubuchila Sakaliya kwinjila Ng'handa ya Mkulu kufunyiza ubani.
Wanhu wenji wali wamemile kunze wolanda Nguluwi mhela awo wa kufunyiza ubani.
Hamba mhilisi wa Mkulu Nguluwi kamlawila Sakaliya, kema kudilo kwa honhu ha kulavila nhambiko ha kufunyiza ubani.
Sakaliya loyamuwene, nakatinuka vibi, yokakama aku yodumba.
Ila mhilisi wa kilanga nakamlonjela, “Sakaliya, uleche kudumba! Nguluwi kahulika kulanda kwa hegwe. Mdala wa hegwe Elisabeti kokulelela mwana mlume, hegwe kompa itagwa Yohani.
Hegwe kosangalala na kusechelela ng'hatu, na wanhu wenji wosechelela kuleligwa heye.
Kowa mng'hangala hali Mkulu. Honwa divai wala chinhu chigazaga. Komema Muhe Yelile kulawa mmunda mwa mamo wa heye.
Kowahilusa wanhu wenji wa Isilaeli wampale Mkulu, Nguluwi wa hewo.
Komlongolela Mkulu, kowa na mong'ho na ludali lwa mloli wa Nguluwi, Eliya, kowadita wahaza na wana wegane. Kowagalamla wanhu wohambe wamkunde Nguluwi wawe na majesa gatanganiche, na kuwakola wanhu wekale goya kumbochela Mkulu.”
Sakaliya nakamuuza ayo mhilisi wa kilanga, “Hino ndovizela ndaze kota mbuli ayi yakukomya? Heni ndala, na mdala wa heni kalala.”
Yula mhilisi wa kilanga nakamlonjela, “Heni Gabulieli, ndilingwima hali Nguluwi. Heye ndo yanhumile kuya kulonga na hegwe na kukulonjela mbuli ayi inojile.
Ila kwa vila hambe ukunde mbuli ayi yoilawila kwa mihela jake, kolemwela kulonga mbaka ago gondikulonjele, galawile.”
Mhela awo, wala wanhu wali wombeta Sakaliya, wabubuwala vyoyali yokawila kulawa mli Ng'handa ng'hulu ya Nguluwi.
Vyoyalawile kunze ya Ng'handa ya Nguluwi, nakalemwela kulonga nawo, ahyo nawavizela kona maono mla mng'handa ya Nguluwi. Kwa vila nayali yolemwela kulonga, ila yaliyolajila na moko.
Mhela wa heye wa kudita mijito kuli Ng'handa ng'hulu ya Nguluwi lo umalile, kahiluka kaye.
Hamba kuli mazuwa mado, mhazwa wa heye Elisabeti kawa na himila, kekala haluga mg'handa myezi jihano. Kalonga,
“Mkulu kanditila aga. Sambi kandajila isungu lya heye. Kambusila soni iwele na heni hali wanhu.”
Kuli mwezi wa sita wa himila ya Elisabeti, Nguluwi kamlajiza mhilisi wa kilanga yalinguchemigwa Gabulieli, yalute kuli muji ulinguchemigwa Nasaleti, kuli isi ya Galilaya.
Nakoya kwa mhinza yumwe yalinguchemigwa Maliya, yabanichilwe na munhu yumwe itagwa lyake Yusufu wa lukolo lwa mndewa Daudi.
Mhilisi wa kilanga nakaluta kwa heye, kamlamusa, “Kulamka! Mkulu Nguluwi kahamwe na hegwe, naheye kakutambichiza ng'hatu!”
Maliya loyahuliche luzi awo, nakesinza lukami, kaza ngijesa mnhumbula ya heye, kulamsa aku kwa ndaze?
Ila yula mhilisi wa kilanga nakamlonjela, “Maliya, uleche kudumba! Nguluwi kakugalila kunoga kwa heye.
Ahino, kowa na himila, hamba kolela mwana wa udewele mlume na komchemela itagwa Yesu.
Heye kowa mng'hangala na kochemigwa Mwana wa Nguluwi nayali kuchanya ng'hatu. Mkulu Nguluwi komdita yawe mndewa kota vyoyali sekulu wa heye Daudi.
Kowa mndewa wa lukolo lwa Yakubu kolutilila, na undewa wa heye wowa hela kuduma!”
Maliya nakamlonjela mhilisi wa kilanga, “Heni, sinating'hana na mlume. Lelo ago gowa ndaze?”
Yula mhilisi wa kilanga nakamlonjela, “Muhe Yelile kokudulichila, na mong'ho wa Nguluwi lokugubika. Kwa mbuli ayo, mwana yelile yoleligwa kochemigwa, Yelile mwana wa Nguluwi.
Ulole, Elisabeti mng'holoze heye! Wanhu nawamchemile mhende, leka sambi kana himila ya myezi sita, nakulala koyalalile.
Mina kwa Nguluwi kuduhuli mbuli iwele ngulemwelwa.”
Maliya kalonga “Heni nda chitumagwa wa Mkulu, iwe kota vyoulonjile.” Hamba yula mhilisi wa kilanga nakoka.
Logakolile mazuwa mado, Maliya nakawoha majendo kuluta himahima mbaka mji umwe, uwele mchidunda cha Yuda.
Ako nakenjila mng'handa ya Sakaliya, kamlamsa Elisabeti.
Elisabeti lowahuliche kulamusa kwa Maliya, chali chitigasika mmunda mwa heye. Elisabeti kamemezwa Muhe Yelile,
na heye kalonga kwa lizi likulu, “Kutambichizwa kusinda wadala weng'ha, na mwana youmulela kotambichizwa.
Heni nda whaani, leka mamo wa Mkulu wa heni yanjendele?
Lonyhuliche ulamso wa hegwe, chali mmunda mwa heni chitagasika kwa kusangalala.
Kutambichizwa ng'hatu hegwe kwa kukunda mbuli ya Mkulu, kwa vila yowa ikomya kwa gala Mkulu goyakulonjile hegwe!”
Maliya kalonga, “Nhumbula ya heni yangumutogola Mkulu,
na muhe wa heni wangusangalala kwa Mbuli ya Nguluwi mlohozi wa heni,
Lekachoni kang'humbuka, chitumagwa wa heye yaholile! Kulawa sambi na kulutilila, wanhu weng'ha wonyhema mtambichizwa,
kwa vinhu vikulu Nguluwi vyoyaditile. Itagwa lya Nguluwi lyela.
Kulawa ulelo awu na kulutilila, kawalajila Isungu weng'ha walingumdumba heye.
Kadita mbuli ng'hulu kwa moko wa heye. Kawasambalula wali na mnvimnvi majesa ga mnhumbula za hewo.
Kawadulisa wandewa kulawa mvigoda vya hewo vya undewa, nakawakwiniza wala waholile.
Wali na nzala kawagutiza vinhu vinojile, wali na lufufu kawaleka walute moko yeng'ha.
Kambochela Isilaeli chitumagwa wa heye, yokumbuka isungu lyake.
Kota vonawalongane na wakulu wa hetwe, Abulahamu na ulelo wa heye mazuwa gose.”
Maliya nakekala na Elisabeti myezi jidatu, hamba kahiluka kaye kwa heye.
Mhela wa Elisabeti kulela naufika, kalela mwana mlume.
Wanhu wahabehi na haluga hake nawahulika Mkulu Nguluwi kamonela isungu ng'hatu, nawasangalala hamwe na heye.
Hamba mazuwa nane nagafika ga kumwinjiza yula mwana ikumbi, wazangugana kumchemela itagwa lya mhaza wa heye, Sakaliya.
Ila mayake kalonga, “Hebu! Kochemigwa Yohani.”
Wamlonjela, “Lekachoni haduhu munhu mlukolo lwenu, yalinguchemigwa itagwa ali?”
Wamgodeza mhaza wa mwana yalonje, mwanage yapegwe itagwa lyachi.
Heye kalanda chibao cha kwandika kandika hino, Yohani ndo itagwa lyake, weng'ha wekala wabubuwale.
Bahala umyango na mlomo wa Sakaliya ugubuka kazangulonga kahi yomtogola Nguluwi.
Woga nauwenjila wanhu weng'ha wa hala habehi, na mbuli azo zenela chila honhu mchidunda cha Yudeya.
Weng'ha wahuliche mbuli ayo, nawejesa mnhumbula zawo wolonga, mwana ayu kowa ndaze? Mana loneka ludali lwa Mkulu Nguluwi lwali hamwe na heye.
Sakaliya, mhaza wa Yohani, kamemezwa Muhe Yelile, kazangulonga lizi lya Nguluwi.
Yatogolwe Mkulu Nguluwi wa Isilaeli, kawoyela na kuwagombola wanhu wa heye.
Katugalila mlohozi mkulu nayali na ludali, lukolo lwa Daudi mtumigwa wa heye.
Na katulonjela aho katali kukolela kuli waloli wa heye welile.
Hino kotulohola mmoko mwa watwihilwe hetwe, na kulawa mmoko mwa wanhu weng'ha wehile.
Kalonga kowonela isungu wakulu wa hetwe, na kukumbuchila ilagano lyelile.
Kamlahila Abulahamu sekulu wa hetwe.
Kutulohola mmoko mwa wanhu watwihilwe, tuwafugamile ne kudumba,
Tuwe welile na watanganiche hali heye, mazuwa geng'ha ga ukomu wa hetwe.
Na hegwe go mwana wa heni, kochemigwa mloli wa Mkulu Nguluwi nayali kuchanya ng'hatu, komlongola Nguluwi mwana komgongomanyila nzila,
kowatagusila wanhu kota woloholigwa, na kusilwa gehile gowaditile.
Nguluwi wa hetwe kana isungu. Kotusomolela lumuli lya ulohozi lituyila kulawa kuchanya.
Nakuwamwesela weng'ha wekale kutitu kuli kwaga, na yalongoze migulu ja hetwe mnzila ya kikala goya.
Mwana kakula na ludali mli Muhe. Nekekala kugunuche mbaka loyelajile kwa wanhu wa Isilaeli.
Zuwa lila mndewa wa Loma Agusto nakalajiza, yogana wanhu weng'ha wa isi ila wawazigwe.
Kuwazigwa ako kwali kulongole, mhela Kulenio loyali mkulu wa Siliya.
Weng'ha nawaluta kuza kuwazigwa, chila munhu kaye koyekalaga.
Yusufu nakalawa muji wa Nasaleti kuli isi ya Galilaya nakaluta muji wa Betelehemu ya mkowa wa Yudeya koyaleligwe mndewa Daudi. Yusufu nakaluta ako kwa vila nayali wa lukolo lwa Daudi.
Nakaluta kuza wazigwa hamwe na mchewake Maliya heye Maliya nayali na himila.
Lowali ako zuwa lyake lya kulela Maliya nalifika,
nakalela mwana wa mwaluko wa udewele mlume, kamvika vibende vya chiwhana na kumuwasiliza mulibani lya kulisila misenga. Kwa vila nawahusa honhu ha kuwasa kuli ng'handa za wajenzi.
Honhu aho kwali na wadimi wochikala meho hamihe wololela migongolo jowafujile kwa kibochelela.
Mhilisi wa mkulu kawalawila ne kulonga, na ukulu wa Nguluwi uwamwesela nzingo zeng'ha wadumba.
Mhilisi wa kilanga nakawalonjela, “Mleche kudumba ikugalilani Mbuli Inojile iwoyele wanhu weng'ha.
Kwa vila, lehano kuli honhu ha Daudi, kaleligwa mlohozi kwa mbuli ya hemwe yuye Kilistu mkulu mlohozi yahaguligwe na Nguluwi.
Achi chokulajilani hemwe mochifika chali chivalizigwe nguwo za chiwana yawasilizwe hali honhu ha kudila misenga.
Baho chilundo chikulu cha wahilisi wa kilanga chilongozwa na ahyo mhilisi, wazangumtogola Nguluwi wolonga.”
“Tumtogole Nguluwi wa kilanga, kikala goya muisi kuli wanhu yawaganile!”
Bahala mhilisi wa kilanga nakoka na kuhiluka kilanga, wadimaji wazangilonjela. “Tucheni mbaka Betelehemu tukalilole ali lilawile lyotulonjelwe na Mkulu.”
Waluta wobilima, wamfika Maliya na Yusufu na yula mwana yawasilizwe honhu ha kulisila misenga,
Awo wadimi lowamuwene ayo mwana wawalonjela wayao mbuli yowahuliche ya ayo mwana.
Weng'ha wahuliche ago wekala mlomo mwazi mbuli zowalonjelwe na awo wadimi.
Ila Maliya nakagawika na kijesa aga geng'ha mnhumbula ya heye.
Wala wadimi wahiluka kaye kowekalaga kuno womtogola Nguluwi kwa geng'ha gowahuliche na kugona, geng'ha gawa hihila kota vowalonjelwe.
Mazuwa nane logafichile ga kumwinjiza ikumbi ayo mwana, nakapegwa itagwa lilila lya Yesu lyonayapeligwe na mhilisi wa kilanga yang'hali hola nyinda.
Mazuwa logafichile ga Maliya na Yusufu za kuhovugwa kota voiganigwe na malajizo ga Musa, wakulu awo nawamuhola yula mwana waluta naye Yelusalemu wamuwiche kumwando kuli ng'handa ya Nguluwi.
Mli mzilo wa mkulu yandichigwa. “Chila mwana mlume yalongole kuleligwa, yalavigwe kwa Mkulu.”
Kahi nawaluta wakalavye nhambiko, ng'hunda mbili kota mzilo wa Mkulu Nguluwi vyoulingulonga.
Mihela ajo ako Yelusalemu kwali na munhu yumwe, nayali yanojile na yalingumdumba Nguluwi itagwa lyake Simoni, heye yaliyobeteza ulohozi wa Isilaeli. Muhe Yelile nayali hamwe na heye.
Muhe Yelile naimtawiza kota hobagama hebu mbaka yamone Kilistu wa Mkulu.
Yolongozwa na Muhe Yelile, Simoni nakenjila kuli luga lwa Ng'handa ya Nguluwi, wahaza wa Yesu wamgala mwana wa hewo wamditile kota vyoilinguganigwa na malajizo ga Musa,
Simoni nakambochela ayo mwana mmoko mwa heye kuno yomtogola Nguluwi yolonga,
“Lelo Nguluwi Mkulu kudita choulonjile, mkundize chitumagwa wa hegwe yalute kwa kikala goya.
Mina kwa meho gangu ndiwona ulohozi wa hegwe,
uwichile woneche na wanhu weng'ha,
alu ndo lumuli louwamwesele wanhu wa isi, na ukulu kwa wanhu wa hegwe Isilaeli.”
Mhaza wa Yesu na mayake newekala mlomo mwazi kwa ulonzi woyaliyolonga Simeoni kuli yula mwana.
Simoni kamtambichiza nakamlonjela Maliya mayake ayu mwana kahaguligwa na Nguluwi kuwifya na kigala ulohozi, kowalohola wanhu wenji wa Isilaeli. Heye kowa ulajilo wa chinhu chilemigwa na wanhu.
Majesa ga wanhu wenji gozangoneka hazelu usungu uwele ukali kota ipanga woihoma nhumbula ya hegwe.
Hali na munhu yumwe yatumigwe mdala itagwa lyake Ana mhinza wa Fanueli wa nhanzi ya Asheli. Nekekala na mlume mihela saba kulawa loyaholigwe.
Nakekala nayali hela mlume mbaka mihela ajo yawele mng'hangala wa miyaka makumi nane na gane mihela ajo jeng'ha nekekala hali Ng'handa ya Nguluwi yokwesela kulya na kulanda nemisi na nechilo,
Mihela jijo kalawa kumwando kamtogola Nguluwi na kudamla mbuli za ayo mwana kwa wanhu weng'ha awala wali wobeteza ugombozi wa Yelusalemu.
Maliya na Yusufu lowaditile geng'ha gowalonjeligwe na mzilo wa Mkulu Nguluwi, wahiluka kaye kwawo Nasaleti wilaya ya Galilaya.
Mwana kakula kawa na ludali na luhala lukami, kunoga kwa Nguluwi kwali na heye.
Chila mhela wahaza wa Yesu nawazowela kuluta Yelusalemu wone iwe mnvina ya Pasaka.
Yesu navyoyali na miyaka kumi na mili weng'ha waluta kuli mnvina vowazowele,
Mnvina loimalile nawaluka kuhiluka kaye kwawo, ila msongolo Yesu nakapona Yelusalemu ne wahaza wa heye kuvizela.
Nawavizela nayali hamwe na chilundo cha wanhu wawele ngilongoza, wajenda misi yeng'ha, hamba waluka kumpala hali wanhu yoyawazowele.
Lowawene hambe wamone nawahiluka Yelusalemu wompala.
Zuwa lya kadatu nawamfika kuli luga lwa Ng'handa ya Nguluwi hamwe na walangusa wa malajizo yowahulichiza na kuwauza mbuli.
Weng'ha wahuliche ulonzi wa heye wekala mlomo mwazi luhala loyali nalo kwa kwidichila gowali womuuza.
Wahaza wake lowamuwene wekala mlomo mwazi. Mayake kamuuza, “Gwa gomwana lekachoni kutuditila ahi? Mhaza wa hegwe na heni twali tukupala kwa isungu.”
Heye kawalonjela, “Lekachoni mnzengumala? Hamvizelele nanganigwa ndikale mng'handa ya Mhaza wa heni?”
Wahaza wa heye hawavizelele chila choyali yowalonjela.
Yesu kahiluka hamwe mbaka aho Nasaleti, kawahulika. Mayake kawika geng'ha gala mnhumbula.
Yesu kakula kwa lukuli na kwa luhala na kwakumnojeza Nguluwi na kuwanojeza wanhu kahi.
Yali miyaka ja kumi na jihano ja undewa wa Kaizali Tibeliyo na Pontio Pilato nayali yolongoza honhu ha Yudeya na Helodi nayali yolongoza honhu ha Galilaya na mng'holoze Filipo nayali yolongoza honhu ha Itulea hamwe na honhu ha Tlakoniti, hamba Lusania nayali yolongoza honhu ha Abilene kahi.
Anasi na Kayafa wali watambika wakulu. Mihela ajo lizi lya Nguluwi nalimuyila Yohani mwanage Sakaliya kuli honhu hagunuche.
Yohani nakaluta mweng'ha mla mbakane na lwanda lwa Yolodani. Kazangulangusa wanhu, mumgalamchile Nguluwi na kubatizigwa leka Nguluwi yawosele gehile.
Vyoyandichigwe mchitabu cha mloli Isaya, “Lizi lya munhu lyanguchema hagunuche, ‘Mgongomanyileni Mkulu nzila ya heye, mgolole nzila za heye ya kukola.
Hagwile howa hatiligwe, mla mwinuche mowa muselegwe, habinuche howa hagoloswe, nzila zihile zowa zigoloswe.
Na weng'ha womona Nguluwi yowalohola wanhu!’ ”
Wanhu wenji wali wokuya hala kubatizwa na Yohani na heye kazanguwalonjela, “Hemwe lulelo lwa izoka, yalikohi yowadeteleza kota moibilima ng'halazi ya Nguluwi ilihabehi kuya?
Mlajile kwa madito kota mumgalamchila Nguluwi. Mleche kwaluka sambi kota moibilima ng'halazi ya Nguluwi kwa kulonga, mhaza wa hetwe Abulahamu. Ndanguwalonjelani ng'hatu, Nguluwi kana ludali lwa kugagalula aga maganga gawe wana wa Abulahamu.
Iwago liwichigwa goya kuli mizabi ja igodi. Chila mgodi wohambe ulele mafuza ganojile, wotemangwa na kutajigwa mchiluli.”
Wala wanhu wamemile wamuuza, lelo tudite choni?
Nakawedichila, “Yawele na migwanda mili yamgawile nayali hela, hihyo nayali na ndiya yadite hiho.”
Wakongoza sendi nawo woya kubatizigwa, wamuuza, “Mlangusa tudite ndaze?”
Heye nakawalonjela, “Mleche konjeza kuhola chila chima chiwichigwe.”
Wamizi nawo wamuuza, “Hetwe natwe tudite choni? Kawedichila, mleche kuhola chinhu cha munhu kwa ludali kahi ne kumtagusa munhu kwa udesi, chikukwileni chila cho mpegwa.”
Weng'ha wali wobeteza chinhu chimwenga, waluka kiuza mnhumbula za hewo zilingumlapa Yohani. Wazanguvizela heye ndo Kilistu Mlohozi yahaguligwe na Nguluwi.
Baho Yohani kawalonjela weng'ha, “Heni ndanguwabatiza kwa mazi, ila kanguya myangu nayali na ludali kusinda heni. Sijeza kudohola ng'weso za makwamba ga heye. Heye kowa yobatiza kwa Muhe Yelile na kwa chiluli.
Heye kana luhelo lwa kuyugulila nyhadikwa, yalunde uhemba kuli ng'hano, na mibadu kojisoma kwa chiluli hambe chizime.”
Hamwe na luzi lwinji, Yohani nakawahimiliza wanhu yowadamlila Mbuli Inojile.
Ila Yohani nakamdeuza mndewa Helodi, kamuwala, nakamhola Helodiya mdala wa mng'holoze na kumdita mdala wa heye, hamba nakadita ganji menji gehile.
Kahi Helodi nakadita chinhu chinji chihile kwa kumuhindila Yohani mchinweng'ho.
Wanhu weng'ha lowabatizigwe, Yesu naye nakabatizigwa. Hoyali yomlanda Nguluwi, ulanga naugubuligwa,
Muhe Yelile imlagalila kota ng'hunda na lihulikwa lizi kulawa kilanga ilonga, “Hegwe ndo mwanangu ndikuganile, nojezwa na hegwe.”
Yesu loyaluche kukola mijito, nayali na miyaka makumi gadatu, wanhu wali wochijesa heye mwana wa Yusufu mwanage Heli.
Heli nayali mwanage Matati na Matati nayali mwanage Lawi na Lawi nayali mwanage Meleki na Meleki nayali mwanage Yanai na Yanai nayali mwanage Yusufu,
Yusufu nayali mwanage Matasia na Matasia nayali mwanage Amosi na Amosi nayali mwanage Nahumu na Nahumu nayali mwanage Hesili na Hesili nayali mwanage Nagai,
Nagai nayali mwanage Maati na Maati nayali mwanage Matasia na Matasia nayali mwanage Shemeni na Shemeni nayali mwanage Yoseki na Yoseki nayali mwanage Yuda,
Yuda nayali mwanage Yoanani na Yohanini nayali mwanage Lisa na Lisa nayali mwanage Selubabeli nayali mwanage Shatieli na Sheatieli nayali mwanage Neli,
Neli nayali mwanage Meliki na Meliki nayali mwanage Adi nayali mwanage Kosamu na Kosamu nayali mwanage Elimadamu na Elimadamu nayali mwange Eli,
Eli yula nayali mwanage Yoshuwa na Yoshuwa nayali mwanage Elieseli na Elieseli nayali mwanage Yolimu na Yolimuyali mwanage Matati na Matati nayali mwanage Lawi,
na Lawi nayali mwanage Simeoni na Simeoni nayali mwanage Yudasi na Yudasi nayali mwanage Yusufu na Yusufu nayali mwanage Yonamu na Yonamu nayali mwanage Eliakimu,
na Eliakimu nayali mwanage Melea na Melea nayali mwanage Mena, na Mena nayali mwanage matata na Matata nayali mwanage Natani na Natani nayali mwanage Daudi,
na Daudi nayali mwanage Jese na Jese nayali mwanage Obedi na Obedi nayali mwanage Boasi na Boasi nayali mwanage Salimoni na Salimoni nayali mwanage Nashoni,
na Nashoni nayali mwanage Aminadabu, na Aminadabu nayali mwanage Alini na Alini nayali mwanage Hesiloni na Hesiloni nayali mwanage Pelesi na Pelesi nayali mwanage Yudasi,
Na Yudasi nayali mwanage Yakubu na Yakubu nayali mwanage Isaka na Isaka nayali mwanage Abulahamu, na Abulahamu nayali mwanage Tela na Tela nayali mwanage Naholi,
Na Naholi nayali mwanage Selugi, na Selugi nayali mwanage Leu na Leu nayali mwanage Pelagi na Pelegi nayali mwanage Ebeli na Ebeli nayali mwanage Sala,
na Sala nayali mwanage Kainamu, na Kainamu nayali mwanage Afakisadi na Afakisadi nayali mwanage Shemu na Shemu nayali mwanage Nuhu na Noa nayali mwanage Lameki,
Na Lameki nayali mwanage Metusela na Metusela nayali mwanage Henoki na Henoki nayali mwanage Yaledi na Yaledi nayali mwanage Mahalaleli na Mahalaleli nayali mwanage Kainamu.
Na Kainamu nayali mwanage Enoshi na Enoshi nayali mwanage Seti na Seti nayali mwanage Adamu na Adamu nayali mwana wa Nguluwi.
Yesu kalawa mlwanda lwa Yolodani yamemile Muhe Yelile, na Muhe ayo kamlongoza mbaka kugunuche.
Ako nakajezigwa na Limazoga mazuwa makumi gane. Mazuwa ago geng'ha hadile chinhu choneche chila, na logamalile mazuwa ago, kaihulika nzala
Limazoga limlonjela, “Wone uwele Mwanage Nguluwi, lilonjele iganga lino ligaluke kuwa ibumunda.”
Yesu nakamwidichila, “Yandichigwa, ‘Munhu howa mkomu kwa ibumunda hela.’ ”
Hamba Limazoga limhola mbaka kuchanya ng'hatu na kamlajila undewa weng'ha uli muisi.
Nabaho Limazoga limlonjela Yesu, “Ndokupa undewa na ludali lwa vinhu vyeng'ha vino, kwa vila vinhu vyeng'ha vya heni, na ndoweza kumha yeng'ha yula yondanda.
Avi vyeng'ha vyowa vya hegwe, wone ufugamile heni.”
Yesu nakamwidichila, “Yandichigwa, ‘Umfugamile Mkulu, Nguluwi wa hegwe na umditile heye yaliyeka.’ ”
Na baho Limazoga limhola Yesu mbaka Yelusalemu limkwiniza kuli ludandalo lwa Ng'handa ya Nguluwi, limlonjela, “Kota uwele Mwana wa Nguluwi wilagaze kulawa hano mbaka hasi.
Kwa vila yandichigwa, ‘Nguluwi kowalajiza wahilisi wa kilanga wa heye wakwamilile.’
Na, ‘Hewo wokuhola mmoko mwawo, leka uleche kikwang'hwala magulu ga hegwe mmiganga.’ ”
Hamba Yesu nakamwidichila, “Yandichigwa, ‘Uleche kumjeza Mkulu Nguluwi wa hegwe.’ ”
Limazoga vyolisindile kumjeza chila nzila, hamba kamleka mbaka mhela ukundigwe.
Nabaho Yesu kahiluka Galilaya yawele yamemile mong'ho wa Muhe Yelile, mbuli za heye zenela Galilaya na kuli isi zeng'ha zilihabehi.
Na heye kazanguwalangusa wanhu mli ng'handa za kusalila, na kekala yotogoligwa na weng'ha.
Baho Yesu nakaluta Nasaleti, honhu hoyakulile, kuli Zuwa lya Kwesela, kenjila mli ng'handa ya kusalila kota chili chihendo cha heye. Kema leka yasome Maandiko Matakatifu kwa lizi.
Kabochela chitabu cha mloli wa Nguluwi wa Nguluwi Isaya. Kagubula na kusoma honhu handichigwe hino!
“Muhe wa Mkulu, kahachanya ha heni, kwa vila kanyhagula heni ndiwegalile wazunwa Mbuli Inojile, kanhuma ndiwadamlile wawele mchinweng'ho wodoholigwa, wala wohambe walole wozangulola, na kuwalohola walinguleligwa,
na kudamla mhela ufika wa Mkulu kuwalohola wanhu wa heye.”
Na baho kachigubika chila chitabu, kampa chitumagwa, kekalisa hasi. Wanhu weng'ha wekalile mli ng'handa ya kusalila wamnogolela meho.
Na heye kaluka kuwalonjela, “Maandiko Matakatifu, lehano genela mli makutu genu.”
Weng'ha wakwejigwa na heye, wekala wabubuwale na mbuli zinojile zoyaliyolonga, nawauza “Ambi! Ayu hawele mwana wa Yusufu?”
Na heye nakawalonjela, “Ndivizela mondonjela ulonzi awu, ‘Mganga, wilohole uliyeka.’ Geng'ha gotuhuliche kudita Kapanaumu, gadite hano haluga hako.”
Kalutilila ngulonga, “Ndangulonga ndikomya, Mloli hotogoligwa hakaye hake.
Ila mhulichize, ndangukomya kwali na wadala wenji walekwa kuli isi ya Isilaeli mihela ja Eliya. Mihela awo, nhonya haitowile mhela wa miyaka jidatu na nusu, ahyo kwali na nzala ng'hulu kuli isi yeng'ha.
Ahyo, Eliya hatumigwe kwa mgane yoneche Isilaeli ila kwa mdala mlekwa wa Salefati kuli isi ya Sidoni.
Kahi mhela wa Mloli Elisha kwali na wanhu wenji wawele na uswema kuli isi ya Isilaeli, haduhu munhu yoneche yaloholigwe, ila Naamani yuye mwenyenghaye wa isi ya Siliya.”
Wanhu weng'ha nawekale mli ng'handa ya kusalila lowahuliche ago, wazudila lukami.
Wema, wamlavya Yesu hanze ya haluga hawo, na kumigala hachanya mchidunda wogana wamtoze hasi.
Ila Yesu kakola bahala hagati ya howali, kaluta kaye.
Na baho Yesu kadulika mbaka Kapanaumu, wilaya ya Galilaya, Zuwa lya Kwesela kekala yowalangusa wanhu.
Wabubuwala kwa ulanguso wa heye, kwa vila nayali yolangusa kota nayali na ludali.
Mla mli ng'handa ya kusalila mwali na munhu nayali na chijeni chihile kazanguyowa.
“Kuna choni na hetwe, hegwe Yesu wa Nasaleti? Nakuya kutudumya? Tuvizela hegwe kwa whaani, hegwe kwa msenga Yelile yatumigwe na Nguluwi!”
Yesu kachideuza acho chijeni yolonga, “Nyamalile! Ulawe kuli munhu ayu! Chila chijeni lochimgwisile hanyi yula munhu chilawa chileka kumdita ne chinhu.”
Wanhu weng'ha wekala wabubuwale, wazangilonjela “Aku kulangusa kwachi? Munhu yuno kana mong'ho na ludali lwa kuving'hanuchila vijeni vihile, navyo vyangumhulika.”
Ahyo mbuli za Yesu zenela chila honhu muli isi ila.
Yesu kalawa mla mli ng'handa ya kusalila, kaluta kaye kwa Simoni, mamo yumwe, mkweye Simoni nayali yotamika lukami, nawamlanda Yesu yamuse utamwa.
Yesu koya na kema behi na mdala yula kaudeuza ula utamwa, utamwa umleka na baho mdala yula kenuka na kwaluka kuwawichila chilyo.
Isanya lolyali lizinga, weng'ha wawele na watamwa wawo nawawegala kwa heye, na heye kawawichila moko gake mchanya chila yumwe na kawosela matamwa weng'ha.
Vijeni viwalawa wanhu wenji, wazanguyowa wolonga, “Hegwe ndo Mwana wa Nguluwi!” Ila Yesu kawadeuza, kawalemeza kulonga, nawavizela kota heye nayali Kilistu Mlohozi.
Mitondo kung'hali lufuku, Yesu nakoka kaluta honhu ha uyeng'ha kulihela wanhu. Wanhu wazangumpala, na lowamuwene, wamlemeza yaleche kuka.
Ila heye nakawalonjela, “Nganigwa kudamla Mbuli Inojile ya Undewa wa Nguluwi kuli miji jiyage kahi, kwa vila achi ndo Nguluwi choyanhumile kudita.”
Ahyo kalutilila kuwadamlila wanhu kuli ng'handa za kusalila za isi ya Yudeya.
Zuwa limwe, Yesu yaliyemile hafungo mwa ilamba lya Genesaleti, wanhu wenji wali wamzungulute wochibana, wohulichiza mbuli ya Nguluwi.
Kajona mitumbwi mili hafungo mli ilamba, hewo walowa somba wali wochile, wohovuga utandawala wawo.
Yesu kenjila mli itumbwi limwe lya Simoni, nakamlonjela yauhejeze hatali chidogo kulawa hafungo mwa ilamba mbaka mmazi. Na baho kekala mumo mli itumbwi na kulangusa lung'hongola lwa wanhu.
Loyasindile kulangusa, nakamlonjela Simoni, Iigale itumbwi mbaka hagati kuli mazi menji na baho mkatoze utandawala wa hemwe mlowe somba.
Simoni nakamwidichila, “Mkulu tujeza kuvula somba hamihe yeng'ha hatupatile ne chinhu ila kwa vila hegwe kulonga ndotoza utandawala.”
Lowaditile ahyo wavula somba nyiji, mbaka utandawala wa hewo na waluka kudaduka.
Wawachema wayao wali mli itumbwi liyage woye wawatanze. Woya wamemeza somba mitumbwi jeng'ha mili na behi jahazibile.
Simoni Petili loyawene gala, kafugama hoyali Yesu kalonga, “Mkulu uche habehi na heni! Heni nda munhu ndili na gehile!”
Simoni na wayage weng'ha wabubuwala kwa vila vyowalowile somba nyinji vila.
Hihyo Yakubu na Yohani, wanage Sebedayo, wala wali walowa hamwe na Simoni. Yesu nakamlonjela Simoni, “Uleche kudumba, kulawa sambi kozanguwa mlowa wanhu.”
Ahyo, lowajigale jila mitumbwi hafungo mwa ilamba waleka geng'ha kumuwinza Yesu.
Yali hino, Yesu loyali kuli miji jimwenga ja ako, munhu yumwe nayali na uswema lukuli lweng'a kamona. Leka, munhu ayo kagwa chifunama kamlanda Yesu, “Mkulu wone ulingugana kombusila utamwa wondilingugula!”
Yesu nakagolola moko, kamdoliza na kulonga, “Ndangugana wezuligwe!” Bahala ula uswema umlawa.
Yesu nakamlonjela, “Uleche kumlonjela ne munhu. Ila ulute wikelajile kwa mtambika mkulu, ulavye nhambiko kwa kwezigwa kwa hegwe kota vyoyalajize Musa, Ahyo wanhu weng'ha walavye ulolezi kota hegwe kuwa mkomu.”
Ila Mbuli za Yesu zenela chila honhu, na wanhu wenji na woya kumhulichiza na kuwosela matamwa gawo.
Ila heye nakaluta nayali yeng'ha honhu hali haduhu wanhu, na kulanda.
Zuwa limwe Yesu nayali yolangusa. Mafalisayo na walangusa wa Malajizo ga Musa, kulawa chila chijiji cha Galilaya na Yudeya na Yelusalemu, wali wekalise baho. Ludali lwa Mkulu lwali hamwe na heye kwa kuwalohola watamwa.
Wanhu wamwe na woya, wampapile munhu yaziliche kumwe, wojeza kumwinjiza mng'handa wamuwiche kumwando kwa Yesu.
Ila nawalemwela kwinjila mng'handa kwa vila wanhu wenji wali wekale. Ahyo wamkwinhiza ayo yaziliche kuchinduwiko, nawatubula kuchinduwiko, wamdulisa ayo yaziliche mchinhanda cha heye, wamuwika hagati hali lung'hongola lwa wanhu hali Yesu.
Yesu voyawene vyowawele na makundo, nakamlonjela ayo munhu yaziliche, “Goloko kusilwa gehile ga hegwe.”
Walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa na Mafalisayo wazangiuza, “Hino ayu yalihi nayali yokovula? Haduhuli munhu yolohola gehile ila Nguluwi nayali yeng'ha!”
Yesu nakavizela majesa ga hewo, kawauza, “Lekachoni mwangijesa mnhumbula za hemwe?
Lilikohi liwele ubewe ng'hatu. Kulonga, ‘Kusilwa gehile ga hegwe,’ Ama kulonga, ‘Wime ujende?’
Ila ndangugana mvizele kota, Mwana wa Munhu kana ludali lwa kuwosela wanhu gehile ga hewo, mno muisi yeng'ha.” Baho nakamlonjela yula yaziliche, “Winuche uhole chinhanda cha hegwe, ulute kaye!”
Baho yula munhu yoyekale yaziliche kenuka kumwando kwa hewo, kedwika chinhanda cha heye na kaluta kaye, kuno yomtogola Nguluwi.
Wanhu weng'ha nawabubuwala ng'hatu! Na kudumba na kumtogola Nguluwi kuno wolonga, “Tuvyona vinduzanduza lehano.”
Hamba, Yesu kalawa kunze, kamona mkongoza kodi yumwe nayali nguchemigwa Lawi, yekalise mchituka cha kodi. Yesu nakamlonjela, “Umbinze!”
Na baho kenuka, kaleka chila chinhu, kamuwinza.
Na baho Lawi kamditila Yesu mnvina ng'hulu kaye hake. Na chilundo cha wakongoza kodi na wanhu wanji na wekala hamwe na hewo.
Ila Mafalisayo na walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa wamwe, wazangulonga wowalonjela wala walanguswa wa Yesu, walonga, “Lekachoni muwele ngulya na kunwa na wakongoza kodi na wadita gehile?”
Yesu nakawedichila, “Wanhu wawele wakomu hawalingumlapa mteleka mikwandi, ila wawele watamwa.
Suyile kuwachema wanhu wala wanojile, ila wala wawele na gehile wamgalamchile Nguluwi.”
Wanhu wanji wamlonjela Yesu, “Walanguswa wa Yohani Mbatiza wali wokwesela kulya na kulanda, na wa Mafalisayo waditaga hiho, ila walanguswa wahegwe wangulya na kunwa.”
Yesu nakawedichila, “Lelo wala walalikwe kuli mnvina ya kuhesa waganigwa kwesela kulya na mkasano nayali na mnvina nayali hamwe na hewo? Hebu!
Ila mhela wokuya hoyokusigwa mkasano nayali na mnvina hali hewo, baho wokwesela kulya.”
Yesu nakawalonjela nhelo ayi, “Haduhu munhu yalingukanha chibende chinyale na kuhoneleza kuli nguwo ya katali. Wone yadite ahyo, koiwifya ila nguwo inyale, chila chilingulawa kuli nguwo inyale hachiwana na nguwo ya katali.
Kahi kuduhu munhu yowika divai ya lehano kuli chizombe cha igozi cha katali. Kwa vila wone yadite hino, divai ya lehano yozatula jila mihako, divai yobohoka na mihako jotulika.
Divai ya lehano yowichigwa mli vizombe vya igozi vinyale.
Kuduhu munhu yalingunwa divai ya katali, na baho yogana kunwa divai ya lehano. Kwa vila kolonga ‘Divai ya katali inona lukami.’ ”
Zuwa limwe lya kwesela, Yesu na walanguswa wa heye nayali yokola mli migunda ja uhemba. Walanguswa wa heye wazangubena mibeleje ja uhemba, wazangupugusa nyhule na moko, wolya.
Mafalisayo wamwenga nawawauza, “Lekachoni mwangudita mbuli hambe ikundigwe kudita Zuwa lya Kwesela?”
Yesu nakawedichila kawalonjela, “Hamsomile vyonayaditile Daudi na wayage lowali na nzala?
Heye nakenjila ng'handa ya Nguluwi, nakahola mibumunda jilavigwe kwa Nguluwi kalya na kuwapa wayage. Malajizo hambe gakundize wanhu wanji kulya mibumunda ajo, ila wakulu wa watambika yeng'ha.”
Ahyo Yesu kuwalonjela, “Mwana wa Munhu ndo Mkulu wa Zuwa lya Kwesela.”
Zuwa linji lya Zuwa lya Kwesela, Yesu nakenjila mng'handa ya kusalila, kuwalangusa mla mng'handa mwali na munhu yumwe nayali na moko wakudilo uziliche.
Walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa na Mafalisayo wamwenga nawekala wopala chinhu cha kumlonjeleza Yesu. Ahyo wazangubeteza walole komlohola munhu kuli Zuwa lya Kwesela.
Ila Yesu nakavizela gowalingijesa, nakamlonjela yula nayali na moko uziliche, “Winuche uye wime hano.” Yula munhu kaluta kema hagati.
Baho Yesu nakamlonjela. “Ndangukuuzani hemwe, kuli Malajizo ga hetwe ikundigwa hemwe kudita choni kuli Zuwa lya Kwesela? Kudita ganojile ama kudita gehile? Kulohola ukomu wa munhu ama kwajiliza?”
Kawalola wanhu weng'ha wowekalile hala, na baho nakamlonjela yula yaziliche moko, “Ugolole moko wa hegwe.” Na heye kadita hiho na moko wa heye uwa mkomu kahi.
Ila hewo wazanguzudila ng'hatu wazangilonjela wawo chinhu chachi chihile chowomditila Yesu.
Zuwa limwe Yesu nakaluta kuchidunda kulanda, yalimeho kuko hamihe yeng'ha yomlanda Nguluwi.
Mitondo lokuchele kawachema wala walanguswa wa heye, kawahagula kumi na weli kulawa mumula mli hewo na kuwachema watumigwa.
Awo ndo Simoni yula Yesu yampele itagwa lya Petili na Andeleya mng'holoze na Yakubu na Yohani na Filipo na Batolomeo na
Matei na Tomasi na Yakubu mwana wa Alufayo na Simoni yalinguchemigwa mtowanila isi ya Isilaeli na
Yudasi mwana wa Yakubu na Yudasi Isikalioti yula hamba yamhinduche Yesu.
Yesu loyeduliche hamwe na walanguswa wa heye mchidunda, Yesu nakema honhu hawele na ibindi hamwe na chilundo cha walanguswa wa heye na lung'hongola lwa wanhu walawile nzingo zeng'ha kulawa Yudeya na Yelusalemu na kulawa kumwhani ya Tilo na Sidoni.
Weng'ha nawoya kumhulichiza Yesu na waloholigwa matamwa gawo. Vivila wanhu waliwogazigwa na chijeni chihile na woya na kuloholigwa.
Wanhu weng'ha nawagana kumdoliza Yesu, nawona mong'ho wali ulawa mgati mwa heye na weng'ha waloholigwa.
Yesu kawalola walanguswa wa heye, kalonga, “Mbweda hemwe wazunwa, kwa vila Undewa wa Nguluwi wa hemwe.
Mbweda hemwe mli na nzala sambi, kwa vila hamba mogutizwa. Mbweda hemwe muwele kulila sambi, kwa vila moza sechelela.
Mbweda hemwe wanhu wokwihilani, wokubagulani na kuwaliga, na kuwalonga hemwe mwiha kwa mbuli ya Mwana wa Munhu.
Msangalale na kuvina ago hogolawila, kwa vila chonolo chomuwichilwe kilanga chikulu. Kwa vila wasekulu wa hemwe na wawaditila waloli wa Nguluwi hiho.
Ila mane mwemwe hemwe muwele na lufufu, mina mhela wa hemwe wa kusechelela umala.
Mane mwemwe hemwe muwelengiguta sambi, mina hamba mohulika nzala! Mochona hemwe muwelenguseka sambi, mina hamba mozangulila!
Mogaya ng'hatu kota wanhu weng'ha, wone wanhu wawatogole, mina wasekulu wawo nawawaditila hiho waloli wa udesi.
“Ila ndangukulonjelani hemwe muwelengunyhulichiza, muwagane wang'honyo wa hemwe, muwadile ganojile wakwihileni.
Muwatambichize wala wawelenguwapanjilani, muwalandile kwa Nguluwi wawele nguwaditila gehile.
Munhu wone yakutowe izeze limwe mgalamlile na lya keli. Munhu wone yakusukule ikoti mlechele yahole na igwanda lyako.
Chila munhu yokulanda chinhu umhe, na munhu wone yakusukule chinhu cha hegwe uleche kumlonjela yakuhilulile.
Waditileni wanhu kota vila vyomlingugana wanhu wawaditileni hemwe.
“Na wone mzenguwagana wala walinguwagana hemwe yeng'ha, mopegwa choni? Haduhu. Kwa vila na wehile nawo wanguwagana wala walinguwagana hewo.
Kahi wone mzenguwaditila ganojile wala wali nguwaditila hemwe ganojile mopegwa choni? Wehile nawo waditaga hiho.
Na wone muwaziche wala mlingona wokuhilusilani lelo mopegwa choni? Wehile nawo wawazikaga wali na gehile wayawo wogana wahilusilwe hihila.
Hebu, ila hemwe muwagane wang'honyo wa hemwe, na muwaditile ganojile, muwaziche mleka kugana kuhilusilwa na baho chila chompegwa chowa chikulu mowa wana wa Nguluwi mkulu nayali kuchanya ng'hatu. Kwa vila heye kana isungu na wala wohambe wamtogole na wanhu wehile.
Muwe na isungu kota Nguluwi wa hemwe vyoyawele na isungu.
“Mleche kuwatagusa wanhu wanji, namwe hamtagusigwa na Nguluwi, mleche kuwatagusa kwa wihe wanhu namwe hatagusigwa kwa wihe. Muwalechele wanji kwa gowaditile namwe molechelwa.
Muwape wanji gowawele ngugana, hemwe namwe mopegwa. Mobochela chipimo chinojile chimemile, chobamandizwa na kusunyunyiza sunyunyiza mbaka kubohoka. Kwa vila chipimilo chichila chomulinguwapimila wanji na heye Nguluwi kopimila chichila.”
Na baho Yesu kawalonjela nhelo imwe, wone muhnu yohambe yalole komlongoza miyage hambe yalole? Weng'ha weli wokwinjila mli ikulubila.
Mlanguswa hambe yamsinde mlangusa, ila yalingulanguswa wone yasinde, kanguwa kota mlangusa wa heye.
“Ila kochona ndaze chibanzi chiwele miziho lya mng'holozo, ila uleka kuchona ching'hanzi chiwele miziho lya hegwe.
Koweza ndaze kumlonjela mng'holozo, ‘Mng'holozangu, Bete ndikuse chibanzi chiwele miziho lyako,’ Na kuno hambe uchone ching'hanzi chiwele miziho lya hegwe? Kwa mdesi hegwe! Tandi use chibanzi chiwele miziho lyako aho koweza kulavya ching'hanzi chiwele miziho lya mng'holozo.
“Igodi linojile halilelaga mafuza gehile, na hiho igodi lihile halilelaga mafuza ganojile.
Chila igodi lyozeleka kwa mafuza gake. Yangoneka wanhu hawabawaga masada kuli migodi jili na miwa, kahi hawabawaga ububu kulawa kuli mikwangwasale.
Munhu yanojile kangulavya ganojile, gawichigwe mnhumbula mwa heye, na munhu yehile kangulavya gehile kulawa mnhumbula ya heye, kwa vila munhu kalongaga kulawa gala gamemile mnhumbula ya heye.
“Lekachoni mwangunyhema, ‘Mkulu, Mkulu’ Na kuno hambe mdite gondilonga?
Munhu yoneche yokuya kwa heni na kunyhulichiza na kugadita.
Ayo kewhana na munhu yazenjile ng'handa, yula yabawile msisi wa heye mchanya hali italawe na kuzenga ng'handa ya heye baho, nhonya ng'hulu na itowa mazi menji na gamema, lukolola lwa mazi luitowa ila ng'handa, ilemwela kutigasika, lekachoni, naizenjigwa goya yimile.
Ila munhu yoneche yawelenguhulika aga gondilonga ila hambe yadite chinhu, ayo kewhana na munhu yazenjile ng'handa hali sangalaza, habawile msisi. Lulawa lwanda lumemile, lutowa ng'handa ila, igwa luu! Itugunika yeng'ha.”
Yesu loyalonjile gala goyaganile wanhu wahulichize, nakaluta Kapanaumu.
Ako kwali na mkulu wa wamizi mloma, nayali na chitumagwa yomgana lukami. Yula chitumagwa wa heye yaliyotamika behi ya kubagama.
Yula mkulu wa wamizi wa Loma loyahuliche mbuli za Yesu kawalonjela wakulu wamwe wayahudi wakamlonjele yoye yamusile utamwa yula mpogozi.
Lowafichile kwa Yesu, wamdedeza ng'hatu, wolonga, “Munhu ayu imgana yaditilwe mbuli ayo.
Mina heye yuye kanguwagana wanhu wa hetwe na isi ya hetwe, na ndo yatuzenjele ila ng'handa ya kusalila.”
Yesu nakaluta hamwe na hewo. Hoyali behi kwinjila kaye ha yula mkulu wa wamizi Mloma, kawalajiza wala weganaga wakamlonjele Yesu, “Mkulu siganigwe winjile mng'handa ya heni.
Ndo mina siwene ndanguganigwa mbuye kouli hegwe, ila ulonje ulonzi hela, chitumagwa wa heni kowa mkomu.
Mina, na heni nani, nda munhu mbichigwa hali ludali lwa wanji, ndanawo wamizi hasi ha heni. Ndangumlonjela yumwe, ‘Ulute!’ Na heye kanguluta, na yunji, ‘Uye!’ Na heye kanguya, na chitumagwa wa heni, ‘Udite chinhu chino,’ Na heye kangudita.”
Yesu loyahuliche ago, nakabubuwala, kamtogola yula mkulu. Hamba kawagalamchila wala wali womuwinza, kalonga, “Ndanguwalonjelani, sinamona munhu yawele na makundo kota aga, mli isi yeng'ha ya Isilaeli.”
Wala wanhu lowafichile kaye wamfika yula chitumagwa yotamika yawele mkomu.
Hamba Yesu nakaluta honhu hamwe hawele nguchemigwa Naini, na wala walanguswa na wanhu wanji, newelongoza.
Hoyali behi na lwizi lukulu lwa kwinjila hali honhu, walawila wanhu wawele wamholile msongolo yumwe yajile, mwana yaganigwe na mamo yumwe yalechelelwe. Wanhu wenji wahala wali hamwe na ayo mamo.
Mkulu loyamuwene ayo kamonela isungu, nakamlonjela, “Uleche kulila.”
Hamba kazakuchidoliza chinhanda chili na munhu yabagame, wala wali wamholile wema. Hamba kalonga, “Msongolo! Ndangukulonjela, winuche!”
Yula yajile kenuka, kekalisa, kaluka kudamla. Hamba Yesu kamhola kamgala kuli maiwake.
Wanhu weng'ha wazangudumba, wazangumtogola Nguluwi wolonga, “Mloli mkulu wa Nguluwi kalawila hotuli. Nguluwi koya kuwalohola wanhu wa heye.”
Mbuli azo zenela Yudeya kweng'ha na isi ya habehi.
Wala walanguswa wa Yohani wamlonjela mbuli zeng'ha zilonjigwe zilingumlapa Yesu. Heye Yohani nakawachema weli mwa wala walanguswa wa heye kawalonjela,
walute kwa Mkulu wamuuze, “Hegwe ndo yula yalinguya, ama tumbete munhu yunji?”
Wala weli yawalanguse lowafichile hali Yesu wamlonjela, “Yohani Mbatiza katulonjela tuye kwa hegwe tukuuze, ‘Hegwe ndo yula nayali nguya, ama tumbeteze munhu yunji?’ ”
Mhela awo, Yesu yaliyowosela matamwa wanhu wenji walingugazigwa na matamwa, wali na vijeni vihile, na wanhu wenji wohambe walole wazangulola.
Yolawa Yesu kawalonjela, “Mlute mkamlonjele Yohani gala gomgahuliche na kugona, wali wohambe walole wangulola, wali na magulu gaziliche wangujenda. Wali na uswema wangwela, wohambe wahuliche wanguhulika, wafile katali wanguzilipuka, wazunwa wangudamlilwa Mbuli Inojile.
Kabweda yula munhu yohambe yandeme heni na gala gondilingudita!”
Aho watumigwa na Yohani lowochile, Yesu kaluka kuwalonjela wanhu wenji wamemile, gala gomlapa Yohani, “Lomlutile kumlola Yohani kugunuche, na mijesa yawele munhu wachi? Hambi na mijesa kowa kota isoli litigaswa na mbeho?
Lelo namluta kulola munhu nayali ndaze? Namluta kumlola munhu yavalile goya? Hebu! Wanhu wawele nguvala goya na wali na ukomu unojile wangikala mli ng'handa za wandewa!
Lelo mndonjele hambi namluta kumlola munhu wachi? Namluta kumlola mloli wa Nguluwi? Ena! Ndanguwalonjelani hemwe, ila nammona mng'hangala kusinda Mloli wa Nguluwi.
Nguluwi kangulonga, ayu Yohani ndo yawele ngulonjigwa mli Maandiko Matakatifu, ‘Ulole heni ndangumigala msenga yakugololele nzila ya hegwe.’
Yesu kasinda kwa kulonga, ndangukulonjelani, wanhu weng'ha haduhu yawele mkulu ng'hatu kusinda Yohani Mbatiza. Ahyo, yula nayali mdodo ng'hatu kuli Undewa wa Nguluwi, ndo mkulu kusinda heye.”
Wanhu weng'ha, na wakongoza kodi lowahuliche ago, nawatogola kunoga kwa Nguluwi ahyo nawakunda kubatizigwa na Yohani.
Ila Mafalisayo na wala wavizelele goya Malajizo ga Musa, nawalema kumhulichiza Nguluwi, kwa vila nawalema kubatizigwa na Yohani.
Yesu nakalonga, “Ulelo awu ndiuwhanize na chinhu chachi? Ndo wanhu wali ndaze?
Kota wasongolo wawele wekalise kuli soko wochichema na kilonjela, ‘Tuwatowelani mluli ila hamvinile! Twimba nzimbo za chililo, ila hamlilile.’
Yohani Mbatiza nakoya kazanguwoha na hanwele ujimbi, hemwe mlonga, ‘Kana chijeni!’
Heye mwana wa munhu koya, kazangulya na kunwa, hemwe mlonga, ‘Mloleni, mlya chila chinhu ayu mgalaji, kangigana na wakongoza kodi, na wehile.’
Ila luhala lwa Nguluwi loneka lunoga kwa wala weng'ha walinguikunda.”
Mfalisayo yumwe nakamchema Yesu kaye koyekalaga kulya ndiya ya hamihe hamwe na heye. Aho Yesu nakaluta kuli ng'handa ya Mfalisayo, na kekalisa kulya ndiya.
Kuli ula mji hali mamo yumwe yawele na gehile. Loyahuliche Yesu kamng'handa ya ayo Mfalisayo, nakahola chupa ya alabasta iwelenguguzigwa kwa sendi nyinji imemile mafuta galingunhunyhilila ng'hatu.
Koya kema habehi hali magulu ga Yesu, kalila, na mahozi gake gasa gumlagalila Yesu mmagulu. Ayo mdala kaza kubagusa magulu ga Yesu kwa mnvili zake. Hamba kamnonela magulu na kumbakaliza gala mafuta gawele ngunhunyhilila.
Yula Mfalisayo yamchemile Yesu yawene ahyo, kazangijesa mnhumbula, “Wone munhu ayu na yawe Mloli wa Nguluwi, yahavizelele mdala ayu yamdolize, kandaze, kana gehile!”
Yesu nakamlonjela ayo Mfalisayo, yamchemile, “Simoni ndina chinhu cha kukulonjela.” Heye Simoni nakamlonjela, “Ena mlangusa undonjele.”
Yesu kaluka kulonga, “Wanhu weli wamwaziche munhu sendi, yumwe nayali yamwaziche sendi zihejile msahala wa mhela umwe na nusu, na yunji sendi denali miya zihano zihejile msahala wa mwezi umwe na nusu.
Lowalemwelile kumhilulila gowaziche ayo munhu, nahawadaile weng'ha weli, awo weli yalikohi yomgana lukami munhu yula yawaziche?”
Simoni nakedichila, “Ndangijesa ndo Yula yalechelwe sendi nyinji zoyawele ngudaigwa.” Yesu nakamlonjela “Goya.”
Hamba kagalamka kwa yula mdala kalonga, “Simoni kwangumona ayu mdala?, Heni honyinjile aha haluga hako humhele mazi ga kuhovujila magulu gangu, ila mdala ayu kanyhovuga magulu gangu na mahozi gake na kumbagusa na mnvili za heye.
Hegwe hundamse kwa kunonela, ila ayu myago mdala kulawa nyhinjile hano nayali yoganonela magulu gangu.
Hegwe hulajile isungu lyako kwa kumbakaliza mafuta ga ngulingunhunyhilila mmutwi, ila ayu myago mdala kadita ahyo kambakaliza magulu gangu.
Ahyo ndangukulonjela, ayu mdala kangungana ng'hatu, na ndo koselwa gehile ga heye menji. Ila munhu yoselwe gehile mado kangugana mado.”
Na baho Yesu nakamlonjela yula mdala, “Kusilwa geng'ha gehile gouditile.”
Aho wala wali hamwe mchisanya wazangiuza, “Munhu ayu kandaze kangumusila munhu gehile goyaditile?”
Heye Yesu nakamlonjela yula mdala, “Makundo ga hegwe gakulohola, ulute goya.”
Ago logapulute, Yesu nakakola mwesa yowadamlila Mbuli Inojile ya Undewa wa Nguluwi. Wala kumi na weli nawelongoza hamwe.
Na wadala wamwe wala Yesu nayawosele chijeni na matamwa, nawelongoza hamwe. Awo wali Maliya yachemigwe Madelena, yula nayosigwe vijeni vihile saba,
na Yohana mdala wa Kusa, mkola mijito mng'hangala wa Helodi. Wadala wali hamwe na Yesu ndo achina Susana na wadala wanji. Awo wadala wali wamditila Yesu kwa lufufu lwao hewo.
Mihela jimwe chilundo cha wanhu chali chimema, na wanhu wali womuyila Yesu kulawa chila honhu. Heye kawalonjela nhelo ayi.
“Mnyalaji nayaliyomiza azo nyhadikwa, zimwe nazigwa mnzila, wakola nzila wazibiga, videje vya kuulanga vilya.
Zinji nazigwa hali maganga, lozotile zikala lozisowile mazi.
Zinji nazigwa hali migodi jiwele na miwa. Jila migodi ja miwa jikula, nyhadikwa lozotile zipilinjilwa.
Zinji nazigwa hali misanga jinojile zota na zilela veduu!” Loyalonjile ahyo, kachemeleza lizi, kalonga, “Lelo mhuliche, yawele na makutu ga kuhulika nayahuliche!”
Walanguswa nawamuuza Yesu, nhelo ayi yangutulangusa choni?
Heye kawalonjela, “Hemwe mpegwa kuzizela zila zivisigwe za Undewa wa Nguluwi, ila awo wanji hebu, leka hewo wangulonjelwa kwa kulanguswa, leka, wone wazengulola waleche kugona, na wone wahuliche waleche kuvizela.
“Lelo nhelo ayi yangulonga ahi, nyhadikwa ndo ulonzi wa Nguluwi.
Zila zigwile mnzila zangulajila wala wanhu wawelenguhulika ulonzi wa Nguluwi, hamba lyokuya Limazoga lyanguzusa mnhumbula za hewo, waleche kukunda waloholigwe.
Zila zigwile hali italawe ndo wala walinguhulika awo ulonzi wanguubochela wasangalale. Ila kota zila nyhadikwa, ila wala wanhu wahela mizabi wangukunda hado hela, ila howojezigwa, wangugozola.
Zila zigwile mli igodi liwele na miwa, ndo zangulangusa wala wanhu wawelenguhulika ula ulonzi, hado hela, lowoluta wangubanigwa na kudumba, na vinhu vinojile vya isi, na hambe walele mafuza gakangale.
Na zila zigwile mli misanga jinojile, ndo wala wanhu wawelenguhulika ulonzi awo, wangibatilila mnhumbula, awo wangwimilila mbaka wangulela mafuza.
“Wanhu hawawesaga chenje na kuchigubika chidoto ama kuwika mluvungu lwa chinhanda. Ila wawikaga kuli honhu ha kuwichila chenje wogana wanhu lowokwinjila mla mng'handa wazengulola chila chenje.
“Chila chinhu chivisigwe chogubuligwa na chila chinhu chigubikwe, chozeleka na kuwichigwa hazelu.
“Lelo milolele vyomuwelenguhulika, mina yawele na chinhu kokonjezelwa, ila yula yalihela chinhu, chila choyalingijesa kanacho choholigwa.”
Aho mamo na wang'holoze Yesu wamuyila, ila na walemwela kumhejelela habehi wanhu nawamema lukami.
Munhu yumwe nakamlonjela Yesu, “Mayako na wang'holozo wakunze wangugana wakone.”
“Ila Yesu kawalonjela wanhu, mayangu na wang'holozangu ndo wala walinguhulika lizi lya Nguluwi na kibatilila.”
Zuwa limwe Yesu nakakwina mli itumbwi limwe hamwe na wala walanguswa, kawalonjela, “Tuloche ilamba mbaka kumwambu.” Waluka kuluta.
Lowali woluta mli itumbwi, Yesu nakebatigwa na usinjizi. Kawasa. Nhigu ya mazi ng'hangala yaluka kuputa, mazi galuka kwinjila mli itumbwi, kwaluka kwiha,
wala walanguswa wamlutila Yesu, wamwinula wolonga, “Mkulu, Mkulu! Tozangumala!” Yesu kenuka kaideuza ila nhigu na mbeho, baho vileka, kuwa tulu!.
Yesu kawauza, “Gakohi makundo ga hemwe?” Ila hewo wazangupulisa na kudumba kuno wochilonjela ayu ndo whaani? “Kanguilonjela nhigu na mbeho vyangumuhulika?”
Yesu nawalanguswa wa heye nawalutilila na majendo. Wafika mwhani ya isi ya Wagelasi ili kumwambu kwa ilamba lya Galilaya.
Loyali yodulika mwhani, munhu yumwe yawele na chijeni hala kulawa katali, ayo munhu hali yovala nguwo kahi nayali hambe yochikala kaye ila nakekalaga kuwele na vilaga!
Loyamuwene Yesu ketoza hanyi hoyali Yesu na kulonga lizi likulu, “Hegwe Yesu Mwana wa Nguluwi Mkulu, yawele kuchanya ng'hatu, kuna choni na heni ndangukulanda uleche kungaza!”
Nakalonga ahyo Yesu yaliyochilonjela acho chijeni chihile mlawe munhu ayu. Chijeni acho chihile nachimuyilaga ayo munhu mala nyinji. Wanhu nawamuwohaga na minyololo na kumhindila, ila myao nakadoholaga vyowamuwohile kangubilimiswa na acho chijeni chihile mbaka honhu hagunuche.
Yesu kamuuza, itagwa lyako kwa whaani? Heye kedichila itagwa lyangu chilundo cha wamizi. Mina mimazoga minji ja mumu.
Avyo vijeni vimdedeza uleche kutugala kuli ikulubila.
Honhu hala hali na migubi minji jidimigwa mchidunda. Ahyo, avyo vijeni vilawe viwenjile. Baho Yesu kawakundiza.
Avyo vijeni vimlawa yula munhu, wazakwinjila kuli migubi, jila migubi jilawa jifiduka jizakwinjila kuli ilamba lya mazi jibagama.
Wala wadimi lowagawene ago geng'ha galawile nawabilima waza kuwalonjela wanhu mbuli azo kuli miji na kumigunda.
Wanhu woya kulola galawile, wamlutila Yesu Wamona yula munhu yalavigwe chijeni yekalise habehi na Yesu yavalile nguwo yawele na luhala lwake luhiluche, wanhu weng'ha wadumba.
Wala wanhu waliwene alyo lilawile wawasimila wayao, vila ayo munhu yawele na chijeni voyaloholigwe.
Wenyeng'haye wa isi ya Gelasi, nawadumba heko! Wazangumlonjela Yesu yoche, baho Yesu nakakwina kahi mli itumbwi, koka
Yula munhu yalavigwe vijeni kazangumdedeza Yesu walutase. Ila Yesu hakundile, ila nakamlonjela
“Hiluche kaye kalonje geng'ha Nguluwi goyakuditile.” Yula munhu kaluta yodamla chila honhu hali muji ula gala geng'ha Yesu goyamditile.
Yesu loyahiluche nzingo iyage ya ilamba, wanhu wenji wambochela kwa mina wali wombeteza
Baho koya munhu yumwe yawele nguchemigwa Jailo, mkulu wa ng'handa ya kusalila, kafugama mmagulu ga Yesu kamlanda yalute kaye kwa heye,
Mina mwanage mdala yawele na miyaka kumi na mili, nayali mtamwa lukami behi na kubagama. Yesu loyali yoluta, wanhu waza kummemelela chila nzingo
Aho hali na mdala yumwe hali wala wanhu wamemile, nayali na utamwa wa kulawa danda miyaka kumi na mili. Na heye nakalavya sendi nyinji kwa walaguzi yochiteleka, ila haduhuli yamlohole.
Ayo mdala nakamuwinza Yesu mmbele, nakadoliza lupembo lwa nguwo ya heye. Baho kaloholigwa utamwa wa heye wa kulawa danda.
Yesu kauza, “Yalikohi yandolize?” Weng'ha walonga haduhuli munhu yakudolize. Wanhu weng'ha walema ila Petili kalonga, “Mkulu wanhu wenji wakuzunguluta na kiminyangaminyanga.”
Ila Yesu kalonga, “Kakuko munhu yandolize, mina nambona mong'ho wa heni wa kulohola undawa.”
Yula mdala yawene howeza kivisa kalawa yokakama kuno yodumba, ketoza mmagulu ga Yesu. Hala nakamlonjela Yesu kumwando hali wanhu weng'ha chimwambuze kumdoliza Yesu na vyoyosigwe utamwa bahala.
Yesu nakamlonjela yula mdala, “Mhinza, makundo ga hegwe gakulohola. Ulute goya.”
Yesu loyali yang'hali yodawala, Jailo chilongozi wa ng'handa ya kusalila kegalilwa na chitumagwa nguto kulawa kaye. “Mina mhinza we hegwe nakabagama, lekachoni, uzengumgaza Mlangusa lukami.”
Yesu loyahuliche ago nakamlonjela Jailo, “Uleche kudumba ukunde! Heye kowa mkomu.”
Loyafichile kaye kwa Jailo hamkundize munhu kwinjila mg'handa hamwe na heye, ila Petili nayali yeng'ha. Yohani, na Yakubu na wahaza wa ayo mdala.
Wanhu weng'ha wali wowemba na kwimbilila. Ila Yesu kawalonjela, “Mleche kuwemba, yuno mwana habagame kawasa hela!”
Hewo wazangumseka mina nawavizela yula mwana kabagama.
Ila Yesu kambata moko kalonga, “Gomwana winuche!”
Muhe wa heye imuhiluchila, bahala kalilimka. Yesu kawalonjela mgalileni ndiya.
Wala wahaza wahuliche wabubuwala, ila Yesu kawalonjela waleche kumlonjela ne munhu ago galawile.
Yesu nakawachema hamwe walanguswa wa heye kumi na weli na kawapa mong'ho na ludali lwa kulavya vijeni na kuwosela wanhu matamwa.
Na baho kawalajiza walute kudamla mbuli ya Undewa wa Nguluwi na kuwosela wanhu matamwa.
Kawalonjela, “Lomkuka mleche kuhola chinhu choneche chila, mleche kuhola ng'hweku ne mhako ne ndiya ne sendi ne igwanda lya keli.
Chila ng'handa yoneche yomkwinjila na kubocheligwa, mikale mumo mbaka lomkuka kuli muji awo.
Na wanhu wone waleme kukubochelani mlawe aho honhu, namwe lomlawa mkung'hune nhimbwisi iwele mmagulu genu iwe ulolezi wa kuwapanjila hewo.”
Walanguswa waluka kuluta, na wakola mli vijiji wodamla Mbuli Inojile na kuwosela wanhu matamwa chila honhu.
Helodi mndewa wa Galilaya loyahuliche mbuli zeng'ha lozilawile, kadumba ng'hatu kwa vila wanhu wenji na wekala wolonga kota Yohani Mbatiza kazilipuka kulawa koyabagame.
Wamwe walonga Eliya kalawila na wamwe walonga yumwe wa waloli wakatali kazilipuka kulawa kowabagame.
Ila mndewa Helodi kalonga, “Yohani ndimdumula mutwi. Hambi! Zino zondihulika mbuli za heye yalihi?” Ahyo kagana yamone Yesu.
Wala watumigwa lowahuliche, wamlonjela Yesu chila chinhu chowaditile. Yesu kawahola waliyeng'ha, kaluta nawo mbaka chijiji chiwelenguchemigwa Betisaida.
Ila wanhu lowavizelele koyalutile, nawamuwinza. Yesu kawabochela, kalonga na hewo mbuli za Undewa wa Nguluwi na kawalohola wala waliwogana kuloholigwa.
Isanya lolyaluche kuzinga, walanguswa kumi na weli waluta na kumlonjela, “Walonjele wanhu walute kuli vijiji na migunda ja habehi, wekepalile chilyo na honhu ha kuwasa, kwa vila honhu aha twa kisolo.”
Ila Yesu kawedichila, “Muwape hemwe chilyo walye.” Hewo wamwidichila, “Hetwe twanajo mibumunda jihano na somba mbili. Mane twangona tulute twetwe tukawagulile ndiya wanhu weng'ha awa!”
Walume waliyeng'ha wali hala, wali elufu zihano. Yesu kawalonjela wala walanguswa, “Muwalonjele wanhu wekalise hasi chila honhu walume elufu zihano.”
Wala walanguswa wadita hihila, na wanhu weng'ha wekala hasi.
Baho Yesu kahola jila mibumunda jihano na zila somba mbili, kalola kuchanya kilanga, katambichiza, kamogola mibumunda na somba na kawapa walanguswa wa heye wawagawile wanhu.
Wanhu weng'ha walya, na weguta. Walokoteza usanyangwa uponile vimema vikowe kumi na vili.
Zuwa limwenga Yesu nayali yomlanda Nguluwi yaliyeka. Walanguswa wamuyila na heye kawauza, “Hambi Wanhu wangulonga heni nda yalihi?”
Na Hewo wamwidichila, “Wamwe wangulonga hegwe Yohani Mbatiza, wamwe wangulonga hegwe Eliya, na wamwe wangulonga yumwe wa waloli wa Nguluwi wakatali yazilipuche kulawa kowabagame.”
Na heye kawauza, “Na hemwe mwangulonga heni nda whaani?” Petili kedichila, “Hegwe ndo Kilistu Mlohozi yahaguligwe na Nguluwi.”
Na baho Yesu kawalonjela waleche kumlonjela ne munhu chinhu chino.
Hamba kawalonjela, “Mwana wa munhu koganigwa kugazigwa ng'hatu na kulemigwa na walalile na watambika wakulu na walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa. Kokomigwa, ila zuwa lya kadatu kozilipuka.”
Na baho kawalonjela wanhu weng'ha, munhu yoneche yogana kumbinza heni yeleme yuye, yahole msalaba wa heye yambinze.
Kwa vila munhu yoneche yogana kuulohola ukomu wa heye kowajiliza, ila munhu nayali ngwajiliza ukomu wa heye kwa mbuli ya heni koulohola.
Ndaze, munhu yowa na chila chinhu mu isi yeng'ha, ila yowajiliza ukomu wa heye, munhu ayo kopata choni chinojile?
Wone munhu yambonele soni na gala gondilingulangusa, mwana wa munhu komonela soni ayo munhu mihela joyokuya mu ukulu wa heye na wa Mhaza na wahilisi wa kilanga welile.
Ndangukulonjelani ndikomya, wabahano wanhu hawobagama mbaka wawone Undewa wa Nguluwi.
Mazuwa nane kulawa loyalonjile mbuli azo, Yesu nakawahola Petili na Yohani na Yakubu, kaluta nawo kuchidunda kulanda.
Yesu Loyali yolanda, chihanga cha heye chigaluka na livalo liwa izelu chwee!
Na baho wanhu weli woneka wolonga na heye. Wanhu awo wali Musa na Eliya,
nawoneka wana ukulu wa kilanga, na wolonga na Yesu mbuli za heye zizangulawila ako Yelusalemu.
Petili na wayage wali wawasile, ila lowalilipuche, wawona ukulu wa Yesu na wanhu weli na wali wemile hamwe na heye.
Awo wanhu wala lowamlechile Yesu, Petili nakamlonjela Yesu. “Mkulu, goya hetwe tikale hano! Leka tuzenje vibumuli vidatu, chimwe cha hegwe na chimwe cha musa na chimwe cha Eliya.” Petili na havizelele hebu choyaliyolonga.
Petili loyalutilile kulonga ago, ng'hungugu ilawila iwagubika, na ng'hungugu ila loiwoyele wala walaguswa nawadumba ng'hatu lowagubichwe na ng'hungugu ayo!.
Lizi ilonga kulawa mli ila ng'hungugu, “Ayu ndo mwana wa heni ndimhagule, muhulichize heye.”
Lizi loihulikwe, Yesu nakoneka nayali yeng'ha. Walanguswa wanyamalila na hawamlonjele ne munhu mbuli ayo yowaiwene.
Mitondo yake, Yesu na wala walanguswa wadatu lowali wodulika kulawa kuchidunda, lung'hongola lwa wanhu wenji naluting'hana na Yesu.
Mumula mli wanhu wenji kalawila munhu kachemeleza lizi yolonga, “Mlangusa! Ndangukulanda umlole mwana wa heni, ka mwana yaliyeng'ha yonditumbila!
Chijeni chimgazaga, na chimditaga yanzenguyowa, chimditaga chinzilisa na ifulo lilawaga kumlomo, chilemaga kumleka na kumzuhulanga.
Nandiwalanda walanguswa wa hegwe wamlavye chijeni acho, ila walemwela.”
Yesu kedichila, “Hambi hemwe ulelo lulihela makundo, wajilile na uli na gehile! Ndochikala na hemwe mbaka nili?” Na baho nakamlonjela munhu yula, “Ngalile msongolo wa hegwe hano.”
Msongolo yula loyezile, chila chijeni nachimgwisa hanyi chimzilisa. Yesu nakaching'hanuchila chila chijeni chihile na kumlohola yula, na baho kamhilusila mhaza wa heye.
Walanguswa weng'ha wekala wabubuwale kwa ukulu woyawele nawo Nguluwi. Wala wanhu lowang'hali bahala wabubuwale mbuli zila zoyaditile, Yesu kawalonjela wala woyalinguwalangusa,
“Mhulichize chino cho ndikulonjelani! Mwana wa Munhu kanguzawichigwa mmoko mwa wanhu.”
Ila hewo hawauzelele hebu uviso wa ulonzi awo, kwa vila nauvisigwa kwa hewo waleche kuvizela hebu, na hewo wadumba kumuuza Yesu.
Wala walanguswa walikiuza hewo kwa hewo, yalihi yawele mkulu ng'hatu hali hetwe.
Yesu kagona majesa ga hewo, kamhola mwana mdodo, kamuwika habehi na hewo.
Na baho Kawalonjela, “Munhu yoneche yawele ngumbochela mwana mdodo ayu, kwa itagwa lyangu kangumbochela heni, na munhu yoneche yele ngumbochela heni, kangumbochela yula yanhumile. Kwa vila munhu nayali mdodo homuli, ayo mkulu kusinda weng'ha.”
Yohani nakamlonjela Yesu. “Mkulu tumona munhu yolavya chijeni kwa itagwa lya hegwe. Tumlemeza kudita vila, kwa vila hetwe hatulikilongoza na heye.”
Ila Yesu nakamlonjela Yohani na walanguswa wamwe, “Mleche kumlemeza! Kwa vila munhu yula yokulemele hegwe, kahamwe na hegwe.”
Mazuwa ga kuholigwa kwa Yesu kilanga louwele habehi, Yesu kagana kuluta Yelusalemu.
Kawalajiza walanguswa wamlongole, walute kuli chijiji chimwe chili muisi ya Samaliya kumuwichila goya chila chinhu.
Ila wenyeng'haye wa hala, hawaganile kumbochela, kwa vila nawavizela kota nayali yoluta Yelusalemu.
Walanguswa wa heye, Yohani na Yakubu lowagawene ago, wamuuza Yesu, “Mkulu, hambi kwangugana tuchilonjele chiluli chiwadulichile kulawa kilanga uwalakaze weng'ha?”
Ila heye kawagalamchila kawadeuza.
Na baho Yesu na walanguswa wa heye waluta kuli chijiji chiyage.
Lowali wokola mnzila, munhu yumwe nakamlonjela Yesu, “Ndokuwinza koneche kouluta.”
Yesu kawalonjela, “Mibwa ja kisolo jina mhalika na videje vya kuulanga vina vimvulila, ila mwana wa munhu kahela honhu ha kuwasiliza mutwi na kwesela.”
Hamba Yesu nakamlonjela munhu yumwenga, “Umbinze.” Ila munhu ayo kalonga, “Mkulu ung'hundize tandi ndute ndikamtile mhaza wa heni.”
Yesu kamwidichila, “Waleche wabagame wawatile wayao wabagame, ila hegwe ulute kadamle kuya kwa Undewa wa Nguluwi.”
Munhu yumwenga nakamlonjela, “Ndokuwinza hegwe Mkulu, ila undeche ndikawalaje wang'holozangu kaye.”
Yesu nakamlonjela, “Munhu yoneche yengibata ihuka kulima kumgunda, baho yolola kumbele, hambe yaganigwe kuli Undewa wa Nguluwi.”
Hamba, Mkulu nakawahagula wanhu wanji sabini na weli, kawalajiza weliweli, wamlongole chila honhu na chila chijiji hoyaganile heye kuluta.
Kawalonjela, “Mbena nyinji, ila wakola mijito wachefu. Lelo mumlande Mkulu yalajize wakola mijito wabene mbena ya heye.
Mluteni, ndanguwalajiza hemwe kota wana ming'holo kuli mibwa ja kisolo
Mleche kuhola sendi ne mhako ne makwamba na mleche kwima na kumlamsa munhu yoneche mnzila.
Ng'handa yoneche yila yomkwinjila, mlongole na kuwalamsa ahi, ‘Mikale goya mng'handa ino.’
Wone kuwe baho na munhu yalingugana kikala goya, kikala goya kowa hamwe na heye, wone hebu kikala goya kowahiluchilani.
Mikale mli ng'handa yiyo, mulye na kunwa cheng'ha chila chowawichilani, kwa vila mkola mijito kangugana yapegwe sendi za heye. Mleche kulabajila kulawa ng'handa imwe kuli nyinji.
Wone mfiche kuli muji na wanhu wawabochelani, mulye chilyo chompegwa.
Muwosele matamwa wali ku muji awo, na muwalonjele, Undewa wa Nguluwi wa habehi na hemwe.
Ila wone mwinjile kuli muji na wanhu waleme kuwabochela, mlawe namwe lomkola mnzila za hewo, mlonje,
‘Na nhimbwisi za hakaye ha hemwe jeng'ha jing'hang'hanile mmagulu getu twangujikung'huna hali hemwe. Ila mvizele Undewa wa Nguluwi wa habehi na hemwe!’
Ndangulonga ndikomya, kuli zuwa lya utaguso, Nguluwi koutagusa muji ula vikulu kusinda yila ya wanhu wa Sodoma.
“Mane gwegwe, muji wa Kolasini! Kozakugaya! Hegwe muji wa Betisaida kozagaya! Kwa vila kota vinduzanduza vikoleke Tilo na Sidoni, wanhu wa hala wahavalile mivalo ja kulombocheza na kubakala mivu kulajila kota wamgalamchila Nguluwi.
Kuli zuwa lya utaguso Nguluwi kowatagusa hemwe vikulu kusinda yila ya Tilo na Sidoni.
Na hegwe Kapanaumu! Ndaze kogana kiinula mbaka kilanga? Hebu! Kozabiduswa mbaka kuli isi ya wabagame!”
Yesu nakawalonjela walanguswa wa heye, “Munhu yoneche yalinguwahulichiza hemwe, kangunyhulichiza heni, na yalingulema kuwabochela hemwe, kangundema heni. Na yula yalingulema kumbochela, kangulema kumbochela yula yanhumile.”
Hamba wala mkumi saba na weli nawahiluka wasangalale, wolonga, “Mkulu na vijeni vihile vituhulika lotuchemile itagwa lya hegwe.”
Yesu kawedichila, “Na ndilyona Limazoga lyolagala kulawa kilanga kota lumuli.
Ndiwapa ludali lwa kubiga mizoka na nyinje na mong'ho weng'ha wa kuwasumya wakwihileni, na kuduhu chinhu chiwalumiza.
