Ahyo mleche kusangalala kwa vila lomuwene vijeni viwahuliche, ila msangalale kwa vila matagwa genu gandikwa kilanga.”
Mhela wuwula, Yesu kasangalala kwa Muhe Yelile ya Nguluwi. Na baho kalonga, “Ndangumtogola, Mhaza, Mkulu wa kilanga na muisi, na kuwavisa wali na luhala na wasomile mbuli azi, kuwagubulila wana wadodo. Ena Mhaza, ahyo ndo vouganile.”
Hamba kalonga, “Mhaza wa heni kanipa vinhu vyeng'ha. Kuduhu yamzelele Mwana ila Mhaza, na kuduhu yamzelele Mhaza ila Mwana, na yoneche yula Mwana yogana kumgubulila heye.”
Hamba kawahinduchila walanguswa wa heye na kulonga nawo chinyele, “Wabweda wanhu wala walinguvyona vinhu vyomlinguvyona hemwe!
Ndangukulonjelani ndikomya, waloli wenji na wandewa nawagana kugona aga gomlingugona hemwe, ila hawagawene, na kuhulika gala gomhuliche hemwe, hawagahuliche.”
Munhu yumwe yagazelele ng'hatu malajizo ga Musa koya kwa Yesu kumjeza, kamuuza, “Mlangusa, hambi ndite ndaze ndiuhole ukomu wa mazuwa gose ne kuduma?”
Yesu kamwidichila, “Malajizo gangulonga ndaze? Hegwe kugazela ndaze?”
Munhu yula kamwidichila, “ ‘Mgane Mkulu Nguluwi kwa nhumbula ya hegwe yeng'ha na kwa muhe wa hegwe weng'ha na kwa mong'ho wa hegwe weng'ha na kwa luhala lwako lweng'ha’ Na ‘Umgane youlingikalasa habehi kota, kota vyoulingigana gwegwe baho.’ ”
Yesu kamwidichila, “Kwidika goya, udite ahyo nagwe kozanguwa mkomu.”
Ila munhu yula yogana kiwona kanoga, aho nakamuuza Yesu, “Yali behi na heni kakohi?”
Yesu kamwidichila, “Kwali na munhu yumwe yalawile kulawa Yelusalemu kuza Yeliko. Loyali mnzila, kebatigwa na wahizi wamsukula vyeng'ha vyoyali navyo na kumtowa. Wamleka yawasile bahala kota yabagame.
Baho mtambika yumwe kakola kuli nzila ila loyamuwene munhu yula yatowigwe, kakola hafungo.
Vivila na Mulawi yumwe voyafichile hala na kumona munhu yatowigwe, na heye kakola hafungo.
Ila Msamalia yumwe loyaliyojenda, nakafika hala hoyali yula munhu yatowigwe, na heye loyamuwene, kamonela isungu.
Kamhejelela habehi, kambumba vilonda vya heye, na kuvibakaliza mafuta na Divai. Hamba kamkwiniza mchanya mwa idogowi lyake, kamigala mbaka kuli ng'handa ya wajenzi na kumwimilila.
Mitondo Msamaliya yula kalavya sendi denali mbili zihejile msahala wa mazuwa meli kamlechela mlolela ng'handa ya wajenzi nakamlonjela, ‘Muguze ayu munhu, choneche chonzezeche kwa chuguzo, ndokuhilusila hondihiluka.’ ”
Hamba Yesu kamuuza munhu yula, “Hambi kuli wala wanhu wadatu, yalikohi yalajile kota munhu wa habehi na heye, yula munhu yatowigwe na wabokaji?”
Na Yula munhu yavizelele ng'hatu Malajizo ga Musa, kedichila, “Yula yamonele isungu.” Yesu nakamlonjela, “Leka nagwe ulute kadite hiho.”
Yesu na walanguswa wa heye lowali woluta mnzila, wenjila mli chijiji chimwe. Mdala yumwe nayali nguchemigwa Malita nakambochela hakaye hake.
Mdala yula nayali kikala na mkulugwe nayali nguchemigwa Maliya, ayu nakekalisa habehi na Mkulu. Na heye na kekala yohulichiza ulanguso wa Yesu.
Ila Malita nayali yodita mbuli ziyage nyinji, kamlutila Yesu na kumuuza, “Mkulu hambi hulingona mng'holozangu voyandechile mbuli zeng'ha ndidita ndiliyeng'ha?, Mlonjele yoye yanhanze!”
Mkulu kamwidichila, “Malita, Malita! Kwanguhangawa na kugaya na vinhu vinji,
Ila Changuganigwa chinhu chimwe hano. Maliya kahagula chinhu chinojile, chili kuduhu munhu yomsukula.”
Zuwa limwe Yesu nayali honhu hamwe yolanda. Loyasindile kulanda, mlanguswa wa heye yumwe nakamlonjela, “Mkulu, twangukulanda tulanguse kulanda kota Yohani Mbatiza voyawalanguse walanguswa wa heye.”
Yesu nakawalonjela, “Lomlanda, mlonje hino, “ ‘Mhaza, itagwa lya hegwe litogoligwe, undewa wa hegwe uye.
Utugalile chila zuwa chilyo cha hetwe chotulingugana.
Utusile gehile getu, kota hetwe vyotulinguwosela hewo weng'ha watuzudize. Uleche kutwinjiza muli kujezigwa.’ ”
Hamba Yesu nakawalonjela walanguswa wa heye, “Tulonje yumwe wa hemwe kanguluta kaye kwa goloko wa heye nechilo na kumlonjela, ‘Goloko, ndangukulanda unyipe chilyo,
lekachoni goloko wa heni kakolela haluga hangu yolawa koyalutile, na heni ndahela ne chilyo cha kumha’
Na tulonje yula goloko nayali mng'handa kangwidichila, ‘Uleche kunganza! Chihindilo mina chihindigwa, na heni na wanangu tuwasa. Hambe nyhinuche ndikupe chinhu choneche chila.’
Ndanguwalonjelani, leka wone hoyile kukupa lekachoni ni goloko wa heye, ila kwavila hulingona soni kulutilila kulanda, kokwinuka na kukupa chila choulanda.
“Ahyo ndanguwalonjelani, Mlande, namwe mopegwa, na mpale, namwe mochona, mhodize, namwe mochumulilwa.
Mina yoneche yolanda kopegwa, na yalingupala kachonaga na yohodiza lwizi, kochumulilwa.
Hino mhaza yalikohi wone mwana wa heye yamlande somba, heye komupa izoka? Wone yamlande libumunda, heye kompa iganga.
Ama yalikohi wone mwana wa heye yamlande ifinga kompa nyhinje?
Wone hemwe hanga muwele wehile, mvizela kuwapa wana wa hemwe vinhu vinojile, ndangukomya Mhaza wa hemwe wa kilanga kodita vikulu ng'hatu, kowapa Muhe Yelile wala walingumlanda?”
Zuwa limwe Yesu nayali yolavya chijeni chihile chilingumudita munhu yumwe yaleche kulonga. Acho chijeni lochilawile, yula munhu kaza ngulonga. Wanhu wenji wabubuwala ng'hatu.
Ila wanhu wamwenga bahala walonga, “Kangulavya vijeni kwa ludali lwa Belisebuli, mkulu wa vijeni.”
Wanhu wamwe nawagana kumjeza Yesu, ahyo yawalajile ulajilo kulawa kilanga.
Ila Yesu nakavizela chowochijesa mnhumbula za hewo, kawalonjela, “Undewa weng'ha wula ugawanuche vilundo vilingitwanza, havilutilila ng'hatu. Kahi lukolo lyochitowa lyosumigwa.
Wone Limazoga lizengugawanuka lilyo, hino undewa wa heye wokwima ndaze? Ndangulonga hino kwavila hemwe mwangulonga heni ndangulavya vijeni kwa ludali lwa Belisebuli.
Wone heni ndilingulavya vijeni kwa ludali lwa Belisebuli, lelo wala wana wa hemwe walavyaga vijeni kwa ludali lwani, lwa Limazoga? Hebu! Ahyo, wana wa hemwe wokunda kuwatagusa hemwe kota mwiha.
Ila wone heni ndanguwinga vijeni kwa ludali lwa Nguluwi, mvizele kota Undewa wa Nguluwi mina ukuyilani hemwe.
“Munhu nayali na ludali yokwamila ng'handa ya heye kwa migoha, vinhu vya heye vya goya.
Ila wone munhu nayali na ludali lung'hangala ng'hatu yoye kumtowa, komsukula migoha jeng'ha yawele kidaila, na kuhola vinhu vya heye vyeng'ha na kuvitaganga.
Yoneche yohambe yebande na heni, kangundema, na yoneche hambe yekungajize hamwe na heni, kangusambalula.
“Chijeni chihile lochiwinjigwa kwa munhu, chibemhelaga honhu hagunuche, chipala honhu ha kwesela. Wone hachipatile, changulonga, ‘Ndohiluka kaye kwa heni.’
Lochihiluka na kuchifika chigoda cha heye chihovugwe na kunoligwa,
choluta kuvihola vijeni vinji saba vihile kusinda heye. Na hevyo vyeng'ha vyoluta na kikala aho. Ahyo ayo munhu kowa yogazigwa ng'hatu kusinda aho hamwande.”
Yesu loyali yolonga ago, mdala yumwe hala hali wanhu wamemile kalonga kwa lizi likulu, “Kabweda mdala yakulelile na kukonyeza!”
Yesu nakedichila, “Wabweda wala weng'ha walinguhulika ulonzi wa Nguluwi na kudita vila vyouwaganile kukola.”
Wanhu wenji lowali wommemelela Yesu, heye kalutilila kuwalonjela, “Lulelo alu ndo lulelo lwihile lulingugana ulajilo! Kuduhu munhu yowapa ulajilo ila ulajilo wa Yona.
Kota vila Yona vyoyali ulajilo kwa wanhu wa Ninawi, ndo hihyo Mwana wa Munhu kowa ulajilo kwa wanhu wa lulelo alu.
Malikiya wa kusini kulawila mhela wanhu awo howotagusigwa kwa wihe, na heye kowatagusa kwa wihe. Mina heye nakajenda kulawa isi ya kutali, nakuya kuhulichiza ulonzi wa luhala wa Solomoni, na hanga hano kuwele na chikulu kusinda Solomoni.
Wanhu wa Ninawi wolawila mhela wa kutagusigwa kwa wihe, na hewo wochitagusa lulelo alu kota luna wihe. Mina Waninawi nawamgalamchila Nguluwi kwa mbuli ya kudamla kwa Yona, na hano hana chikulu kusinda Yona!
“Haduhu munhu yawelenguwesa chenje na kuvisa awu kugubika na chidoto. Ila chenje chiwikagwa honhu ha kuwichila chenje leka wanhu wokwinjila wazengulola lumuli.
Iziho lyako ndo chenje cha lukuli lwa hegwe. Wone iziho lyako liwe lilola, lukuli lwako lweng'ha lowa na lumuli. Ila liziho lyako wone liwe hambe lilole, na lukuli lwako lweng'ha lowa hatitile.
Lelo wilolele, lumuli louwele nalo mgati luleche kutita.
Ahyo wone lukuli lwako lweng'ha luna lumuli, na haduhu honhu hatitile, baho lumuli lowa chila honhu, kota vila chenje lochikumwemwesela lumuli lwake.”
Yesu loyasindile kulonga, Mfalisayo yumwe nakamlanda yalute haluga hake yalye ndiya hamwe na heye. Ahyo Yesu kaluta, kekalisa kulya ndiya.
Mfalisayo ayo kabubuwala loyawene Yesu yolya ndiya nekuhovuga moko.
Mkulu nakamlonjela, “Hemwe Mafalisayo mwanguhovuga chizombe na luhelo kwa kunze, ila mgati mwa hemwe mmema ubuhu na ubokaji na wihe.
Mwawapoka hemwe! Hino heye yalumbile kunze si heye yula yalumbile mgati?
Ila muwape wazunwa vinhu mlinavyo, na Nguluwi kosangalala ng'hatu na chila chinhu chomdita chowa chelile.
“Mochona hemwe Mafalisayo! Lekachoni mwangulavya zaka za vinhu kota vila chizanga na tangawizi, na mboga ziyage zinji za mahamba, ila mwanguleka mbuli zilingutagusa goya na mwanguleka kumgana Nguluwi. Ahi ndo vyomlinguganigwa kudita ne kusemwa zila zinji.
“Mochona hemwe Mafalisayo! Lekachoni mwangugana kikalisa mli vigoda vya kumwando kuli ng'handa za kusalila, na kulamsigwa kwa ukulu kuli masoko.
Mochona hemwe kwa vila mfanda kota vilaga vilihela vilajilo, wanhu wangujenda mchanya hake nekuvizela.”
Yumwe wa wala wavizelele ng'hatu Malajizo ga Musa nakamwidichila Yesu, “Mlangusa, vyoulonga ayo kwangutuliga hetwe!”
Yesu nakamlonjela, “Na hemwe walangusa wa Malajizo mochona! Mwanguwadwika wanhu mhomolo zohambe ziholeche, kuno hemwe mwemwe hambe muwatanze ne kwa chidole hela.
Mochona hemwe! Mwanguzenga vilaga vya waloli wa Nguluwi, na waloli wawo wa Nguluwi nawakopoligwe na wasekulu wa hemwe.
Na hemwe sambi mwangulavya ulolezi kwa chila chowaditile wasekulu wa hemwe, mina hewo nawawakopola waloli, namwe mwanguzenjela vilaga.
Ahyo kwa mbuli ino, luhala lwa Nguluwi lwangulonga ahi, ‘Ndowegalila waloli na watumigwa, wowakopola wamwe na kuwagaza wamwe.’
Ahyo wanhu wa lulelo alu lotagusigwa kwa kuwakopola waloli weng'ha kulawa isi loilumbigwe,
kulawa kukopoligwa kwa Abeli mbaka kukopoligwa kwa Sakaliya, yula nawamkopole hagati ha honhu ha kulavila nhambiko na honhu helile. Ena, ndanguwalonjelani, lulelo alu logazigwa kwa kuwakopola awo weng'ha.
“Mochona hemwe walangusa wa malajizo! Mwanguvisa chichumulilo cha lwizi lwa ng'handa ya luhala. Hemwe mwemwe hamkwinjila, na mwanguwalemeza wanji kwingila.”
Yesu loyaliyolawa hala, wala Mafalisayo na walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa nawaluka kumpinga, na wakamchokoza kwa kumuuza mbuli nyinji,
wogana wamgwilize luzi loyolonga kota kawifya.
Mhela wula, wanhu wenji lukami nawamema mbaka nawazangibiga. Yesu nakaluka kuwalonjela walanguswa wa heye tandi, “Milolele na ulanguso wihile wa Mafalisayo ulinguwahada.
Chinhu choneche chigubikwe chogubuligwa, na chila chivisigwe chozeleka.
Ahyo chila chomlonga kutitu, wanhu wochihulika hali lumuli, na chila chomlonga kwa kupwepwa mliyeng'ha mchihengo, chodamlwa mchanya mli ng'handa.
“Ndangukulonjelani hemwe tuwele ngigana, mleche kuwadumba wawele ngukopola lukuli, hamba howoweza kudita chinhu chinji chihile.
Ndokulajilani yula yalinguganigwa kudumbigwa. Mdumbe Nguluwi, wone yakopole munhu, kana ludali lwa kumtaga muli chiluli cha Jehanamu. Ndangulonga, mdumbeni ayo.
“Ndaze, semembe wahano haviguzwa kwa sendi mbili? Ila kuduhu na chideje nechimwe chisemigwa na Nguluwi.
Lelo hata mnvili za mitwi jenu ziwazigwa zeng'ha. Mleche kudumba, lekachoni hemwe mganigwa kusinda videje!
“Ndangukulonjelani ndikomya, munhu yoneche yalikung'hunda hali wanhu, Mwana wa Munhu na heye komkunda hali wahilisi wa kilanga wa Nguluwi.
Ila munhu yoneche yalingundema hali wanhu, Mwana wa Munhu na heye komlema hali wahilisi wa kilanga wa Nguluwi.
“Munhu yoneche yawelengulonga ulonzi wa kumbeza Mwana wa Munhu kolecheligwa, ila munhu yoneche yalingumkovula Muhe Yelile holecheligwa hebu.
“Lowowagala hemwe kuli ng'handa za kusalila na kumwando kwa wakulu na vilongozi, mleche kuwa na lunhwinhwi ndaze vyomchigombela na vyomkwidichila.
Mina Muhe Yelile yokulangusani mihela jijo chila chomganigwa kulonga.”
Munhu yumwe muli wanhu wala wamemile nakamlonjela, “Mlangusa, mlonjele mng'holozangu tiigawile vinhu vyoyalechile mhaza wa hetwe.”
Yesu nakamlonjela, “Hegwe, yalikohi yambichile heni ndiwe ndiwamulila ama mgawaniza wa vinhu vya hemwe?”
Hamba Yesu nakawalonjela weng'ha, “Milolele na ubuhu, mina ukomu wa munhu hauwele kuli vinhu loyawele navyo!”
Kahi Yesu nakawalonjela nhelo, “Kwali na munhu nayali na lufufu na nayali na mgunda ulelile lukami.
Ayo munhu kazangijesa mnhumbula ya heye, ‘Lelo ndodita ndaze? Ndahela honhu ha kuhega kuwika chilyo cha heni.’
Hamba kelonjela, ‘Ndodita ahi, ndobomola ng'hano za heni na kuzenga zinji zili ng'hangala ng'hatu. Mumo hondiwika chilyo na vinhu vya heni vyeng'ha.
Hamba ndoilonjela nhumbula ya heni, lelo ndiwichila vinhu vya kulya vinojile mihela na mihela. Ahyo wesele, widile, winwele na usangalale!’
Ila Nguluwi nakamlojela, ‘Mpoka hegwe! Lehano nechilo muhe wa hegwe yoholigwa! Vinhu vyeng'ha vyowilundile vyowa vyaani?’ ”
Kahi Yesu nakasinda kwa kulonga, “Ahyo ndo vyoiwa kwa munhu yawelengilundila lufufu kwa heye, na hambe yewichile lufufu kwa Nguluwi”.
Hamba Yesu nakawalonjela walanguswa wa heye, “Na ahyo ndangukulonjelani, mleche kijesa kwa mbuli ya chilyo yomgana leka mikale, na nguwo zomgana mvalize ng'huli za hemwe.
Kwa vila ukomu unoga kusinda chilyo, na lukuli lunoga kusinda nguwo.
Mjilole ajo mibondwa, havilingunyala nyhadikwa, havilingubeta nyhadikwa kahi jahela ng'hano, leka ahyo Nguluwi Mhaza wa hemwe wa kilanga kanguwahombela. Hemwe mnoga ng'hatu kusinda videje.
Ndaze, hagati ha hemwe kuna munhu kwa mbuli ya lunhwinhwi yoweza kuhejeza ne saa imwe ya kikala muisi?
Lelo wone mlemwa kukola mbuli ndodo kota ayo, iwandaze mwangutochela azo mbuli zinji?
Mlole uluwa vyoulingutitima. Hagalingukola chinhu cha kiditila mibadu. Ndangukulonjelani, na heye Solomoni na lufufu lwake lweng'ha, nahavalile goya kota uluwa umwenga kuli uluwa umwenga.
Nguluwi yalingugana mahamba gawe na mibadu, na misolo lehano jangutitima na mitondo janguvunda na kujisoma mchiluli! Ndaze, howaditilani hemwe mzidi? Hemwe wanhu muwele na makundo mado!
“Ahyo mleche kugayila choni cho mulya na choni cho munwa, na mleche kudumba.
Mina ago geng'ha wanhu hawamzelele Nguluwi wangugagayila. Mhaza wa hemwe wa kilanga, kavizela kota mwangugana vinhu avi.
Ahyo mijeseni tandi Undewa wa Nguluwi, na vinhu avi mopegwa.
“Mleche kudumba, hemwe walanguswa wa heni, lekachoni Mhaza wa hemwe wa kilanga kangugana kuwapa hemwe undewa.
Mguze vinhu vyomlinavyo, muwagalile sendi wazunwa. Miditile mihako johambe jilale, na kiwichila ng'hano kilanga, ako hambe imale. Ako wahizi hambe wahize, na mifukuzi hambe jiwifye.
Kwa vila hala ng'hano ya hegwe hoyili, ndo na nhumbula ya hegwe hoiwa.
“Miwiche goya kwa chila chinhu chilawila, na vyenje vya hemwe viwe vikwaka.
Muwe kota wanhu wali ngubeta mkulu wa hewo yahiluche kulawa kuli mnvina ya kuhesa. Loyohiluka na kudumiza lwizi, bahala walute wamchumulile.
Wosangalala ng'hatu wala wahilisi wa kilanga mkulu wa hewo loyohiluka kowafika wobeteza! Ndangukulonjelani ndikomya, ahyo mkulu kochiwopa isali mchuno, wochikalasa hali ndiya na kowakolela mijito.
Wosangalala ng'hatu wone yoye nechilo hagati ama kuzangucha kowafika wali meho.
Mvizele hino, wone yawele na ng'handa nayavizele mhela hoyokuya mhizi, nahalileka ng'handa ya heye ibenigwe na mhizi.
Na hemwe hihyo miwiche goya, mina Mwana wa Munhu kokuya saa yohamuizelele.”
Petili nakamlonjela, “Mkulu, hino nhelo awo wangutulonjela hetwe yeng'ha ama wanhu weng'ha?”
Mkulu nakedichila, “Hino yalikohi chitumagwa wa kitumbila na yawele na luhala, yula mkulu wa heye yozangumuwika mchanya mwa vitumagwa wanji, na yawape wanhu chilyo kwa mhela wuwula?
Kobweda yula chitumagwa wone mkulu wa heye loyohiluka komfika yodita ahyo.
Ndanguwalonjelani ndikomya, komuwika chitumagwa ayo yalolelaje lufufu lwake lweng'ha.
Ila ayo chitumagwa wone yazengulonga mnhumbula ya heye, ‘Mkulu wa heni hambe yahiluche hima.’ Hamba kaluka kuwatowa vitumagwa wayage, walume na wadala, na kwaluka kulya na kunwa mbaka kugala.
Mkulu wa heye kohiluka zuwa lyohejesile na kuli saa yohaizelele mpogozi. Na heye komgaza na kumuwika hamwe na wala walihela makundo.
“Yula chitumagwa yavizelele choyogana mkulu wa heye, ila nahewichile goya kudita choyaganigwe kudita na mkulu wa heye, chitumagwa ayo kotowigwa lukami.
Ila yula yalingudita galingulapa kutowigwa ne kuvizela, kotowigwa hado. Munhu yapeligwe vinhu vinji, kodaigwa vinhu vinji, na munhu yoneche yapeligwe vinhu vinji ng'hatu, kodaigwa vinhu vinji ng'hatu.
“Mbuya kubwinha chiluli isi yeng'ha, na ndangugana ndiwe mbesile katali!
Ndanawo ubatizo wa kugazigwa ndilinguganigwa kuubochela, na heni ndangugaya lukami mbaka imale!
Hino mwangijesa mbuya kigala kikala goya muisi? Nehado! Siwuyile kigala kikala goya ila kibagula.
Na tangia sambi, wanhu wa ivyazi lya wanhu wahano wochibagula, wadatu kwa weli na weli kwa wadatu.
Mhaza kochibagula na wana wa heye wasongolo, na wana wasongolo wochibagula na mhaza wa hewo. Mamo kochibagula na wahinza wa heye na mhinza kochibagula na mamo wa heye. Mkweye mdala kochibagula na mkweye, na mkwe kochibagula na mkweye mdala wa heye.”
Yesu nakawalonjela kahi wala wanhu wamemile, “Lomuyona ng'hungugu ilawila kolizinjilaga zuwa, bahala mwangulonga, ‘Nhonya yotowa,’ Na mwangukomya yangutowa.
Na lomkona mbeho ya ilawila kusini, mwangulonga, ‘Kowa na ivuche,’ Na kwanguwa hiho.
Hemwe wahadi! Mvizela kumeho kwa isi na ulanga, iwandaze hambe mvizele mina ya mihela aji?
“Lekachoni mwangulemwela kwamula mbuli zinojile za kudita?
Mina wone munhu yakulonjeleze yakugale kuli ng'handa ya kutagusila, nayali goya hegwe mihanyise na heye mung'hali mluta mnzila. Leka yaleche kukugala kuli mtagusa, na heye mtagusa kokugala kwa wamizi, na hewo wokwinjiza mchinweng'ho.
Hulawa ako kuchinweng'ho, ndangukulonjela, mbaka housinda kulavya sendi ya mwiso ya zila zoulingudaigwa.”
Mhela wuwo, wanhu wamwe nawamlonjela Yesu mbuli za wanhu wa Galilaya wala Pilato nayawakopole mihela lowali womlavila Nguluwi nhambiko.
Heye Yesu nakawalonjela, “Hino hemwe mwangijesa Wagalilaya awo wali wehile ng'hatu kusinda Wagalilaya wanji kwa vila wechona ahyo?
Nehado! Ndanguwalonjelani, wone na hemwe hamumgalamchile Nguluwi, mobagama kota wawo.
Ama mwangijesa wala wanhu kumi na wanane wala nawagwililwe na muhonyo kula Siloamu wabagama, wali wehile kusinda wanhu weng'ha wawele Yelusalemu?
Nehado! Ndanguwalonjelani, wone na hemwe hamumgalamchile Nguluwi, mobagama kota wawo.”
Hamba Yesu nakawalonjela nhelo ayi, “Munhu yumwe nayali na igodi wa mafuza ya tini kumgunda wa heye wa zabibu. Ayo munhu kaluta kubawa mafuza, ila kalifika halilelile ifuza ne limwe.
Nakamlonjela yawelengulolela mgunda, ‘Mlolele! Kwa mihela midatu ndali ndikuya ndigana mbawe mafuza kuli igodi ali, na heni sambulile ne chinhu. Uteme! Lekachoni uzenguifya misanga hela?’
Ila ayo yawelengulolela mgunda nakedichila, ‘Mkulu, uleche mhela awu yeng'ha, na heni ndiuhalile na kuuwichila midohe.
Wone ulele, goya! Ila wone haulelile, koutema.’ ”
Kuli Zuwa lya Kwesela, Yesu nayali yolangusa mli ng'handa ya kusalila.
Na aho hali na mdala yumwe nayali na chijeni chihile chimditile yawe mtamwa miyaka kumi na minane. Na heye nayali na chiduhi, na nayali yolemwela kwima yagoloche.
Yesu loyamuwene, kamchema, nakamlonjela, “Mamo, utamwa wouwelenawo wusigwa!”
Hamba Yesu kamuwichila moko yula mamo, na bahala yula mamo kagoloka, kaluka kumtogola Nguluwi.
Ila chilongozi wa ng'handa ya kusalila nakazudila lekachoni Yesu kamusa munhu utamwa Zuwa lya Kwesela. Ahyo kawalonjela wala wanhu wamemile hala, “Mwanago mazuwa sita ga kukola mijito. Kuli mazuwa ago, muye musilwe matamwa genu, ila mleche kuya kuli Zuwa lya Kwesela.”
Ahyo Mkulu nakamwidichila, “Hemwe wahadi! Hino kuna munhu yoneche kuli hemwe hali dohola isenga ama idogowi lya heye kulawa mli ng'handa yaligale kunwa mazi kuli Zuwa lya Kwesela?
Lelo hano kabaho mhinza wa Abulahamu, na heye nakawohigwa na Limazoga miyaka kumi na nane. Lelo hainojile kumdoholela kuli Zuwa lya Kwesela?”
Yesu loyasindile kulonga ago, wala weng'ha wamwihile wazangona soni, ila wanhu nawasangalala kwa vinduzanduza vyoyaditile Yesu.
Yesu nakauza, “Hambi Undewa wa Nguluwi wa ndaze? Hambi ndiuhwane na choni?
Lufanda kota nyhadikwa ndodo kusinda zeng'ha ilinguchemigwa haladali, yaiholile munhu na kuinyala mumgunda wa heye. Nyhadikwa ayo yota, hamba liwa igodi ikulu mbaka videje vya kuulanga vizenga vimvulila mli nhagala zake.”
Kahi Yesu nakauza, “Hambi Undewa wa Nguluwi ndiuhwanize na choni?
Ufanda kota nungo yaiholile mamo yumwe na kahanza na utimbo vijemo vidatu, mbaka utimbo weng'ha ufuluma.”
Yesu nakalutilila na majendo kuluta Yelusalemu. Loyali mzila, nakakolela kuli miji na vijiji aku yowalangusa wanhu.
Munhu yumwe kamuuza, “Mkulu, hambi wanhu woloholigwa wado?” Yesu nakawedichila,
“Mikangaze kukolela kuli lwizi luzisili, mina ndangukulonjelani, wanhu wenji wojeza kwinjila, ila howoweza.
Mihela jokuya nayali na ng'handa kokwima na kuhinda lwizi, namwe mokwima kunze na kudumiza lwizi mlonga, ‘Mkulu, tuchumulile lwizi.’ Ila heye kowalonjela, ‘Siwazelele hemwe na komlawile kohi’
Namwe molonga, ‘Tudile na kunwa hamwe na hegwe, na hegwe nakulangusaga muli muji wa hetwe.’
Ila heye kolonga kahi, ‘Sivizelele hemwe mlawa kohi. Muche kumwando kwa heni, hemwe mweng'ha mlingudita gehile!’
Aho ndo homuwa mlila na kujejeda mizino, aho momona Abulahamu na Isaka na Yakubu, na waloli weng'ha wawele hali Undewa wa Nguluwi, na hemwe mtozigwa kunze!
Wanhu wokuya kulawa kolilawilaga isanya na kula kolizinjilaga isanya, kulawa kasikazini na kusini, wochikala na kulya hali Undewa wa Nguluwi.
Ena, wala wawele wa mwiso wowa wa mwaluko, na wala wawele wa mwaluko wowa wa mwiso.”
Mihela jijo Mafalisayo wamwe nawamlutila Yesu, wamlonjela, “Uche hano ulute honhu hanji, lekachoni Helodi kangugana yakukopole.”
Yesu nakawalonjela, “Mlute mkalilonjele alyo libwa lya kisolo ahi, ‘Lehano na mitondo ndanguwinga vijeni na kuwosela wanhu matamwa, haucha ndosinda mijito ja heni.’
Ahyo ingana lehano na mitondo na haucha, ndokwinulila majendo, lekachoni haiwa goya mloli wa Nguluwi yakopoligwe hanze ha Yelusalemu.
“Yelusalemu! Gwa Yelusalemu! Kwanguwakopola waloli na kuwatowa kwa maganga wala watumigwe kwa hegwe. Lwa kalinga njeza kuwakungajiza wana wa hegwe kwa heni kota vila ng'huku vyoilingukungajiza vinziya vya heye hasi hali mbawa za heye, ila hegwe nahuviganile!
Mlole! Mlechelwa ng'handa ya hemwe! Na heni ndangukulonjelani ndikomya, hammbona kahi mbaka homlonga, ‘Yatambichizwe ayo yalinguya kwa itagwa lya Mkulu.’ ”
Zuwa limwe lya kwesela, Yesu nakaluta kulya ndiya ha kaye ha mkulu yumwe wa Mafalisayo. Wanhu wali aho wali womlola kwa kumtegela.
Munhu yumwe yoyali na safula nakamlutila Yesu.
Yesu nakawauza walangusa wa Malajizo na Mafalisayo, “Hino Malajizo ga hetwe gangutukundiza hetwe kumusila munhu utamwa Zuwa lya Kwesela ama hebu?”
Ila hewo wekala wenyamalile. Yesu kamibata ayo mtamwa, kamusila utamwa, nakamlonjela yalute.
Hamba kawalonjela, “Yali kohi hemwe mwanage ama isenga lya heye wone linjile hali izimbo Zuwa lya Kwesela halikulilavya bahala?”
Ila hewo walemwela kwidichila chinhu.
Yesu loyawawene wala walalikwe vowali wohagula kikala kuli vigoda vya kumwando, nakawalonjela weng'ha kwa nhelo ayi;
“Wone munhu yakulaliche kuli mnvina ya kuhola, uleche kikalisa kuli vigoda vya kumwando. Leka munhu yunji mkulu kusinda hegwe koweza kuya,
na munhu yawalaliche weng'ha kokuwiyila na kukulonjela, ‘Mlechele ayu honhu aha.’ Baho kodeula na kuluta kikala kuli vigoda vya kumbele.
Ila wone hegwe uchemigwe honhu, kekale kumbele, leka munhu yula yakulaliche loyokuyila, yakulonjele, ‘Goloko, winuche uye wikale kuno kuli na vigoda vya kumwando,’ baho kotogoligwa hali wanhu weng'ha wekalise hamwe na hegwe.
Kwa vila munhu yoneche yochikwiniza, koduliswa, na munhu yoneche yawele liholile kokwinizwa.”
Hamba Yesu nakamlonjela yula yamlaliche, “Wone kowalalika wanhu kulya chilyo cha nemisi ama cha nechilo, uleche kuwalalika womiganaga ama wang'holozo ama wanhu wa habehi na haluga hako wali na lufufu. Kwa vila wone udite ahyo, hewo nawo wokulalika hakaye hawo, na ahyo wokuhilulila chila chouwaditile.
Ila wone loudita mnvina, walaliche wali wazunwa na waziliche lukuli na wali chete na wali hambe walole
na hegwe kowa utambichizwe na Nguluwi. Mina wawo wali hela chinhu cha kukuhilusila. Nguluwi kokuhilusila kuli zuwa wanhu wanojile howozilipuligwa.”
Yumwe wa wala wanhu wekalise hamwe na Yesu loyahuliche ago, nakamlonjela, “Kabweda munhu yozangulya ndiya mu Undewa wa Nguluwi.”
Yesu nakamlonjela, “Munhu yumwe nakadita mnvina ng'hulu kawalalika wanhu wenji,
Mhela wa kulya loufichile, nakamlonjela chitumagwa wa heye yakawalonjele walalikwe, ‘Muye, chila chinhu cha goya’
Ila weng'ha nawalema, chila munhu nayali na mbuli ya kukola. Munhu wa mwaluko nakamlonjela yula chitumagwa, ‘Ngula mgunda, ahyo ndangugana ndikaulole. Ndangulanda undeche.’
Munhu yunji nakalonga, ‘Ngula misenga kumi ja kulimila kumgunda, lelo ndamnzila ndute ndikajijeze. Ndangulanda undeche.’
Yunji nakalonga, ‘Ndimhola mdala, ahyo ndolemwela kuya.’
“Ayo chitumagwa kahiluka, nakamlonjela mkulu wa heye ayo mbuli. Na heye loyahuliche ago, kazudila, nakamlonjela yula chitumagwa, ‘Lute himahima nzila ng'hulu na nzila ndodo za miji, ukawalonjele wanhu wali wazunwa, na waziliche lukuli, na wohambe walole, na wali chete woye.’
Hamba yula chitumagwa nakalonga, ‘Mkulu, ago goulajize mina gakoligwa, ila na sambi honhu hanji hang'hali hanamema.’
Yula mkulu nakamlonjela chitumagwa wa heye, ‘Lute kuli nzila ng'hulu na mbakane uwakole wanhu lupichi woye wenjile leka ng'handa ya heni imeme.
Mina ndangukulonjelani, haduhu ne yumwe kuli wala walalichigwe yolya chilyo kuli mnvina ya heni!’ ”
Aho wanhu wenji lowali womuwinza Yesu, Yesu nakawagalamchila, kawalonjela,
“Munhu yoneche howa mlanguswa wa heni, wone hanganile heni ng'hatu kusinda vyoyalinguwagana mhaza wa heye na mamo wa heye na mdala wa heye na wanage na wang'holoze na walumbuze.
Munhu yoneche wone hapapile msalaba wa heye na kumbinza, kolemwela kuwa mlanguswa wa heni.
“Mina yalikohi munhu yumwe homuli, wone yagane kuzenga ilingo, holongola kikalisa yalole kana vinhu vikwila kugomanjiza mijito ya heye?
Kwa vila wone kokwaluka kubawa msisi, na wone yalemwele kugomanjiza, wanhu womseka.
Hamba wolonga, ‘Munhu ayu nakaluka kuzenga, ila kalemwela kugomanjiza mijito ya heye!’
“Ama mndewa wachi wone yagane kuza kitowa na mndewa yunji, hochikalisa hasi tandi yejese kokwimilila kwa wamizi wa heye elufu kumi kitowa na mndewa nayali na wamizi elufu makumi meli?
Wone yone hokwimilila, kowalonjela vitumagwa wa heye wakamdedeze yula mndewa yang'hali kutali waleche kitowa wekale goya.
Na hemwe namwe hihyo, wone munhu halechile chila chinhu choyali nacho howeza kuwa mlanguswa wa heni.
“Mwino unona, ila wone uwe haunonile, wonojezwa na choni mbaka uwe unonile kahi?
Hambe ikole ne chinhu kuwika kuli mgunda wala kuhanza na midohe, wanhu woitaga kunze. Yali na makutu ga kuhulichizila, nayahuliche!”
Zuwa limwe wakongoza kodi na wanhu wenji wawelengudita gehile nawaluta kumuhulichiza Yesu.
Mafalisayo na walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa wazakung'ung'uta, “Mlole munhu ayu! Kanguwabochela wadita gehile, kahi kangulya na hewo!”
Yesu nakawalonjela nhelo ayi.
“Wone, munhu yawele na ming'holo miya imwe, wone yone limwe lyajilile, kodita choni? Kojileka jila makumi tisa na tisa mviwala, na kanguluta kupala lila lyajilile mbaka yalyone.
Na wone yalyone, kosangalala na kolipika mmayega,
na kumuhilika haluga. Hamba kanguwachema wali ngigana na wanhu wa habehi na heye na kuwalonjela, ‘Tusangalale hamwe, kwa vila ndilyona lila ling'holo lyangu nalyajilile.’
Kahi ndangukulonjelani, kowa na kusangalala ng'hatu kilanga kwa mdita gehile yumwe kumgalamchila Nguluwi, kusinda wanhu makumi tisa na tisa watanganiche wohambe wagane woselwe gehile.
“Ama mwangona ndaze? Mdala yumwe nayali na migwala kumi, wone yajilize imwe, kangudita choni? Kobwinha chenje, kofajila ng'handa na kupala mholemhole mbaka yayone.
Wone yayone, kanguwachema weganaga na wanhu wa habehi na heye, yolonga, ‘Msangalale hamwe na heni, kwa vila ndilyona ligwala lya heni nalyajilile’
Hihyo ndangukulonjelani, wahilisi wa kilanga wa Nguluwi wosangalala kwa nayali na gehile yumwe yalingumgalamchila Nguluwi.”
Yesu nakalutilila kuwalonjela, “Kwali na munhu yumwe nayali na wana weli wasongolo.
Yula mdodo nakamlonjela mhaza wa heye, ‘Mhaza, nyipe uhalizi wa vinhu vya heni sambi.’ Ahyo mhaza yula kawagawila lufufu lwa heye lweng'ha wala wana weli.
Logakolile mazuwa mado, yula mdodo munhu kaguza vinhu vyeng'ha vyoyahalizwe na mhaza wa heye, hamba koka na kuluta isi ya kutali. Ako nakawifyanga sendi za heye chakachaka.
Loyasindile kidila chila chinhu, nailawila nzala ng'hulu isi ila, na heye kaluka kugaya.
Ahyo nakaluta kukola mijito kwa munhu yumwe nayali mwenyeng'haye wa isi ila, na heye kamuhilika kuli mgunda wa heye yawe yohombela migubi.
Kazangugana kulya chilyo jiwele ngulya migubi, ila haduhu munhu yampele.
Nyhala lozaluche kuhiluka, nakelonjelela, ‘Kula kuluga kwa mhaza wa heni kuna wakola mijito wenji wawele kulya na kulechelela. Iwa ndaze heni hano ndagubagama kwa nzala?
Ndokuka na kuluta kwa mhaza wa heni ndimlonjele kota, Mhaza, ndita gehile kwa hegwe, na ndita gehile kilanga na kwa hegwe Nguluwi.
Hambe nganigwe kuchemwa mwana wa hegwe kahi, ndite kota yumwe wa vitumagwa wa hegwe.’
Ahyo keyinula kaluta kwa mhaza wa heye. “Ila loyali yang'hali kutali, mhaza wa heye kamona. Kamonela isungu, kambilimila, kamlamsa kwa kumkumbatiza na kumnonela.
Yula mwana nakamlonjela, ‘Mhaza, mbifya kilanga na kwa hegwe Nguluwi na ndita gehile kwa hegwe. Hambe nganigwe kuchemigwa nda mwana wa hegwe.’
Ila mhaza wa heye nakawalonjela vitumagwa, ‘Himahima! Migale nguwo inojile mumvalize. Mvicheni pete mchidole cha heye na makwamba mmagulu ga heye!
Hamba mkome lila lisenga ilogota lihatile, tulye na tudite mnvina ng'hangala!
Kwa vila ayu mwana wa heni nayali yabagame ila lelo kazilipuka, nakajilila ila lelo koneka’ Ahyo waluka kudita mnvina.
“Mvina voyali ilutilila, yula mkulugwe nayali kumgunda. Loyali yohiluka na kuwa behi na haluga, kahulika nzimbo na wanhu wovina.
Kamchema chitumagwa yumwe, kamuuza, ‘Hana choni?’
Yula chitumagwa nakamlonjela, ‘Mng'holozako kahiluka haluga, na mhaza wa hegwe kakoma isenga ilogota lihatile loyamuwene yawele mkomu.’
“Ayo msongolo mkulu kazudila ng'hatu, kalema kwinjila mng'handa. Mhaza wa heye kalawa kunze na kumdedeza yenjile mng'handa.
Ila heye nakedichila, ‘Wijese, mihela jeng'ha heni nandikukolela mijito kota chitumagwa, na silemile kuhulichiza ilajizo lya hegwe ne zuwa limwe. Kumha choni? Humhele ne kamhene kamwe kadodo ndite mnvina na wotiganaga!
Ila ayu mwanago yawifile vinhu vya hegwe chakachaka na wang'hondwa loyoile kumchinjila isenga ilogota lihatile!’
Mhaza wa heye nakamwidichila, ‘Gomwana wa heni, mihela jeng'ha wali wikale na heni, na chila chinhu chondali nacho nachali cha hegwe.
Ila itugana tudite mnvina kwa vila ayu mng'holozako nayali yabagame, lelo kamkomu, nayali yajilile lelo koneka.’ ”
Yesu nakawalangusa wala walanguswa, “Muhu yumwe nayali na lufufu, nayali na mkola mijito. Wanhu nawamlonjela ayu mkola mijito wa hegwe kangulya chaka vinhu vya yula yamuwichile,
Yula nayali na lufufu kamchema nakamlonjela, ‘Mbuli zachi za hegwe zondili nguhilika? Undajile choukolele lufufu lwa heni? Mina hegwe huza nguwa chitumagwa kahi.’
Yula chitumagwa kejesa, Ayu mkulu kangumbusa kuli kumwandichila, ndodita ndaze kuluta kumgunda siweza, kuluta kulanda kota wali hela chinhu, ndangona soni.
Ndivizela lya kudita, aho hoyombinga wanhu waze ngunyhema kowekalaga.
“Yolawa kawachema weng'ha walinguganigwa na yula nayali yowandichila yumweyumwe, nakamlonjela yalongole, ‘Zilinga uli ngudaigwa mkulu wa heni?’
Heye nakedichila mibiga ja kutelechela mafuta miya na imwe ga mzeituni. ‘Yula nayandikaga nakamlonjela. Hole ai iwele ngulajila voili ngudaigwa, kalise himahima wandiche hamsini.’
Kahi kamuuza munhu yunji yalingudaigwa, ‘Hegwe kangukudai zilinga?’ Heye nakedichila migunila miya ja uhemba. ‘Hole ayi ilingulajila voulingudaigwa, wandiche samanini.’
“Ila yula mkulu kamtogola ayo yandikaga voyali wakitumbila nayali yakolile luhala, mina wanhu wa ayi isi wana luhala na mbuli za hewo zihile kusinda wanhu wa lumuli.”
Heye Yesu kazangulonga, “Heni ndangukulonjelani migane na wanhu kulawa kuli lufufu lwihile lwa isi, lozimala mobocheligwa na hewo, mozangikala mazuwa gose ne kuduma.
Munhu yoneche yalinguganigwa muli mbuli ndodo. Kowa yaganigwe muli mbuli ng'hangala. Ila munhu halingukundigwa kuli mbuli ndodo, howeza kukundigwa kuli mbuli ng'hulu.
Wone hemwe wanhu wohambe wakukundeni kuli lufufu lwihile lwa amu muisi, munhu yachi yokupani lufufu lwa kukomya?
Na wone hambe mkundigwe kuli lufufu haluwele lwa hemwe, munhu yachi yokupani lufufu luzeleche?
“Haduhu chitumagwa yokola mijio kwa wakulu weli, kwa vila ama komzudila yumwe na kumgana yunji, ama kochilongozaga na yula yumwe na kumbeza ayo yunji. Homfugamila Nguluwi na lufufu.”
Ila Mafalisayo lowahuliche ago geng'ha, ila hewo wali wogana lukami lufufu, wambeza Yesu.
Aho nakawalojela, “Hemwe mwangilola mnoga hali wanhu, ila Nguluwi kavizela mnhumbula ya hemwe. Mina chila chilingoneka chikulu hali wanhu, Nguluwi kochona acho chiha.
“Mizilo na gala gandichigwe na waloli gali mbaka mihela ja Yohani Mbatiza. Kulawa aho Mbuli Inojile ya Undewa wa Nguluwi wangutagusigwa, na chila munhu kangwinjila kwa ludali.
Ila isi yeng'ha na kilanga vyokusigwa chimdawalo hela kusinda helufi imwe ya malajizo gandichigwe kusigwa.
“Yoneche yamleche mchewake na kuhola yunji, mng'hondwa, na yoneche nayali kumhola mdala yalechigwe mng'hondwa.
“Kwali na munhu yumwe nayali na lufufu, nayali yovala mivalo ja sendi nyinji ng'hatu na kitani chinojile na kudita mnvina chila yokwinuka.
Kahi kwali na munhu yumwe nayali nguchemigwa Lasalo, yula nayali na vilonda lukuli lweng'ha nayali womigala mli lwizi lwa yula nayali na lufufu.
Nakaganaga yalye usanyangwa uwele ngulagala kulawa mli mchisanya ya yula nayali na lufufu, na ganji, mibwa jali jikuya jimyanga vilonda vya heye!
“Lelo yula munhu nayali hela chinhu kaholigwa na Nguluwi, mhilisi wa kilanga nakamhola, kekala habehi na Abulahamu na yula nayali na lufufu kaga, nakatiligwa.
Na yula nayali na lufufu yawele yogazigwa kula kuli isi ya wabagame, kenula meho ga heye, kamona Abulahamu kwa kutali na Lasalo yekale hafungo.
Hamba kachema kwa lizi, ‘Mhaza Abulahamu, mbonele isungu, mlonjele Lasalo yadolize chidole cha heye mli mazi yahoze umyango wa heni mina ndangugazigwa kuno kuli chiluli.’
“Ila Abulahamu nakedichila, ‘Kumbuche mwanangu hegwe na kupegwa ganojile lowali uchikala muisi, na Lasalo nakabochela gehile. Lelo heye kanguhozigwa na hegwe kwangugazigwa.
Ila na ago geng'ha, hotuli hetwe na komli hemwe hawichigwa ikulubila ikulu, ili wawele ngugana kuya kumuli kulawa kuno walemwele, na wawele komuli walemwele kuya kuno kotuli.’
Ayo nayali na lufufu nakalonga, ‘Lelo mhaza Abulahamu ndangukulanda umlajize yalute kaye kuli ng'handa ya mhaza wa heni.
Mina ndina wang'holozangu wahano yalute yawakanye waleche kuya kuno kuli kugazigwa.’
“Ila Abulahamu nakamlonjela, ‘Wang'holozo wanago Maandiko Matakatifu ga Musa na waloli wanji wa Nguluwi wowalonjela ago, waleche wawahulichize hewo chowolonga.’
Ila heye nakalonga, ‘Hebu mhaza Abulahamu! Ila wone munhu yazilipuche kulawa wanhu wajile na kuwalutila, womgalamchila Nguluwi.’
Heye Abulahamu nakalonga, ‘Wone hambe wagasome Gandichigwe ga Musa na waloli wanji wa Nguluwi, howojesa hebu! Wone yalute yazilipuche kulawa wanhu wabagame!.’ ”
Hamba Yesu nakawalonjela wala walanguswa wa heye, “Havileka kulawila vinhu vilingujeza wanhu kudita gehile, ila kochona yula yojeza.
Naigana yafunjigwe iganga likulu lya lwala msingo na kutozigwa mli mlwanda, kuleka heye kumwambuza munhu yumwe wa awa wadodo kuwifya.
Milolele! Wone mng'holozo yakuditile gehile mdeuze, wone yakunde kumgalamchila Nguluwi, yamgalachile.
Kahila wone yakuzudize mala saba kwa zuwa limwe na yohiluchila kouli yolonga, ‘Ndimgalamchila Nguluwi,’ goya yakundile.”
Wala watumigwa nawamlonjela, “Mkulu tonjezele makundo.”
Heye mkulu nakawedichila, Wone makundo ga hemwe na gawe mado kota nyhule ndodo ya haladali, mwahajezile kulilonjela ali igodi lya Mfolosadi ng'holeche ukenjile mli lwanda, nawo wawahuliche.
“Tulonje hemwe munhu yumwe kana chitumagwa nayali ngukola mijto ya kumgunda ama kangudima ming'holo lelo yohiluka kulawa kumgunda, komlonjela ayo chitumagwa himahima uye ulye ndiya?
Hebu! Komlonjela nhelechele ndiya wikale ung'holela mijito mbaka londisinda kulya na kunwa, ndo nagwe ulye.
Homnonela ayo mpogozi kwa vila nakakola goyalonjelwe.
Na hemwe namwe wone mdite gomlonjelwe, mlonje, ‘Hetwe wapogozi wohambe tupegwe chinhu, tukola gala gotulonjelwe tukole hela.’ ”
Yesu loyali yojenda kuza Yelusalemu nakakola mmbaka mwa Samaliya na Galilaya.
Loyali yokwinjila mli chijiji chimwe, naketing'ha na wanhu kumi wali na uswema, wemile kutali.
Wachemeleza lizi wolonga, “Yesu mlangusa tonele isungu!”
Loyawawene nakawalonjela, “Mlute mkelajile kwa watambika.” Lowaliwoluta, nawona kuhovujigwa.
Myawo yumwe yonile nakoselwa mayamwa, kahiluka kamtogola Nguluwi kwa lizi ing'hangala.
Ketoza kumwando kuli magulu ga Yesu kuno yomnonela. Ayo nayali Msamalia.
Aho Yesu nakalonga, “Nandisile matamwa mwali kumi? Wala tisa wakohi?
Haduhuli yunji yahiluche kumtogola Nguluwi ila ayu mjenzi yaliyeng'ha?”
Yesu nakamlonjela yula munhu, “Winuche, ulute, makundo gako gakulohola.”
Mhela umwe Mafalisayo nawamuuza Yesu, “Undewa wa Nguluwi wokuya nili?” Heye nakawalonjela, “Undewa wa Nguluwi haukuya ukoneka.
Kahi haduhu munhu yolonga, wahano, ama wahala. Lelo Undewa wa Nguluwi wa mgati mwenu.”
Hamba kawalonjela walanguswa, “Mazuwa ganguya moza ngugana kulola zuwa limwe lya mwana wa munhu, ila hamyona.
Na wanhu wokulonjelani, ‘Mlole ka hala!’ Ama ‘Mlole ka hano!’ Ila hemwe mleche kulawa kahi mleche kuwawinza.
Mina kota hila lumwemwesa lwa limlungu ne kulonga lumwesa kilanga nzingo imwe mbaka iyage, ndo voiwa zuwa alyo Mwana wa Munhu loyokuya.
Ila ago gang'hali, kogazigwa lukami na kulemigwa na lulelo alu.
Kota vyonaiwele mhela wa Nuhu ndo vyoiwa hoyokuya Mwana wa Munhu.
Wanhu nawalyaga na kunwa wohola na kuholeka mbaka mhela ula Nuhu loyenjile mli itumbwi ling'hangala. Mazi metemete logalawile na kuwakopola weng'ha.
Yowa kota vyoilawile mhela wa Loti. Wanhu wazangulya na kunwa, kugula na kuguza, kunyala nyhadikwa na kuzenga.
Ila zuwa Loti loyochile sodoma, maganga ga chiluli nagalawila gazangutowa kota nhonya kulawa kilanga na kuwakopola weng'ha.
Ndo vyoiwa zuwa alyo Mwana wa Munhu loyogubuligwa.
“Zuwa alyo, wone munhu yawele chinduwiko mwa ng'handa ya heye, yaleche kudulika yahole vinhu vya heye vili mng'handa nayali kumgunda yaleche kuhiluka koyalawile.
Mkumbucheni mchewake Loti.
Munhu yalingugana kululohola lukuli lwa heye kolwajiliza, na munhu yolwajiliza kolulohola.
Ndangukulonjelani, zuwa alyo wanhu weli wowa wawasile hamihe, yumwe koholigwa na yunji kolechigwa.
Wadala weli wowa wotwanga ndiya hamwe. Yumwe koholigwa na yunji kolechigwa.”
Wanhu weli wowa kumgunda, yumwe koholigwa na yunji kolechigwa.
Wamuuza kohi Mkulu? Kawalonjela, “Hawele na mtufi, ndo hojimema mikungule.”
Hamba Yesu nakawasimila walanguswa wa heye nhelo ayi, imgana munhu yaze kumlanda Nguluwi ne kugozola.
Nakalonga, “Kuli honhu hamwe kwali na mtagusa yumwe nayali yomuwinza Nguluwi, kahi nahamjesaga ne munhu.
Na honhu aho, kwali na mamo yumwe yalechelelwe, nakamlutilaga ayo mtagusa yomlanda yamtagusile goya kulawa kwa munhu nayali ngumhwihilwa.
Mihela minji ayo mtagusa nahaganaga kumlewela ayo mamo, ila mwiso kazangulonga, ‘Wone hambe ndimjese Nguluwi na wanhu,
Ila ayu mdala kanguya yongaza, ndomleweleza wone siditile ahyo kozanguya hano mwiso konhosa lukami.’ ”
Mkulu nakawalonjela, “Muhulika vyoyalonjile ayo mtagusa yehile.
Lelo Nguluwi howalewela wala yawahagule, wala wali ngulanda nemisi na nechilo? Koleka kuwahulichiza?
Ndangukulonjela kowalewela himahima. Kahi, kowa kuduhu makundo amu muisi mhela Mwana wa Munhu loyokuya?”
Hamba Yesu nakawalonjela kahi nhelo kota hino, wala wanhu nawewonaga watanganika na kuwabeza wayawo wanji.
“Nakalonga, Wanhu weli nawaluta mluga lwa ng'handa ya Nguluwi kuza kulanda Nguluwi, yumwe Mfalisayo, na yunji mkongoza kodi.
“Ayo Mfalisayo kema hafungo na kumlanda Nguluwi mnhumbula, ‘Gwa Nguluwi, malumbo, heni siwele kota wala wawele wadesi, wawele wabuhu na wang'hondwa na walinguboka. Malumbo, heni siwele kota ayu mkongoza sendi.
Ndangwesela kulya mazuwa meli, ndangulavya imwe ya kumi ya lufufu londiwele kupegwa.’
“Ila yula mkongoza sendi, nayali yemile kwa kutali henule ne meho gake kilanga, ila nakebata chipambaga kuno yesinzile kulajila kana masinzo, kalonga, ‘Gwa Nguluwi mbonele isungu heni ndiwele na gehile!’
Ndangukulonjelani,” “Ayu mkongoza sendi kahiluka kaye yawele yakundigwe na Nguluwi kusinda yula Mfalisayo. Mina, chila yalingikwiniza koduliswa, na yoneche yawele liholile, kokwinizwa.”
Wanhu wamigalila Yesu wana wadodo yawawichile moko. Walanguswa wawawene nawawang'hanuchila.
Ila Yesu nakawachema hoyali yolonga, “Muwaleche awo wana wadodo woye kwa heni, mleche kuwalemeza, mina Undewa wa Nguluwi wanguwagana wanhu kota awa.
Ndanguwalonjelani ndikomya ng'hatu, munhu yohambe youbochele Undewa wa Nguluwi kota mwana mdodo, hokwinjila kuli undewa awo.”
Mkulu yumwe wa Wayahudi nakamuuza Yesu, “Mlangusa yanojile, ndite ndaze leka mhegwe ukomu wa mazuwa gose ne kuduma?”
Yesu nakamuuza, “Lekachoni kwangundonjela noga? Haduhu munhu yanojile ila yumwe, Nguluwi yaliyeng'ha.
Kujizela mizilo, ‘Uleche ung'hondwa, uleche kukopola, uleche kuhiza, uleche kumwimilila munhu udesi, uwahulichize mhaza na mayako.’ ”
Heye nakalonga, “Ago geng'ha ndigabata kulawila londali msongolo.”
Yesu loyahuche ago nakamlonjela, “Kwanguganigwa kudita chinhu chimwe, uguze chila chinhu, wagawile wanzunwa, na hegwe kowa na ng'hano kilanga, hamba uye umbinze.”
Ila ayo munhu loyahuliche ago, yawele na masinzo, kwa vila, nayali na lufufu lwinji.
Yesu loyamuwene kangugana ahyo, nakalonga, “Kota voiwa nongwa kwa wali na lufufu, wolemwela kwinjila kuli Undewa wa Nguluwi!
Ahi ndo yowa ubewe kwa Ngamiya lyoweza kukola mlinanga ya chihomo kusinda nayali na lufufu kwinjila kuli Undewa wa Nguluwi.”
Wala wanhu wahuliche ago, nawalonga, “Yalikohi yoloholigwa?”
Yesu kawalonjela, “Gali ngulemweligwa kwa wanhu. Kwa Nguluwi zoditikwa.”
Heye Petili nakamuuza, “Na hetwe ndaze? Tuleka geng'ha natukuwinza!”
Yesu nakawalomjela, ndangukulonjelani ndikomya, “Munhu yalechile ng'handa ama mdala ama mkulugwe ama wamlelile na wana kwa Undewa wa Nguluwi,
Kobochela menji ng'hatu mhela awu wa sambi, na mhela ukuya ukomu wa mazuwa gose ne kuduma.”
Yesu nakawahola hafungo wala walanguswa, kawalonjela, “Mhulichize! Twanguluta Yelusalemu na ako chila chinhu chandikwe na waloli gomlapa Mwana wa Munhu, gowa gakoligwe.
Mina kowichigwa mmoko mwa wanhu hawawele Wayahudi, na hewo womditila gehile na kummizila mite.
Womtowa na ng'hobwa, womkopola, ila zuwa lya kadatu kulawa loyabagame, kozilipuka.”
Ila hewo nahawavizelele mbuli ne imwe, nawavisigwa ulonzi awo, nahawavizelele choni chilingulonjigwa.
Mhela Yesu loyali habehi kwinjila Yeliko, kwali na munhu yumwe hambe yalole yekalise mnzila yolanda,
Yahuliche wanhu wokola kauza, “Hana choni?”
Wamlonjela, “Yesu wa Nasaleti kangukola hano.”
Heye nakachemeleza lizi yolonga, “Yesu Mwana wa Daudi, umbonele isungu!”
Kwangugana ndikuditile ndaze? Wala wanhu walongole wamdeuza wamlonjela nyamalile ila heye hahuliche kaza nguchemeleza lizi, “Mwana wa Daudi, umbonele isungu.”
Yesu kema kawalonjela wamigale hoyali. Yula munhu yohambe yalole loyoile habehi, Yesu nakamuuza,
“Kwangugana ndikuditile choni?” Nakedichila, “Mkulu ndangulanda ndizengulola kahi.”
Yesu nakamlonjela, “Ulole! Makundo ga hegwe gakulohola.”
Bahala yula yawele yohambe yalole kazangulola. Kamuwinza Yesu kuno yomtogola Nguluwi. Wala wanhu weng'ha lowawene ago, wamtogola Nguluwi.
Yesu nakenjila mujini Yeliko, loyali yokola mnzila za honhu aho.
Kalawila munhu yumwe, itagwa lyake Sakayo. Ayo nayali chilongozi wa wakongoza sendi na kahila nayali munhu nayali na lufufu.
Kagana kulola Yesu munhu wachi, lelo wanhu wali wenji lukami, ila heye nayali chifude na kalemwela kumona.
Ahyo! Nakabilima kumwando, kakwina mchanya mli ikuyu leka wamone Yesu, mina nayali yokolela aho.
Yesu loyafichile honhu hala, nakalola mchanya nakamlonjela, “Sakayo, uduliche hasi himahima, mana lelo hano ndogana nsinde haluga hako.”
Sakayo kedulika himahima, kambochela yasangalale.
Wanhu weng'ha lowawene ago, waluka kulonga longa, “Kaluta kikala na munhu yawele na gehile.”
Ila Sakayo kenuka nakamlonjela Yesu, “Hulichize Mkulu! Heni ndowapa wali hela vinhu nusu ya vinhu vya heni na wone ndimlande munhu chinhu, ndomhilusila kota acho mala zine.”
Yesu nakamlonjela, “Lehano ulohozi uya ng'handa ayi, mina ayo na heye mwana wa lukolo lwa Abulahamu.
Mina Mwana wa Munhu koya kupala na kulohola wajilile.”
Mhela wanhu lowang'hali wohulichiza ago, Yesu nakawalangusa kwa nhelo yolonga, aho yalibehi na Yelusalemu, na wanhu wavizela mhela wuwu, Undewa wa Nguluwi wokwiza.
Aho nakawalonjela, “Kwali na munhu yumwe yatanganiche na kadita majendo kuluta isi ya kutali yakabochele undewa, hamba yahiluche.
Yang'hali kuka kawachema wala watumagwa kumi, kampa chila munhu sendi zihejile msahala wa myezi jidatu na kuwalonjela, ‘Mgulile vinhu mzenguguza mbaka londihiluka.’
Ila wanhu wanji nawamwihilwa na wawalajiza watumagwa walute wakalonje! ‘Tumlema ayu yaleche kuwa mndewa wa hetwe.’
“Aho munhu loyapeligwe undewa nakahiluka, bahala kalonga wala watumagwa wapeligwe sendi wachemigwe. Yogana yavizele chila munhu zilela zilinga.
Yula yalongoligwe kupegwa kalawila kalonga, ‘Mkulu zoumhele, ndizonjeza mala kumi.’
Heye nakamlonjela, ‘Goya,’ Hegwe kwa chitumagwa unojile! Kunoga kuli mbuli ndodo, kowa ulongoza miji kumi!,
Chitumagwa wa keli koya, nakalonga, ‘Mkulu, nguza zonjezeka mala zihano ya zila zoumhle!’
Heye nakamlonjela, ‘Nagwe kowa mkulu wa miji jihano.’
“Chitumagwa yunji koya, kalonga, ‘Mkulu, uhole sendi zako, nandizivisa goya mchibende,
nandumba hegwe kwa munhu yang'ang'ale, kwangusa chohuwichile, na kubeta cho hunyalile.’
Heye nakamlonjela, ‘Vyoulonjile ahyo ndokutagusa kwa mlomo wa hegwe, hegwe kwa chitumagwa wihile! Nakuvizela heni nda munhu yang'ang'ale, ndangubeta vyosinyalile.’
Lekachoni huwichile sendi kuli wanhu walingonjeza londikuya nyhole na zila zonjezeche?
“Aho nakawalonjela wala wali hala, ‘Msukuleni alyo igwala limwe, na mumhe yula yawele na zila zonjezeche mala kumi.’
Hewo anwamlonjela, ‘Ila Mkulu heye kanazo zonjezeche mala kumi!’
‘Heye nakawalonjela,’ ‘Chila yawele na chinhu, kokonjezelwa chiyage, ila yula yawele hela chinhu, chila chidodo choyawele nacho, choholigwa.
Na sambi, wala wohambe wagane ndiwe mndewa wa hewo, muwagale aha, muwakopole nani ndilola.’ ”
Yesu nakalonga ago, yolawa nakalongola kumwando kuza Yelusalemu.
Hoyali habehi na Betifage na Betaniya, behi na chidunda cha Mizeituni, nakawalajiza walanguswa wa heye weli.
Nakawalonjela, “Mlute hali chijiji chiwele kumwando kwa hemwe. Lomuwa mukwinjila mchijiji, molifika mwana idogowi liwohigwe halina kwinigwa na munhu, mdohole mligale hano.
Wone munhu yawauze, lekachoni mlingulidohola, mlonje ‘Mkulu kangumgana.’ ”
Wolawa waluta wafika kota Yesu voyawalonjele.
Lowali wolidohola lila lidogowi, hewo wawauza, “Lekachoni mlingulidohola ali idogowi?”
Hewo nawawalonjela, “Mkulu kangumgana.”
Wolawa waligala lila idogowi kwa Yesu. Wolawawahola nguwo za hewo watambalika hamgongo mwa idogowi, wamkwiniza Yesu mchanya wa alyo idogowi.
Yesu kazanguluta yawele mchanya mli idogowi. Na wanhu nawazanza nguwo za hewo mbalabala.
Loyali behi na Yelusalemu, hali mduliko wa chidunda cha Mizeituni, walanguswa wa heye na wanhu wenji wazakwimba na kumtogola Nguluwi kwa lizi ling'hangala kwa mbuli ng'hulu zowaziwene;
Wazangulonga, “Yamtambichize Mndewa yokuya kwa itagwa lya Mkulu. Kikala goya kuchanya kilanga, na ukulu ng'hatu kwa Nguluwi!”
Aho Mfalisayo wamwe wala wali hala hali wanhu wamemile, nawamlonjela, “Mlangusa,” “Walonjele walanguswa wa hegwe wanyamalile!”
Yesu nakawalonjela, “Ndangukulonjelani wone awa wenyamalile, ago maganga gochemeleza lizi.”
Loyali habehi ng'hatu na kuwona muji wa Yelusalemu, Yesu nakaulilila,
yolonga, “Yaligoya hegwe nagwe lelo hano mbuli ilingigala makundo! Ila, lelo gavisigwa mmeho gako.
Mina zuwa lyanguya wakwihilwe wokuzungulusila lugagala, wokuzunguluta na kukibata kulawa nzingo zeng'ha.
Wokukopola hegwe na wanhu walingikala amo, howokulechela ne iganga likwima mli iganga liyage, kwa vila, hauzelele ula mhela Nguluwi hoyokuyila kukulohola.”
Yesu nakenjila mli Ng'handa ya Nguluwi, kaluka kuwawinga kunze wanhu walinguguza vinhu.
Nakawalonjela, “Yandichigwa, ‘Ng'handa ya heni yowa ng'handa ya kulandila.’ Ila hemwe muigalula mhalika ya wabokaji!”
Chila zuwa Yesu kazanguwalangusa ng'handa ya Nguluwi. Watambika wakulu na walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa na wakulu wa wanhu nawagana kumkopola,
Ila hewo hawaliwene lya kudita, mina wanhu weng'ha wali wekale tulu womhulichiza chila luzi.
Zuwa limwe, Yesu nayali yawalangusa wanhu honhu ha kusalila na kuwatagusila Mbuli Inojile, watambika wakulu na walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa na wakulu wamwe nawoya,
Walonga, “Tulonjele! Kwangudita mbuli azi kwa ludali lwachi, ama yalikohi yakupele ludali luno?”
Yesu nakawalonjela. “Na heni ndowauzani,
ludali lwa Yohani lwa kubatiza nalulawa kilanga kwa Nguluwi ama kwa wanhu?”
Ila hewo nawalonga ahi, “Wone tulonje nalulawa kilanga, kotuuza, ‘Lekachoni hamumkundile?’
Na wone tulonje nalulawa kwa wanhu, wanhu weng'ha wa hano wotutowa na maganga, mina weng'ha nawakunda kota Yohani nayali mloli wa Nguluwi.”
Nawamlonjela, “Hatuvizelele alo ludali nalulawa kohi.”
Yesu nakawalonjela, “Na heni siwalonjela ndangudita mbuli zino kwa ludali lwachi.”
Yesu kazangulangusa wanhu yolonga kwa nhelo ayi, “Munhu yumwe nakalima mgunda wa zabibu, nakawabasila walimi, heye nakaheluka isi ya kutali, kekala ako mihela minji.
Mhela wa kubeta, ayo munhu kemigala chitumagwa kwa wala walimile yakahole kumgunda gojilelile mizabibu. Ila wala walimile wamsubula ayo chitumagwa na kumhilusa ne chinhu.
Yula munhu nakamigala chitumagwa yunji, ila hewo kahila wamtowa ayo chitumagwa na kumbasa soni na kumhilusa ne chinhu.
Kahi kamigala wa kadatu, heye ayo lowamlumize, wamuwinga.
Yula yawele na mgunda nakejesa, ‘Ndodita choni? Ndomgala mwana wa heni ndimganile, yolonga heye womhulichiza.’
Wala walingulima lowawene, wazangilonjela, ‘Ayu ndo yohalila. Tumkopole leka kuhalila kwa heye kuwe kwa hetwe.’
Lelo Nawamlavya hafungo mwa mgunda wa mizabibu. Wamkopola.?” Yesu nakauza, “Yula yawele na mgunda kowadita ndaze wala walimi?”
“Kokuya kuwabagamiza awala walingulima, na kowapa walimi wanji awo mgunda wa zabibu.” Wanhu lowahuliche yolonga ahyo, nawalonga, “Hebu haiwa ahyo!”
Ila Yesu kawalola, nakawalonjela gano, “Maandiko Matakatifu gana mana yachi? “ ‘Iganga lilemigwe na walinguzenga, lelo liwa iganga likulu lya msisi!’
Wone munhu yogwa mchanya mwa iganga alyo, kobeneka pasapasa na wone iganga limgwile munhu yoneche, lyomhondanga.”
Walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa na watambika wakulu nawavizela, yaliyowalangusa kwa nhelo ayo yowalangusa hewo, wazangugana wambate bahala, ila nawadumba wanhu
Wazangupala mhela unojile. Wapala wanhu wazengidita wanoga, kumuuza. Aho wali wogana wambate na kumgala kuli ludali lwa chilongozi.
Wala wapugajizi nawamlonjela, “Mlangusa, tuvizela hegwe kwangulangusa na kulonga aku wokomya, tuvizela hambe umbagule munhu, kwangulangusa nzila za Nguluwi.
Lelo tulonjele iwa goya kumpa mndewa wa Loma kodi?”
Yesu nakavizela aho wangumjeza, nakawalonjela,
“Mndajile sendi ayo. Ndaze mutwi na itagwa ali ndo lya whaani?” “Mutwi wa Kaizali.” Nawedichila.
Yesu nakawalomjela, “Goya, mmigalile Kaizali gawele ga Kaizali na mmigalile Nguluwi gawele ga Nguluwi.”
Aho hali wanhu walemwela kumgwiliza, wekala tulu wochijesa vyoyawalonjele.
Wala Masadukayo, nawawele walonga kuduhu uzilipuko kwa wabagame, woya hali Yesu, wazangulonga.
“Mlangusa, Musa nakatwandichila, ‘Wone mng'holozo yumwe yaje ne kulela mwana, yogana munhu yumwe wa lukolo lwenu yamhalile ayo mdala, yamlelele wana mng'holoze.’
Lelo mhela umwe kwali na wanhu saba wa lukolo lumwe. Yula yalongole kamhola, hamba nakabagama ne kulela mwana.
Mng'holoze wa keli nakamhola yula mdala mlekwa, naye kahi nakabagama.
Na wakadatu hiho. Wazanguluta hiho mbaka weng'ha saba nawabagama haduhu yalechile mwana kuli yula mdala.
Logadumile, yula mdala na heye nakabagama.
Lelo zuwa lya wabagame kuzilipuka mdala ayo kowa mdala wa yalikohi? Weng'ha saba na wali wamhesile.”
Yesu nakawalonjela, “Walume na wadala wa mihela aji wanguhola na kuholeka,
Ila wala Nguluwi yowawika mbaka mhela wa kuzilipuka, howohesa ne kuhesigwa hebu.
Awo howobagama kahi, kwa vila, wowa kota wahilisi wa kilanga wa Nguluwi. Na ndo wana wa Nguluwi mina hewo walawa kuli wanhu wabagame.
Ila kuzilipuka kwa wabagame, Musa kahi nakakunda mbuli azo kuli gandichigwe gelile. Yolajila hala honhu hali chisosolo lochali chikwaka chiluli, kangumchema Mkulu kota Nguluwi wa Abulahamu na Nguluwi wa Isaka na Nguluwi wa Yakubu. Lelo heye hawele,
Nguluwi wa wanhu wabagame, ila Nguluwi wa wanhu wakomu, mina wala yawachemile kowali, wangikala na heye.”
Walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa nawalonga, “Mlangusa kwidichila goya ng'hatu.”
Mina huganile kumuuza kahi chinhu chinji.
Yesu nakauza, “Lekachoni wanhu walingulonga Kilistu Mlohozi ndo mwana wa Daudi?
Mina yuye Daudi kangulonga mlichitabu cha heye cha zabuli, “ ‘Mkulu, nakamlonjela Mkulu wa heni, kalise nzingo ya heni ya kudilo,
mbaka ndiwawiche wang'honyo wa hegwe, wawe chigoda cha kuwichila magulu ga hegwe.’
Daudi na kamchema ahyo heye, ‘Mkulu,’ Yowa ndaze lelo, Kilistu Mlohozi yawe mwana wa Daudi?”
Yesu nakawalonjela walanguswa hali wanhu weng'ha,
“Milolele na walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa hewo waganaaga kukola wavalile kanzu, wangana kulamsigwa na wanhu watanganiche kuli masoko. Na kikalisa kumwando mli ng'handa za kusalila na kuhola vigoda vya kumwando hali mnvina.
Wanguwabunza wadala walekwa na wangihada hewo wanoga kwa kulanda kwa sala zihejile. Zuwa Nguluwi loyowazapa wanhu, wotagusigwa kwa wihe lukami ng'hatu!”
Yesu nakalola kweng'ha, kawona wanhu wali na lufufu wojela ndolendole zowegale mli isanduku lya ndolendole kuli ng'handa ya Nguluwi,
kahi nakamona mamo yumwe mlekwa mzunwa yolavya mumo migwala mili midodo.
Nakalonga, “Ndangukulonjelani ndikomya, mamo ayu mlekwa nakalavya nyinji ng'hatu kusinda wanhu weng'ha.
Mina wanhu wawele na lufufu nawalavya ndolendole kulawa kuli lufufu nalowawele nawo. Ila ayu mamo kwa uzunwa wa heye, kalavya chila chinhu choyawele nacho.”
Walanguswa wamwe wali wolonga mbuli za Ng'handa ya Nguluwi, vyoizenjigwe na maganga ga sendi nyinji, na vinhu vyowalavile kwa Nguluwi. Yesu nakalonga,
“Aga geng'ha go mgona zuwa likuya haduhu iganga nelimwe lya ng'handa lisigala mchanya mwa iganga liyage, chila chinhu chowifigwa.”
Wanhu nawamuuza Yesu, “Mlangusa, mbuli azo zolawila nili? Choni chowa ulajilo wa mbuli azo zahabehi kulawila?”
Yesu nakawalonjela, “Milolele, mleche kubadigwa, mina wanhu wenji wokuya kwa kukolela itagwa lya heni wolonga, ‘Heni nda Kilistu Mlohozi yahaguligwe na Nguluwi, Mhela wa habehi. Ila hemwe mleche kuwawinza!’
Lelo lomhulika mbuli za ngondo na kugazigwa, mleche kutigasigwa, mina ago golongola kulawila, ila kuduma kwa geng'ha kung'hali.”
Yesu nakalutilila kulonga, “Isi imwe yochitowa na isi iyage, na undewa umwe wochitowa na undewa uyage.
Chila honhu howa na jimachinyina mikulu, kowa na nzala na matamwa ga kulecheza. Kowa na vinduzanduza vya kudumbigwa na ulajilo mkulu kilanga.
Ila logowa gang'hali kulawila ago geng'ha, wokubatani, wokugazani na kuwagalani mli ng'handa za kusalila na kuwawika mchinweng'ho. Mohilikwa kuli wandewa na vilongozi kwa chiwalo cha itagwa lya heni,
leka mlavye ulolezi kwa hewo.
Ila hemwe mleche kuwa na lunhwinhwi ndaze vyomchigombela.
Kwa vila nene ndokupani ulonzi wa kulonga na wanhu wakwihileni howoweza kiziganila na hemwe kahi howoibeza.
Molemigwa na wakulu wa hemwe na wang'holozenu na wanhu weng'ha womiganaga. Nawo wowakopola wamwe wa hemwe.
Wanhu weng'ha wokulemani kwa nongwa ya kumbinza heni.
Ila nemnvili imwe haikwajilila mmitwi ja hemwe.
Kwa kwimilila kwa hemwe, molohola ukomu wa hemwe.
“Lomuuwona muji wa Yelusalemu uzumgulutwe na wamizi, mvizele kuwifigwa kwake kwa habehi.
Aho wawele Yudeya wabilimile kuchidunda, wala wawele mli muji walawe na wala wawele kumgunda waleche kwinjila kuli muji awo.
Mazuwa ago ndo mazuwa ga kugazigwa, leka geng'ha gandikwe galawile.
Mane wawo wala wawele na himila na walingonyeza zuwa azo! Mina muli isi mowa na nongwa ng'hulu ng'hatu na ng'halazi ya Nguluwi yowoyela wanhu awa.
Wamwenga wakopoligwa kwa ipanga, wamwenga wochibatigwa woholigwa mli isi zeng'ha, na muji wa Yelusalemu wobijigwa na isi zinji, mbaka mhela houkuya.
“Kowa na vinhu vyokoneka kuli zuwa na nyelezi na nondwe. Wanhu weng'ha muisi wozangugaya kwa chiwalo cha kudumba mtigasiko wa nigu za bahali.
Wanhu wozilika kwa kudumba, wololela mbuli ziza ngulawila muisi, mina mong'ho ubatilile vinhu avyo vyeng'ha wotigaswa,
Hamba womona Mwana wa Munhu yokuya kuli ng'hungugu. Yali na ludali na ukulu lwinji.
Mhela mbuli azo lozikwaluka kulawila, mwinuche na kwinula mitwi jenu mchanya, mina kugomboligwa kwa hemwe kwa habehi.”
Hamba nakawalangusa yolonga kwa nhelo, “Mlole ikuyu na migodi jinji jeng'ha.
Wone mone galuka kuzuka mahamba, mvizela mhela wa nhonya wa habehi.
Namwe hihyo, homkona mbuli azo zilawila, mvizele Undewa wa Nguluwi wa habehi.
“Ndanguwalonjelani ndikomya, lulelo alu halubagama gang'hali ago geng'ha kulawila.
Ulanga na isi zopuluta, ila ulonzi wa heni haupuluta hebu.
“Muwe meho nhumbula za hemwe zileche kuganilila kuli vinhu vinji vya ukomu awu, kudita kuli mbuli zihile na mijito ja amu muisi. Zuwa alyo lyokuyilani ne kuvizela.
Mina chokuyilani kota chinhu chitejigwe, wanhu weng'ha wali ngikala muli isi.
Milolele, mze ngulanda leka muwe na ludali lwa kukola mli mbuli azo zeng'ha zilawila, na kwima kumwando kuli Mwana wa Munhu.”
Zuwa alyo, nemisi, Yesu nayali yowalangusa wanhu Mng'handa ya Nguluwi ila hamihe nakalutaga kuli chidunda cha Mizeituni na kikala ako.
Wanhu weng'ha nawalutaga hali Ng'handa ya Nguluwi kung'hali lufuku. Wazengumhulichiza.
Mnvina ya mibumunda hajisasile, ilinguchemigwa Pasaka, nayali habehi.
Watambika wakulu na walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa wazangupala nzila ya kumkopola Yesu, ila nawawadumba wanhu.
Na baho Limazoga limwinjila Yudasi yalinguchemigwa Isikalioti, yumwe wa wala walanguswa kumi na weli.
Ahyo nakaluta kwa wakulu wa watambika na walolezi wa ng'handa ya Nguluwi, nakalonga nawo vila vyoyomuhinduchila Yesu.
Na hewo wasechelela nawalagana kumha sendi.
Yudasi nakakunda na kazangupala mhumhu ya kumhinduchila Yesu ne wanhu kuvizela.
Zuwa lya mnvina ya mibumunda hajisasile wali habehi. Ahyo ndo vyoili mwanaing'holo kolavigwa nhambiko ya Pasaka.
Yesu nakawalajiza Petili na Yohani kawalonjela, “Mlute mkatugongomanyile mnvina ya Pasaka tulye.”
Hewo nawamuuza, “Kohi kotuluta kugongomanyila ndiya?”
Nakawedichila, “Mhulichize! Lomuwa mluta mjini, moting'hana na mlume yawele yedwichile chiya cha mazi. Mumuwinze mbaka ng'handa yoyokwinjila.
Na mumlonjele yawele na ng'handa, ‘Mlangusa kanguuza, chilikohi chihengo cha wajenzi choyodila Pasaka hamwe na walanguswa?’
Na heye kokulajilani chihengo chikulu cha mchanya mina chiwichigwe goya, mgongomanyile mumo.”
Nawaluta wona hihila kota Yesu vyoyawalonjele. Na hewo nawawika goya ndiya ya Pasaka.
Mhela loufichile, Yesu kawahola watumigwa wa heye na kikala na hewo mchisanya.
Nakawalonjela, “Ndangugana kulya hamwe na hemwe mnvina ayi ya pasaka nding'hali kugazigwa!
Kwa vila ndangukulonjelani, silya kahi mbaka kuli Undewa wa Nguluwi.”
Hamba kahola chizombe cha divai, katambichiza, kalonga, “Mbochele chino munwe mweng'ha.
Ndangukulonjelani kulawa sambi sinwa divai kahi mbaka undewa wa Nguluwi houkuya.”
Hamba kahola ibumunda, katambichiza na kamogola, kawapa walanguswa wa heye yolonga, “Alu ndo lukuli lwa heni, loulavigwa kwa mbuli ya hemwe. Mdite hino lomng'humbuka heni.”
Kahi hiho na chizombe, loyadile kalonga, “Chizombe chino cha ilagano lya sambi lilingulajila kwa danda ya heni yoibohoka kwa mbuli ya hemwe.
“Ila loleni! Munhu yula yongalamka kabahano kangulya hamwe na heni!.
Mwana wa Munhu kanguluta kukopoligwa kota voyaganile Nguluwi, ila mane munhu yula yamuhinduche.”
Aho wazangiuza wawo yeng'ha yalikohi yodita mbuli ayo.
Nakulawila kitwanza hali walanguswa yalikohi yozanguwa mkulu ng'hatu hali hewo weng'ha.
Yesu nakawalonjela, “Vilongozi wa isi walongozaga wanhu kwa lupichi na hewo wochichema ‘Watanza wanhu.’
Ila hemwe ileche kuwa ahyo, nayali mkulu hali hemwe imgana yawe mdodo kusinda weng'ha, na yawele mkulu imagana yawe kota chitumagwa.
Kwa vila yalikohi nayali mkulu? Yula yalingikalisa mchisanya na kulya, ama yula nayali chitumagwa? Hebu! Yowa yula yalingikala mcchisanya na kulya ndiya! Ahyo, heni nda hano hagati ha hemwe kota mkolamijito.
“Hemwe ndo mponile na heni, mhela weng'ha wa kujezigwa kwa heni.
Kota mhaza wa heni voyangalile heni undewa wuwula. Na heni nani, ndangukupani hemwe undewa.
Molya na kunwa mchisanya ya heni kuli undewa wa heni na kikalisa mvigoda vya undewa na kutagusa nhanzi kumi na mbili za Isilaeli.
“Simoni, Simoni! Hulichize! Limazoga lyangugana kuwabetani hemwe kota munhu yobeta uhemba.
Ila heni ndokulandila kwa Nguluwi leka makundo ga hegwe galeche kuwa mado. Wone uhiluche kuli heni wasindamize nhumbula wang'holozo.”
Petili nakalonga, “Mkulu, heni ng'hunda kuluta na hegwe mchinweng'ho na kuli kubagama.”
Yesu nakamlonjela, “Ndangukulonjela Petili, lehano izogolo ling'hali kwika, kombela kadatu kota hunzelele heni.”
Hamba Yesu kawauza walanguswa wa heye. “Hala ndiwalajize mli hela sendi ne mhako ne makwamba, namwisilwa chinhu?” Nawamwidichila, “Hatwisilwe ne chinhu hebu!”
Yesu nakawalonjela, “Ila sambi yoneche yula yalihela mhako wa sendi yahole. Na nayali na mhako yadite hiho! Na nayali hela ipanga, yaguze ikoti lyake yagule umwe.
Kwa vila Maandiko Matakatifu galonga, ‘Na heye kohanzwa hamwe na wehile,’ Ndanguwalonjelani, geng'ha gandichigwe mbuli ya heni, ganguza kuduma.”
Walanguswa nawalonga, “Mkulu ulole hano hana mipanga mili.” Nakawalonjela, “Ikwila!”
Yesu koka na kuluta kuli chidunda cha Mizeituni kota vyoyazowele, walanguswa wa heye na hewo wamuwinza.
Loyafichile ako nakawalonjela, “Mlande leka mleche kwinjila kuli kujezigwa.”
Na baho kawaleka, kaluta honhu hatali hado ha munhu kutoza iganga, kafugama, kalanda.
“Mhaza wone ulingugana, umbusile chino chizombe cha kugazigwa kwa heni, ila haiwele vyondigana heni, leka kota vyoulingugana hegwe gakoleke.”
Aho mhilisi kulawa kilanga kalawila kaza kumtanza.
Yawele mli usungu ukulu, kakobanya kulanda ng'hatu, na chituguti chiwele kota danda, kizangulagala hasi.
Loyasindile kulanda, kawahiluchila walanguswa wa heye, nakawafika wawasile, kwa vila nawali na masinzo lukami.
Nakawalonjela, “Lekachoni muwasile? Mwinuche mlande mleche kwinjila kuli kujezigwa.”
Yesu loyali yolutilila kulonga, lung'hongola lwa wanhu, welongoze na yula nayachemagwe Yudasi, yumwe wa wala kumi na weli. Yudasi kumlamsa Yesu kwa kumnonela.
Ila Yesu nakamlonjela, “Yudasi! Kwangumlavya Mwana wa Munhu kwa kumnonela?”
Walanguswa nawekale hamwe na Yesu, lowawene mbuli zila zilawile, nawauza, “Mkulu tuwahenje na mipanga?”
Na myao yumwe kamtowa kwa ipanga chitumagwa yumwe wa mtambika mkulu, nakamdumula ikutu lya kudilo.
Baho Yesu nakalonga. “Leka ayi ikwila!” Kalidoliza lila ikutu na kumlohola.
Hamba Yesu nakawalonjela watambika wakulu na walolezi wa ng'handa ya Nguluwi woyile kumibata. “Muya na mipanga na nyimbati kundibata kota heni nda mbokaji?
Londali hamwe na hemwe chila zuwa na ndikala hamwe na hemwe mli ng'handa ya Nguluwi, hambichile hali ludali lwa hemwe hebu. Ila saa ino ya hemwe, na undewa wa kutitu.”
Wambata Yesu na kumhola, waluta naye kuli ng'handa ya mtambika mkulu. Petili kazangumuwinza kumbele nayali kutali.
Nawawesa chenje hagati hali luga, wekalisa hamwe, Petili na kekalisa hamwe na hewo.
Chitumagwa yumwe mdala loyamuwene Petili yekalise behi na chenje, kazangumlola na kalonga, “Munhu ayu nayali hamwe na Yesu.”
Ila Petili nakabela mbuli ila yolonga, “Mdala hegwe, simzelele yuno youmlonga!”
Hamba munhu yunji nakamona Petili, kalonga, “Na hegwe nagwe kwa yumwe wa hewo!” Ila Petili kedichila kalonga, “Mkulu, hebu! Siwele heni!”.
Baho saa imwe hamwande, munhu yumwe kakangaza yolonga, “Ndangukomya, munhu yuno nayali hamwe na Yesu kwa vila heye naye nakalawa Galilaya.!”
Ila Petili kedichila, “Munhu hegwe, sivizelele ne choulingulonga!” Na baho loyali yang'hali yolonga, izogolo nalika.
Mkulu kahinduka kamlola Petili. Petili nakakumbuchila gala gonayamlonjele Yesu. “Lehano izogolo halina kwika kombela mala zidatu kota hunzelele.”
Petili kalawa kunze, nakalila lukami.
Wala wanhu wali womlolela Yesu wazangumtowa na kumbeza.
Wamuwoha chibende kumeho, wazangumuuza, “Tulagulile lelo, yalikohi yakutowile?”
Wazangumlonjela mbuli nyinji za kumliga Yesu.
Loifichile mitondo, balaza lya wasekulu, watambika wakulu na walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa nawating'hana hamwe mchitala na kumchema Yesu.
Nawalonga, “Tulonjele! Hegwe kwa Kilistu Mlohozi yahaguligwe na Nguluwi?” Yesu nakawedichila, “Wone ndikulonjeleni hamkunda,
na wone ndikuuzeni, hamkwidichila hebu.
Ila kulawa sambi na kulutilila, Mwana wa Munhu kowa yekalise kudilo kwa Nguluwi nayali na mong'ho weng'ha.”
Weng'ha nawamuuza, “Hambi hegwe kwa Mwana wa Nguluwi?” Na heye kawedichila, “Hemwe mwangulonga heni nda mwana wa Nguluwi.”
Wazangulonga, “Hambi topala chinhu chachi kahi? Hetwe baha tuhulika yolonga kwa mlomo wa heye du!”
Hamba, wanhu weng'ha wenuka, wamigala Yesu kwa Pilato.
Waluka kumlonjeleza wolonga, “Tumfika munhu ayu yowahada wanhu wa hetwe, yowalemeza kulavya kodi kwa mndewa wa Loma na kichema heye Kilistu Mlohozi yahaguligwe na Nguluwi.”
Pilato nakamuuza, “Hegwe kwa mndewa wa wayahudi?” Yesu kedichila nakamlonjela, “Hegwe kulonga.”
Pilato nakawalonjela watambika wakulu na wala wanhu wamemile, “Sichiwene chinhu cha kumtagusa munhu yuno.”
Ila Hewo wang'ang'anila walonga, “Nakanguwasonjeleza wanhu vibi wetowe na undewa wa Loma kwa ulanguso wa udesi muli isi yeng'ha ya Yudeya, kaluchila Galilaya na sambi ka hano.”
Pilato loyahuliche ago, nakawauza, “Munhu ayu mwenyeng'haye wa Galilaya?”
Loyavizelele Yesu nayali hasi ha ulongozi wa mndewa Helodi, kamgala kwa Helodi, mhela awo nayali Yelusalemu.
Helodi loyamuwene Yesu kazangusechelela ng'hatu. Kwa vila nakagana kumona kulawa mazuwa menji. Nakahulika mbuli za heye, na kagana yamone yodita vinduzanduza.
Lelo kamuuza Yesu mbuli nyinji kwa mhela uhejile, ila Yesu hedichile ne chinhu.
Watambika wakulu na walangusa wa malajizo ga Musa, wema wamlonjeleza Yesu kwa lupichi.
Helodi hamwe na wala walingulolela wazangumbasa soni Yesu na kumbeza, wolawa wamvalisa nguwo ya chiundewa, wamhilula kwa Pilato.
Helodi na Pilato, wala aho katali wali wehilwe, kulawa zuwa lilila wazangigana.
Pilato nakawachema watambika wakulu na vilongozi na wanhu.
Baho nakawalonjela, “Mmigala munhu ayu kwa heni, mlonga kota nayali yowahada wanhu. Lelo mhulichize! Na heni ndizipugajiza mbuli za heye, ila sonile ne chinhu choyawifile kuli mbuli azo zomumlonjeleze.
Si nene yeng'ha, na heye Helodi hachiwene ne chinhu choyawifile munhu ayu chilingumgana yakomigwe.
Ahyo ndangugana yazapigwe ng'hobwa hamba ndomlechela.”
Kwa vila kaganigwa yamlechele munhu yumwe kwa wala wawele mchinweng'ho kuli mnvina ya Pasaka.
Ila lung'hongola lweng'ha lwa wanhu wachemeleza hamwe, “Mkopoleni munhu ayo na utuchumulile Balaba!”
Balaba nayali yahindilwe kwa kwambuza wanhu kuhinduka kuli muji na kukopola.
Pilato nakagana kumlechela Yesu, yolawa kalongana nawo kahi,
ila hewo wachemeleza, “Muwambeni mumsalaba, muwambeni mumsalaba.”
Pilato nakawalonjela lwa kadatu, “Kadita choni chihile? Hambe ndichone chinhu chimwambuza yabagame, ndolajiza yasubuligwe ng'hobwa, hamba ndomlechela.”
Ila hewo waza nguchemeleza lukami ng'hatu twangugana Yesu yawambigwe mumsalaba, hamba lizi lyawo lihulikwa hamba wakundizwa chowaganile.
Pilato nakalonga iditigwe kota vyowalingugana.
Kachumula kamlavya yula walingumgana, yula yawohigwe kwa kwambuza kuhinduka na kukopola wanhu, yolawa kamlavya Yesu wamditile vowogana.
Lowali womgala wating'hana na munhu yumwe nayali nguchemigwa Simoni mwenyeng'haye wa Kilene, nayali yolawa kumgunda. Wamibata wamdwika ula msalaba yauhole kumbele kwa Yesu.
Lung'hongola lwa wanhu lwali lumuwinza, wali mumo wadala womlilila na kumuwembela.
Yesu kagalamka nakawalonjela, “Hemwe wadala wa Yelusalemu! Mleche kundilila heni, ila mililile mwemwe na wana wa hemwe!
Kwa vila mazuwa ganguya mozangulonga, ‘Wabweda wala wali mhende, hewo hawalelile na hambe wonyeze wana!’
Baho wanhu wokwaluka kuvilonjela vidunda, ‘Tugwile!’ Na vidunda, ‘Tugubicheni!’
Kwa vila wanhu wangudita vinhu avi kuli igodi idodi, ahyo yowa ndaze kwa igodi likalile?”
Wanhu wanji weli wehile na wegaligwa bahala, wakopoligwe hamwe na Yesu.
Lowafichile honhu hamwe hali nguchemigwa, “Izeje lya mutwi,” Baho wamuwamba Yesu mumsalaba hamwe na wala wabokaji, yumwe kudilo na yumwe kumoso.
Yesu nakalonga, “Mhaza uwalechele kwa vila hawavizelele hebu chowalingudita.” Wahola nguwo zonayavalaga kwa kuzitowela simbi.
Wanhu wema wazanguwalola. Wakulu wa Wayahudi wazangubeza wolonga, “Kawalohola wanhu wanji, lelo yelohole yuye wone heye yawele Kilistu Mlohozi yahaguligwe na Nguluwi!”
Wamizi nawo wazangumbeza, waluta wampa divai izazame.
Wolonga, “Wilohole uliyeka wone hegwe ndo uli Mndewa wa Wayahudi.”
Mchanya ha msalaba wa heye, na wandika mbuli ino, “Yuno ndo Mndewa wa Wayahudi.”
Yumwe wa wala wabokaji wawambigwe hamwe na Yesu nakamliga Yesu kalonga, “Hambi hegwe hauwele Kilistu Mlohzi!? Wilohole gwegwe na hetwe.”
Ila yula mbokaji yumwe, kamdeuza miyage, yolonga, “Hegwe hambe umdumbe Nguluwi hebu? Hegwe nagwe kwa mumo kuli kutagusigwa kwa wihe hihyo.
Hetwe, twangutagusigwa hano kwa mbuli zihile zotuditile. Ila ayu munhu haditile ne chinhu chihile.”
Hamba nakamlonjela Yesu, “Yesu! Ung'humbuche loukwinjila Undewa wa hegwe.”
Yesu nakamlonjela, “Ndangukulonjela ndikomya lelo hano kowa hamwe na heni kuli lubehelo kuchanya kwa Nguluwi.”
Yali iwele saa sita nemisi; jiza ligubika isi yeng'ha mbaka saa tisa
na ipaziya lya honhu helile ng'hatu kuli ng'handa ya Nguluwi lidejeka vibende vili.
Yesu nakalila kwa kuchemelela, “Mhaza mmoko wa hegwe ndanguwika muhe wa heni.” Na loyalonjile hino, nakatwesemka lwa mwiso.
Mkulu wa wamizi wa Loma, loyawene gogalawile, kamtogola Nguluwi yolonga, “Kakomya, ayu nayali munhu yanojile.”
Na wanhu weng'ha wali aho wamemile wololela mbuli ayo, vyowawene ago galawile wahiluka kuluga wotowa vipambaga kwa kulajila masinzo.
Wala wanhu weng'ha wamzelele Yesu na wala wadala wamuwinzile Galilaya, wema kutali wolola vinhu avyo.
Kwali na munhu yumwe itagwa lya heye Yusufu, Mwenyeng'haye wa chijiji chimwe cha Wayahudi chilinguchemigwa Alimataya. Nayali munhu yanojile yodita galinguganigwa na Nguluwi.
Nakekala yobeteza kuya kwa Undewa wa Nguluwi, ila heye nayali munhu wa Alimataya muji umwenga wa Wayahudi, yumwe wa wakulu wa kutagusa, hakundile chila chowadile wayage.
Heye kaluta kwa Pilato, kalanda yapegwe lukuli lwa Yesu.
Kaludulisa hasi, kaugubichiza sanda inojile ng'hatu, kauwika mchilaga chihongoligwe mmitalawe na hachinawichigwa ne lukuli mgati.
Zuwa alyo lyali Ijumaa, lya kiwika goya Zuwa lya Kwesela gali gokwaluka.
Wala wadala nawelongoze hamwe na Yesu kulawa Galilaya nawamuwinza Yusufu, wahona hala honhu hali chilaga na wawona lukuli lwa Yesu houwichigwe.
Na baho wahiluka kuluga, waza hola mafuta ga kunhunyhilila na Malihamu ga kulukumbika lukuli lwa Yesu. Kuli Zuwa lya Kwesela, nawesela kota Malajizo ga Musa vyogalingugana.
Jumapili kung'hali lufuku ng'hatu, wadala wahola mafuta ga kunhunyhilila gowawichile na waluta kuli chilaga.
Walifika lila iganga lowadinyile chilaga, lihejele kutali na lwizi lwa chilaga.
Wenjile mgati mchilaga hawauwene lukuli lwa Mkulu Yesu.
Wang'hali wabubuwale na mbuli ayo, bahala wanhu weli wavalile nguwo nzelu chweya! Wema behi na howali.
Wadala wazangudumba ng'hatu na wenamiza hanyi. Ila wala wanhu wawalonjela, “Lekachoni mwangumpala nayali mkomu kuli wanhu wabagame?
Yesu haduhu hano, nakazilipuka. Mkumbuchile vyonayakulonjeleni loyali kula Galilaya,
‘Mwana wa Munhu kolavigwa kulimhoko ga wanhu wehile, hewo womgaza na kumuwamba mumsalaba, ila zuwa lya kadatu kozilipuka.’ ”
Baho wala wadala wakumbuchila mbuli ila yoyawalonjele.
Lowahiluche kulawa kuchilaga, wawalonjela mbuli yila wala walanguswa kumi na yumwe na wanhu weng'ha.
Walonjile mbuli azo kwa watumigwa wali, Maliya Madelena na Yohana na Maliya mayake Yakubu na wadala wanji wawele hamwe kuli chilaga.
Watumigwe na wona mbuli azo kota hazitanganiche, nahawakundile.
Ila Petili kalawa hala na kubilima mbaka kuli chilaga. Loyafichile, kenamiza na kusunjilila mgati, baho kayona ila sanda. Kahiluka kaye aku yabubuwale kwa gala galawile.
Kuli zuwa lilila, wanhu weli walwele walanguswa wa Yesu wali woluta kuli chijiji chilinguchemigwa Emau, utali wa chilomita kumi na imwe kulawa Yelusalemu.
Wazangulonga mbuli zila za vinhu vyeng'ha lozilawile.
Lowaliwolonga na kiuza, heye Yesu nakalawila, kaza kilongoza na hewo.
Wazakumona na meho ila hawali womzela kota ndo Yesu.
Yesu nakawauza, “Mbuli zachi zino zomlonga kuno mjenda?” Wema tulu, wakwisuche kumeho kuno wesinzile.
Yumwe yalinguchemigwa Kiliopasi, nakamlonjela, “Hegwe kwa mjenzi hano Yelusalemu, hugazelele galawile ako mazuwa gano?”
Yesu nakawauza, “Mbuli zachi?” Na hewo nawamwidichila, “Mbuli zimlawile Yesu wa Nasaleti, heye nayali mloli wa Nguluwi, yadahile kulangusa mbuli zeng'ha hali Nguluwi na hali wanhu weng'ha.
Watambika wakulu na wakulu wa hetwe wamigala kwa wakulu wa Loma yatagusigwe kwa wihe kubagama, na hewo wamuwamba mumsalaba.
Hetwe natukunda kota heye ndo yawagombole Waisilaeli. Lelo kwa ago geng'ha lehano zuwa lya kadatu kulawa lovilawile vinhu avyo.
Vivila wadala wamwenga kulawa mchilundo cha hetwe watinuswa ng'hatu. Mitondo kung'hali lufuku nawaluta kuli chilaga.
Ila hawaluwene lutufi lwake. Wahiluka walonga walawilwa na wahilisi wa kilanga walonjelwa ka mkomu.
Wanhu wamwenga kulawa mchilundo cha hetwe, waluta kuli chilaga, na hewo wona kota wadala wala vyowalonjile, ila heye hawamuwene.”
Na baho Yesu nakawalonjela, “Lekachoni mli wapoka ahi na nhumbula za hemwe hambe zikunde geng'ha galonjigwe na waloli wa Nguluwi?
Haimganile Kilistu Mlohozi yahaguligwe na Nguluwi kugazigwa, na hamba yenjile mli ukulu wa heye?”
Na Yesu kawagubulila mbuli zeng'ha zilingumgana heye kuli Maandiko Matakatifu, kwaluchila chitabu cha Musa mbaka gandichigwe na waloli wa Nguluwi weng'ha.
Lowali behi na chijiji chowaliwoluta, Yesu kedita kota kangulutilila na majendo kumwando.
Ila hewo wamlanda wolonga, “Wikale hamwe na hetwe kwa vila zuwa liswa, chilo changwinjila.” Baho kenjila wekala hamwe.
Loyali yekalise hamwe na hewo kulya ndiya, kahola ibumunda, katambichiza kamogola kawapa.
Bahala meho gawo gagubuligwa na wamzela ndo Yesu, ila heye na kajilila hawamuwene kahi.
Wazangulonga hewo kwa hewo, “Nhumbula za hetwe ha zali zimweka mgati mwa hetwe loyali yolonga na hetwe mnzila na kutudamlila goya Maandiko Matakatifu?”
Bahala hihila woka, wahiluka Yelusalemu, kula wawafika wala watumigwa kumi na yumwe, wehanzile na wanhu wanji.
Walonga ng'hatu, “Mkulu kazilipuka kamlawila Simoni.”
Wala watumigwa weli nawawalonjela wayao mbuli zeng'ha zowalawile mnzila, na vyowamzelele Mkulu kwa kumogola ibumunda.
Bahala lowali wochilonjela ago. Yesu kema hagati howali, nakawalonjela, “Mikale goya.”
Watinuka na wazangudumba na wejesa kota wangulyona ilaika
Na heye kawalonjela, “Lekachoni mwangisinza? Na mmemile majesa Mnhumbula za hemwe?
Ila Mlole moko na magulu ga heni nda yuye. Mbateni mndole, mina ilaika lyahela lukuli na mizeje kota vyommbona.”
Na loyasindile kulonga ago, kawalajila moko na magulu.
Lowali wekale wabubuwale aku hambe wakunde kwa kusangalala, nakawauza, “Hano mwanacho chinhu cheng'ha chila cha kulya?”
Wampa somba ibanichigwe.
Yesu kahola na kalya weng'ha womona.
Hamba nakawalonjela, “Ahino ndokota vonandikulonjeleni londali hamwe na hemwe. Goye geng'ha ga heni, mizilo ja Musa na gandichigwe kuli vitabu vya waloli na zabuli.”
Na baho Yesu kawagubulila luhala yogana wavizele Maandiko Matakatifu
Nakawalonjela, “Yandichigwa hino, Kilistu Mlohozi kogazigwa na zuwa lya kadatu kozilipuka.
Na baho iganigwa kwa itagwa lya heye isi zeng'ha kulawa Yelusalemu zidamuligwe mbuli zinojile kota wanhu wanguganigwa kumgalamchila Nguluwi na Nguluwi kowosela gehile ga hewo.
Na hemwe mokwimilila mbuli azo, na azo ziganigwa mkazilavile ulolezi.
Na Heni baha ndowegalila yula Mhaza nayalagane na hetwe komlajiza, ila mbeteze mbaka homchigalilwa mong'ho kulawa kilanga.”
Yolawa kawalongoza hafungo ha muji mbaka Betaniya, na heye kenula mhoko gake kuchanya na kawatambichiza.
Loyawawichile moko na kuatambichiza, kawaleka, kaholigwa kuluta kilanga.
Na hewo wamfugamila wahiluka Yelusalemu, wawele wasangalale ng'hatu,
Wekala kuli luga lwa ng'handa ya Nguluwi womtogola Nguluwi, mhela weng'ha.
